Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The user requested implementation of the Avant Compendium Pipeline Roadmap, specifically proceeding through Phase D (Link Rewriting) and Phase E (Round-trip Validation). The primary goal was to create a robust JSON-to-LevelDB compendium pack workflow where JSON files serve as the single source of truth, with proper UUID cross-referencing and round-trip validation for CI consistency checks.

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - JSON-First Compendium Architecture with permanent 16-character `_id` fields
   - FoundryVTT compendium pack generation (.db format)
   - Link rewriting from plain trait references to UUID format (`@UUID[Compendium.avant.avant-traits.{id}]{Label}`)
   - Round-trip validation for CI pipeline consistency
   - Deterministic build processes with hash consistency verification
   - TypeScript CLI tools with comprehensive error handling
   - GitHub Actions CI/CD integration for automated validation
   - CompendiumLoader class with enhanced validation and fallback systems
   - Phase-based pipeline implementation (A through E)

3. Files and Code Sections:
   - **scripts/compendium/link-rewriter.ts**
     - Created comprehensive link rewriting engine for Phase D implementation
     - Converts trait references from plain text to UUID format
     - Key function for trait processing:
     ```typescript
     private processTraitReferences(item: CompendiumDocument, result: LinkRewriteResult, fileName: string): void {
       if (item.system?.traits && Array.isArray(item.system.traits)) {
         for (let i = 0; i < item.system.traits.length; i++) {
           const traitName = item.system.traits[i];
           
           if (typeof traitName === 'string' && !traitName.startsWith('@UUID')) {
             const traitId = this.findItemIdByName('traits', traitName);
             
             if (traitId) {
               const uuidReference = `@UUID[Compendium.avant.avant-traits.${traitId}]{${traitName}}`;
               item.system.traits[i] = uuidReference;
             }
           }
         }
       }
     }
     ```

   - **scripts/compendium/round-trip-extractor.ts**
     - Created comprehensive round-trip validation system for Phase E
     - Extracts data from built compendium packs and validates consistency
     - Key validation function:
     ```typescript
     private async validatePackRoundTrip(packName: string, sourceDir: string, options: ExtractionOptions): Promise<RoundTripResult> {
       // Load source data
       const sourceData = await this.loadSourceData(sourceDir);
       
       // Extract built data
       const extractedResult = await this.extractPack(packName, options);
       
       // Compare counts, IDs, and structure
       result.consistency.itemCount = sourceData.items.length === extractedResult.items.length;
       result.consistency.folderCount = sourceData.folders.length === extractedResult.folders.length;
       
       return result;
     }
     ```

   - **package.json**
     - Added new CLI commands for Phase D and E:

     "compendium:rewrite": "tsx scripts/compendium/link-rewriter.ts rewrite",
     "compendium:rewrite-dry": "tsx scripts/compendium/link-rewriter.ts rewrite --dry-run",
     "compendium:links": "tsx scripts/compendium/link-rewriter.ts validate",
     "compendium:extract": "tsx scripts/compendium/round-trip-extractor.ts extract",

     ```

     const roundTripExtractor = new RoundTripExtractor();

     if (!roundTripValidation) {
       console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è  Round-trip validation failed - some inconsistencies detected');

    67‚Üí    console.log(`üìÅ Packs directory: ${this.packsDirectory}`);
    68‚Üí    
    69‚Üí    if (!fs.existsSync(this.packsDirectory)) {
    70‚Üí      console.error(`‚ùå Packs directory not found: ${this.packsDirectory}`);

    72‚Üí    }

    75‚Üí    this.validationResults.clear();

    81‚Üí    const packDirs = fs.readdirSync(this.packsDirectory, { withFileTypes: true })
    82‚Üí      .filter(dirent => dirent.isDirectory())
    83‚Üí      .map(dirent => dirent.name);
    84‚Üí
    85‚Üí    console.log(`üì¶ Found pack types: ${packDirs.join(', ')}`);
    86‚Üí
    87‚Üí    let allValid = true;
    88‚Üí
    89‚Üí    // Validate each pack
    90‚Üí    for (const packDir of packDirs) {
    91‚Üí      const packPath = path.join(this.packsDirectory, packDir);
    92‚Üí      const packValid = await this.validatePack(packDir, packPath, options);
    93‚Üí      
    94‚Üí      if (!packValid) {
    95‚Üí        allValid = false;
    96‚Üí      }
    97‚Üí    }

    99‚Üí    // Check for duplicate IDs across all packs
   100‚Üí    this.checkDuplicateIds();
   101‚Üí
   102‚Üí    // Print summary
   103‚Üí    this.printValidationSummary(options);
   104‚Üí
   105‚Üí    const duplicateCount = Array.from(this.duplicateIds.entries())
   106‚Üí      .filter(([_, files]) => files.length > 1).length;
   107‚Üí
   108‚Üí    return allValid && duplicateCount === 0;
   109‚Üí  }

   111‚Üí  /**

   114‚Üí  private async validatePack(packName: string, packPath: string, options: ValidationOptions): Promise<boolean> {
   115‚Üí    console.log(`\nüìã Validating pack: ${packName}`);
   116‚Üí    
   117‚Üí    // Get all JSON files
   118‚Üí    const jsonFiles = fs.readdirSync(packPath)
   119‚Üí      .filter(file => file.endsWith('.json') && !file.startsWith('_'))
   120‚Üí      .sort();
   121‚Üí
   122‚Üí    if (jsonFiles.length === 0) {
   123‚Üí      console.log(`  ‚ö†Ô∏è  No JSON files found in ${packName}`);
   124‚Üí      return true;
   125‚Üí    }
   126‚Üí
   127‚Üí    console.log(`  üìÑ Found ${jsonFiles.length} JSON files`);
   128‚Üí
   129‚Üí    let packValid = true;
   130‚Üí    const packResult: ValidationResult = {
   131‚Üí      valid: true,
   132‚Üí      errors: [],
   133‚Üí      warnings: [],
   134‚Üí      fixed: false
   135‚Üí    };
   136‚Üí
   137‚Üí    // Validate each file
   138‚Üí    for (const jsonFile of jsonFiles) {
   139‚Üí      const filePath = path.join(packPath, jsonFile);
   140‚Üí      const fileResult = await this.validateFile(filePath, packName, options);
   141‚Üí      
   142‚Üí      this.totalDocuments++;
   143‚Üí      
   144‚Üí      if (!fileResult.valid) {
   145‚Üí        packValid = false;
   146‚Üí        packResult.valid = false;
   147‚Üí      }
   148‚Üí
   149‚Üí      if (fileResult.fixed) {
   150‚Üí        this.totalFixed++;
   151‚Üí        packResult.fixed = true;
   152‚Üí      }
   153‚Üí
   154‚Üí      packResult.errors.push(...fileResult.errors);
   155‚Üí      packResult.warnings.push(...fileResult.warnings);
   156‚Üí
   157‚Üí      // Log file result
   158‚Üí      if (options.verbose || !fileResult.valid) {
   159‚Üí        const status = fileResult.valid ? '‚úÖ' : '‚ùå';
   160‚Üí        const fixedText = fileResult.fixed ? ' (fixed)' : '';
   161‚Üí        console.log(`    ${status} ${jsonFile}${fixedText}`);
   162‚Üí        
   163‚Üí        if (fileResult.errors.length > 0) {
   164‚Üí          fileResult.errors.forEach(error => console.log(`      ‚ùå ${error}`));
   165‚Üí        }
   166‚Üí        if (fileResult.warnings.length > 0) {
   167‚Üí          fileResult.warnings.forEach(warning => console.log(`      ‚ö†Ô∏è  ${warning}`));
   168‚Üí        }
   169‚Üí      }
   170‚Üí    }
   171‚Üí
   172‚Üí    this.validationResults.set(packName, packResult);
   173‚Üí    
   174‚Üí    console.log(`  üìä ${packName}: ${jsonFiles.length} files, ${packResult.errors.length} errors, ${packResult.warnings.length} warnings`);
   175‚Üí    
   176‚Üí    return packValid;
   177‚Üí  }
   178‚Üí
   179‚Üí  /**
   180‚Üí   * Validate a single JSON file
   181‚Üí   */
   182‚Üí  private async validateFile(filePath: string, packName: string, options: ValidationOptions): Promise<ValidationResult> {
   183‚Üí    const fileName = path.basename(filePath);
   184‚Üí    const result: ValidationResult = {
   185‚Üí      valid: true,
   186‚Üí      errors: [],
   187‚Üí      warnings: [],
   188‚Üí      fixed: false
   189‚Üí    };
   190‚Üí
   191‚Üí    try {
   192‚Üí      // Read and parse JSON
   193‚Üí      const fileContent = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
   194‚Üí      const document: CompendiumDocument = JSON.parse(fileContent);
   195‚Üí
   196‚Üí      let modified = false;
   197‚Üí
   198‚Üí      // Validate _id field
   199‚Üí      if (!document._id) {
   200‚Üí        if (options.fix) {
   201‚Üí          document._id = generateFoundryId();
   202‚Üí          modified = true;
   203‚Üí          result.fixed = true;
   204‚Üí          result.warnings.push(`Generated missing _id: ${document._id}`);
   205‚Üí        } else {
   206‚Üí          result.valid = false;
   207‚Üí          result.errors.push('Missing required _id field');
   208‚Üí        }
   209‚Üí      } else {
   210‚Üí        // Validate _id format (16 characters)
   211‚Üí        if (document._id.length !== 16) {
   212‚Üí          if (options.fix) {
   213‚Üí            document._id = generateFoundryId();
   214‚Üí            modified = true;
   215‚Üí            result.fixed = true;
   216‚Üí            result.warnings.push(`Fixed invalid _id format: ${document._id}`);
   217‚Üí          } else {
   218‚Üí            result.valid = false;
   219‚Üí            result.errors.push(`Invalid _id format: must be 16 characters, got ${document._id.length}`);
   220‚Üí          }
   221‚Üí        }
   222‚Üí
   223‚Üí        // Check for duplicate _id
   224‚Üí        const existingFiles = this.duplicateIds.get(document._id) || [];
   225‚Üí        existingFiles.push(`${packName}/${fileName}`);
   226‚Üí        this.duplicateIds.set(document._id, existingFiles);
   227‚Üí      }
   228‚Üí
   229‚Üí      // Validate required fields
   230‚Üí      if (!document.name) {
   231‚Üí        result.valid = false;
   232‚Üí        result.errors.push('Missing required name field');
   233‚Üí      }
   234‚Üí
   235‚Üí      if (!document.type) {
   236‚Üí        result.valid = false;
   237‚Üí        result.errors.push('Missing required type field');
   238‚Üí      }
   239‚Üí
   240‚Üí      // Validate category (required for traits, inferred for others)
   241‚Üí      if (!document.category) {
   242‚Üí        if (options.fix) {
   243‚Üí          document.category = this.inferCategory(packName, document.type);
   244‚Üí          modified = true;
   245‚Üí          result.fixed = true;
   246‚Üí          result.warnings.push(`Inferred category: ${document.category}`);
   247‚Üí        } else {
   248‚Üí          if (packName === 'traits') {
   249‚Üí            result.valid = false;
   250‚Üí            result.errors.push('Missing required category field for trait');
   251‚Üí          } else {
   252‚Üí            result.warnings.push('Missing category field (will be inferred from pack type)');
   253‚Üí          }
   254‚Üí        }
   255‚Üí      }
   256‚Üí
   257‚Üí      // Type-specific validation
   258‚Üí      this.validateTypeSpecific(document, result);
   259‚Üí
   260‚Üí      // Save modifications if any
   261‚Üí      if (modified && options.fix) {
   262‚Üí        const updatedContent = JSON.stringify(document, null, 2);
   263‚Üí        fs.writeFileSync(filePath, updatedContent, 'utf8');
   264‚Üí      }
   265‚Üí
   266‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   267‚Üí      result.valid = false;
   268‚Üí      if (error instanceof SyntaxError) {
   269‚Üí        result.errors.push(`Invalid JSON syntax: ${error.message}`);
   270‚Üí      } else {
   271‚Üí        result.errors.push(`File read error: ${error.message}`);
   272‚Üí      }
   273‚Üí    }
   274‚Üí
   275‚Üí    return result;
   276‚Üí  }
   277‚Üí
   278‚Üí  /**
   279‚Üí   * Infer category from pack name and document type
   280‚Üí   */
   281‚Üí  private inferCategory(packName: string, docType: string): string {
   282‚Üí    // Category mapping based on pack type
   283‚Üí    const categoryMap: Record<string, string> = {
   284‚Üí      'traits': 'general',
   285‚Üí      'talents': 'combat',
   286‚Üí      'augments': 'cybernetic',
   287‚Üí      'macros': 'utility'
   288‚Üí    };
   289‚Üí
   290‚Üí    return categoryMap[packName] || 'general';
   291‚Üí  }
   292‚Üí
   293‚Üí  /**
   294‚Üí   * Validate type-specific requirements
   295‚Üí   */
   296‚Üí  private validateTypeSpecific(document: CompendiumDocument, result: ValidationResult): void {
   297‚Üí    switch (document.type) {
   298‚Üí      case 'trait':
   299‚Üí        if (!document.system?.color) {
   300‚Üí          result.warnings.push('Missing system.color field for trait');
   301‚Üí        }
   302‚Üí        if (!document.system?.icon) {
   303‚Üí          result.warnings.push('Missing system.icon field for trait');
   304‚Üí        }
   305‚Üí        break;
   306‚Üí
   307‚Üí      case 'talent':
   308‚Üí      case 'augment':
   309‚Üí        if (!document.system?.description) {
   310‚Üí          result.warnings.push(`Missing system.description field for ${document.type}`);
   311‚Üí        }
   312‚Üí        break;
   313‚Üí
   314‚Üí      case 'script':
   315‚Üí        if (!document.command) {
   316‚Üí          result.valid = false;
   317‚Üí          result.errors.push('Missing command field for macro');
   318‚Üí        }
   319‚Üí        break;
   320‚Üí    }
   321‚Üí  }
   322‚Üí
   323‚Üí  /**
   324‚Üí   * Check for duplicate IDs across all documents
   325‚Üí   */
   326‚Üí  private checkDuplicateIds(): void {
   327‚Üí    console.log('\nüîç Checking for duplicate IDs...');
   328‚Üí    
   329‚Üí    const duplicates = Array.from(this.duplicateIds.entries())
   330‚Üí      .filter(([_, files]) => files.length > 1);
   331‚Üí
   332‚Üí    if (duplicates.length > 0) {
   333‚Üí      console.log(`‚ùå Found ${duplicates.length} duplicate ID(s):`);
   334‚Üí      duplicates.forEach(([id, files]) => {
   335‚Üí        console.log(`  ID ${id} appears in:`);
   336‚Üí        files.forEach(file => console.log(`    - ${file}`));
   337‚Üí      });
   338‚Üí    } else {
   339‚Üí      console.log('‚úÖ No duplicate IDs found');
   340‚Üí    }
   341‚Üí  }
   342‚Üí
   343‚Üí  /**
   344‚Üí   * Print comprehensive validation summary
   345‚Üí   */
   346‚Üí  private printValidationSummary(options: ValidationOptions): void {
   347‚Üí    console.log('\nüìä Validation Summary');
   348‚Üí    console.log('‚ïê'.repeat(50));
   349‚Üí
   350‚Üí    const totalErrors = Array.from(this.validationResults.values())
   351‚Üí      .reduce((sum, result) => sum + result.errors.length, 0);
   352‚Üí    
   353‚Üí    const totalWarnings = Array.from(this.validationResults.values())
   354‚Üí      .reduce((sum, result) => sum + result.warnings.length, 0);
   355‚Üí
   356‚Üí    const validPacks = Array.from(this.validationResults.values())
   357‚Üí      .filter(result => result.valid).length;
   358‚Üí
   359‚Üí    console.log(`üìÅ Total documents: ${this.totalDocuments}`);
   360‚Üí    console.log(`‚úÖ Valid packs: ${validPacks}/${this.validationResults.size}`);
   361‚Üí    console.log(`‚ùå Total errors: ${totalErrors}`);
   362‚Üí    console.log(`‚ö†Ô∏è  Total warnings: ${totalWarnings}`);
   363‚Üí    console.log(`üîß Documents fixed: ${this.totalFixed}`);
   364‚Üí    console.log(`üîó Duplicate IDs: ${this.duplicateIds.size > 0 ? Array.from(this.duplicateIds.entries()).filter(([_, files]) => files.length > 1).length : 0}`);
   365‚Üí
   366‚Üí    // Check for duplicate IDs
   367‚Üí    const duplicateCount = Array.from(this.duplicateIds.entries())
   368‚Üí      .filter(([_, files]) => files.length > 1).length;
   369‚Üí
   370‚Üí    // Overall status
   371‚Üí    const allValid = totalErrors === 0 && duplicateCount === 0;
   372‚Üí    console.log(`\nüéØ Overall Status: ${allValid ? '‚úÖ PASS' : '‚ùå FAIL'}`);
   373‚Üí
   374‚Üí    if (options.fix && this.totalFixed > 0) {
   375‚Üí      console.log(`\nüîß Fixed ${this.totalFixed} documents. Run again to verify.`);
   376‚Üí    }
   377‚Üí  }
   378‚Üí
   379‚Üí  /**
   380‚Üí   * Get detailed results for programmatic use
   381‚Üí   */
   382‚Üí  getResults(): {
   383‚Üí    valid: boolean;
   384‚Üí    totalDocuments: number;
   385‚Üí    totalErrors: number;
   386‚Üí    totalWarnings: number;
   387‚Üí    totalFixed: number;
   388‚Üí    duplicateIds: number;
   389‚Üí    packResults: Record<string, ValidationResult>;
   390‚Üí  } {
   391‚Üí    const totalErrors = Array.from(this.validationResults.values())
   392‚Üí      .reduce((sum, result) => sum + result.errors.length, 0);
   393‚Üí    
   394‚Üí    const totalWarnings = Array.from(this.validationResults.values())
   395‚Üí      .reduce((sum, result) => sum + result.warnings.length, 0);
   396‚Üí
   397‚Üí    const duplicateCount = Array.from(this.duplicateIds.entries())
   398‚Üí      .filter(([_, files]) => files.length > 1).length;
   399‚Üí
   400‚Üí    return {
   401‚Üí      valid: totalErrors === 0 && duplicateCount === 0,
   402‚Üí      totalDocuments: this.totalDocuments,
   403‚Üí      totalErrors,
   404‚Üí      totalWarnings,
   405‚Üí      totalFixed: this.totalFixed,
   406‚Üí      duplicateIds: duplicateCount,
   407‚Üí      packResults: Object.fromEntries(this.validationResults)
   408‚Üí    };
   409‚Üí  }
   410‚Üí}
   411‚Üí
   412‚Üí// CLI interface
   413‚Üíif (import.meta.url === `file://${process.argv[1]}`) {
   414‚Üí  const args = process.argv.slice(2);
   415‚Üí  const options: ValidationOptions = {
   416‚Üí    fix: args.includes('--fix'),
   417‚Üí    verbose: args.includes('--verbose') || args.includes('-v'),
   418‚Üí    packsDirectory: args.find(arg => arg.startsWith('--packs='))?.split('=')[1]
   419‚Üí  };
   420‚Üí
   421‚Üí  const validator = new CompendiumValidator(options.packsDirectory);
   422‚Üí  
   423‚Üí  validator.validateAll(options).then(success => {
   424‚Üí    process.exit(success ? 0 : 1);
   425‚Üí  }).catch(error => {
   426‚Üí    console.error('‚ùå Validation failed:', error);
   427‚Üí    process.exit(1);
   428‚Üí  });
   429‚Üí}
   430‚Üí
   431‚Üíexport default CompendiumValidator;
```

```
1‚Üí#!/usr/bin/env node
     2‚Üí
     3‚Üí/**
     4‚Üí * @fileoverview Split Pack Script - Phase B: File Granularity
     5‚Üí * @version 2.0.0 - Pipeline Implementation
     6‚Üí * @description Migrate from monolithic JSON to one file per document
     7‚Üí * @author Avant VTT Team
     8‚Üí */
     9‚Üí
    10‚Üíimport fs from 'fs';
    11‚Üíimport path from 'path';
    12‚Üíimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url';
    13‚Üí
    14‚Üí// ES module compatibility
    15‚Üíconst __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
    16‚Üíconst __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);
    17‚Üí
    18‚Üíinterface CompendiumDocument {
    19‚Üí  _id: string;
    20‚Üí  name: string;
    21‚Üí  type: string;
    22‚Üí  category?: string;
    23‚Üí  [key: string]: any;
    24‚Üí}
    25‚Üí
    26‚Üíinterface SplitOptions {
    27‚Üí  dryRun: boolean;
    28‚Üí  verbose: boolean;
    29‚Üí  overwrite: boolean;
    30‚Üí  packsDirectory?: string;
    31‚Üí}
    32‚Üí
    33‚Üíexport class PackSplitter {
    34‚Üí  private packsDirectory: string;
    35‚Üí  private processedFiles = 0;
    36‚Üí  private skippedFiles = 0;
    37‚Üí  private errors: string[] = [];
    38‚Üí
    39‚Üí  constructor(packsDirectory?: string) {
    40‚Üí    this.packsDirectory = packsDirectory || path.join(__dirname, '../../packs');
    41‚Üí  }
    42‚Üí
    43‚Üí  /**
    44‚Üí   * Split all monolithic JSON files into individual files
    45‚Üí   */
    46‚Üí  async splitAll(options: SplitOptions = { dryRun: false, verbose: false, overwrite: false }): Promise<boolean> {
    47‚Üí    console.log('üîÑ Starting Pack Splitting (Phase B: File Granularity)...');
    48‚Üí    console.log(`üìÅ Packs directory: ${this.packsDirectory}`);
    49‚Üí    
    50‚Üí    if (options.dryRun) {
    51‚Üí      console.log('üîç DRY RUN MODE - No files will be modified');
    52‚Üí    }
    53‚Üí
    54‚Üí    if (!fs.existsSync(this.packsDirectory)) {
    55‚Üí      console.error(`‚ùå Packs directory not found: ${this.packsDirectory}`);
    56‚Üí      return false;
    57‚Üí    }
    58‚Üí
    59‚Üí    // Get all pack directories
    60‚Üí    const packDirs = fs.readdirSync(this.packsDirectory, { withFileTypes: true })
    61‚Üí      .filter(dirent => dirent.isDirectory())
    62‚Üí      .map(dirent => dirent.name);
    63‚Üí
    64‚Üí    console.log(`üì¶ Found pack types: ${packDirs.join(', ')}`);
    65‚Üí
    66‚Üí    // Process each pack directory
    67‚Üí    for (const packDir of packDirs) {
    68‚Üí      const packPath = path.join(this.packsDirectory, packDir);
    69‚Üí      await this.splitPackDirectory(packDir, packPath, options);
    70‚Üí    }
    71‚Üí
    72‚Üí    this.printSummary();
    73‚Üí    return this.errors.length === 0;
    74‚Üí  }
    75‚Üí
    76‚Üí  /**
    77‚Üí   * Split a single pack directory
    78‚Üí   */
    79‚Üí  private async splitPackDirectory(packName: string, packPath: string, options: SplitOptions): Promise<void> {
    80‚Üí    console.log(`\nüìã Processing pack: ${packName}`);
    81‚Üí    
    82‚Üí    // Look for potential monolithic JSON files
    83‚Üí    const jsonFiles = fs.readdirSync(packPath)
    84‚Üí      .filter(file => file.endsWith('.json'))
    85‚Üí      .filter(file => !file.startsWith('_')) // Skip special files like _folders.json
    86‚Üí      .sort();
    87‚Üí
    88‚Üí    // Check if we already have individual files (modern structure)
    89‚Üí    const hasIndividualFiles = jsonFiles.some(file => {
    90‚Üí      const filePath = path.join(packPath, file);
    91‚Üí      try {
    92‚Üí        const content = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
    93‚Üí        const data = JSON.parse(content);
    94‚Üí        // Individual files have a single document with _id
    95‚Üí        return data._id && typeof data._id === 'string' && !Array.isArray(data);
    96‚Üí      } catch {
    97‚Üí        return false;
    98‚Üí      }
    99‚Üí    });
   100‚Üí
   101‚Üí    if (hasIndividualFiles) {
   102‚Üí      console.log(`  ‚úÖ Pack ${packName} already uses individual files (${jsonFiles.length} files)`);
   103‚Üí      return;
   104‚Üí    }
   105‚Üí
   106‚Üí    // Look for monolithic files (arrays of documents)
   107‚Üí    const monolithicFiles = jsonFiles.filter(file => {
   108‚Üí      const filePath = path.join(packPath, file);
   109‚Üí      try {
   110‚Üí        const content = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
   111‚Üí        const data = JSON.parse(content);
   112‚Üí        return Array.isArray(data) && data.length > 0;
   113‚Üí      } catch {
   114‚Üí        return false;
   115‚Üí      }
   116‚Üí    });
   117‚Üí
   118‚Üí    if (monolithicFiles.length === 0) {
   119‚Üí      console.log(`  ‚ÑπÔ∏è  No monolithic files found in ${packName}`);
   120‚Üí      return;
   121‚Üí    }
   122‚Üí
   123‚Üí    console.log(`  üìÑ Found ${monolithicFiles.length} monolithic file(s) to split`);
   124‚Üí
   125‚Üí    // Process each monolithic file
   126‚Üí    for (const file of monolithicFiles) {
   127‚Üí      await this.splitMonolithicFile(packName, packPath, file, options);
   128‚Üí    }
   129‚Üí  }
   130‚Üí
   131‚Üí  /**
   132‚Üí   * Split a monolithic JSON file into individual files
   133‚Üí   */
   134‚Üí  private async splitMonolithicFile(packName: string, packPath: string, fileName: string, options: SplitOptions): Promise<void> {
   135‚Üí    const filePath = path.join(packPath, fileName);
   136‚Üí    
   137‚Üí    try {
   138‚Üí      const content = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
   139‚Üí      const documents: CompendiumDocument[] = JSON.parse(content);
   140‚Üí      
   141‚Üí      if (!Array.isArray(documents)) {
   142‚Üí        if (options.verbose) {
   143‚Üí          console.log(`    ‚ÑπÔ∏è  ${fileName} is not an array, skipping`);
   144‚Üí        }
   145‚Üí        return;
   146‚Üí      }
   147‚Üí
   148‚Üí      console.log(`    üìÑ Splitting ${fileName} into ${documents.length} individual files`);
   149‚Üí
   150‚Üí      // Create backup if not dry run
   151‚Üí      if (!options.dryRun) {
   152‚Üí        const backupPath = `${filePath}.backup`;
   153‚Üí        if (!fs.existsSync(backupPath)) {
   154‚Üí          fs.copyFileSync(filePath, backupPath);
   155‚Üí          console.log(`    üíæ Created backup: ${fileName}.backup`);
   156‚Üí        }
   157‚Üí      }
   158‚Üí
   159‚Üí      // Process each document
   160‚Üí      for (const doc of documents) {
   161‚Üí        await this.createIndividualFile(packPath, doc, options);
   162‚Üí      }
   163‚Üí
   164‚Üí      // Remove original monolithic file if successful
   165‚Üí      if (!options.dryRun) {
   166‚Üí        fs.unlinkSync(filePath);
   167‚Üí        console.log(`    üóëÔ∏è  Removed original monolithic file: ${fileName}`);
   168‚Üí      }
   169‚Üí
   170‚Üí      this.processedFiles++;
   171‚Üí
   172‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   173‚Üí      const errorMessage = `Failed to split ${fileName}: ${error.message}`;
   174‚Üí      this.errors.push(errorMessage);
   175‚Üí      console.error(`    ‚ùå ${errorMessage}`);
   176‚Üí    }
   177‚Üí  }
   178‚Üí
   179‚Üí  /**
   180‚Üí   * Create an individual file for a document
   181‚Üí   */
   182‚Üí  private async createIndividualFile(packPath: string, doc: CompendiumDocument, options: SplitOptions): Promise<void> {
   183‚Üí    if (!doc._id) {
   184‚Üí      throw new Error(`Document "${doc.name}" missing required _id field`);
   185‚Üí    }
   186‚Üí
   187‚Üí    // Generate filename from document name
   188‚Üí    const filename = this.generateFilename(doc.name);
   189‚Üí    const filePath = path.join(packPath, filename);
   190‚Üí
   191‚Üí    // Check if file already exists
   192‚Üí    if (fs.existsSync(filePath) && !options.overwrite) {
   193‚Üí      console.log(`      ‚ö†Ô∏è  Skipping ${filename} (already exists)`);
   194‚Üí      this.skippedFiles++;
   195‚Üí      return;
   196‚Üí    }
   197‚Üí
   198‚Üí    if (options.verbose) {
   199‚Üí      console.log(`      üìù Creating ${filename} (ID: ${doc._id})`);
   200‚Üí    }
   201‚Üí
   202‚Üí    // Write individual file
   203‚Üí    if (!options.dryRun) {
   204‚Üí      const content = JSON.stringify(doc, null, 2);
   205‚Üí      fs.writeFileSync(filePath, content, 'utf8');
   206‚Üí    }
   207‚Üí  }
   208‚Üí
   209‚Üí  /**
   210‚Üí   * Generate a filename from a document name
   211‚Üí   */
   212‚Üí  private generateFilename(name: string): string {
   213‚Üí    return name
   214‚Üí      .toLowerCase()
   215‚Üí      .replace(/[^a-z0-9\s-]/g, '') // Remove special characters
   216‚Üí      .replace(/\s+/g, '-') // Replace spaces with hyphens
   217‚Üí      .replace(/-+/g, '-') // Collapse multiple hyphens
   218‚Üí      .replace(/^-|-$/g, '') // Remove leading/trailing hyphens
   219‚Üí      + '.json';
   220‚Üí  }
   221‚Üí
   222‚Üí  /**
   223‚Üí   * Print processing summary
   224‚Üí   */
   225‚Üí  private printSummary(): void {
   226‚Üí    console.log('\nüìä Split Pack Summary');
   227‚Üí    console.log('‚ïê'.repeat(50));
   228‚Üí    console.log(`üìÑ Processed files: ${this.processedFiles}`);
   229‚Üí    console.log(`‚è≠Ô∏è  Skipped files: ${this.skippedFiles}`);
   230‚Üí    console.log(`‚ùå Errors: ${this.errors.length}`);
   231‚Üí
   232‚Üí    if (this.errors.length > 0) {
   233‚Üí      console.log('\n‚ùå Error Details:');
   234‚Üí      this.errors.forEach((error, index) => {
   235‚Üí        console.log(`   ${index + 1}. ${error}`);
   236‚Üí      });
   237‚Üí    }
   238‚Üí
   239‚Üí    const status = this.errors.length === 0 ? '‚úÖ SUCCESS' : '‚ùå FAILED';
   240‚Üí    console.log(`\nüéØ Overall Status: ${status}`);
   241‚Üí  }
   242‚Üí}
   243‚Üí
   244‚Üí// CLI interface
   245‚Üíif (import.meta.url === `file://${process.argv[1]}`) {
   246‚Üí  const args = process.argv.slice(2);
   247‚Üí  const options: SplitOptions = {
   248‚Üí    dryRun: args.includes('--dry-run'),
   249‚Üí    verbose: args.includes('--verbose') || args.includes('-v'),
   250‚Üí    overwrite: args.includes('--overwrite'),
   251‚Üí    packsDirectory: args.find(arg => arg.startsWith('--packs='))?.split('=')[1]
   252‚Üí  };
   253‚Üí
   254‚Üí  const splitter = new PackSplitter(options.packsDirectory);
   255‚Üí  
   256‚Üí  splitter.splitAll(options).then(success => {
   257‚Üí    process.exit(success ? 0 : 1);
   258‚Üí  }).catch(error => {
   259‚Üí    console.error('‚ùå Split operation failed:', error);
   260‚Üí    process.exit(1);
   261‚Üí  });
   262‚Üí}
   263‚Üí
   264‚Üíexport default PackSplitter;

1‚Üí#!/usr/bin/env node
     2‚Üí
     3‚Üí/**
     4‚Üí * @fileoverview Folder Validator - Phase C: Folder Support
     5‚Üí * @version 2.0.0 - Pipeline Implementation
     6‚Üí * @description Validates _folders.json structure and references
     7‚Üí * @author Avant VTT Team
     8‚Üí */
     9‚Üí
    10‚Üíimport fs from 'fs';
    11‚Üíimport path from 'path';
    12‚Üíimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url';
    13‚Üí
    14‚Üí// ES module compatibility
    15‚Üíconst __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
    16‚Üíconst __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);
    17‚Üí
    18‚Üíinterface FolderDocument {
    19‚Üí  _id: string;
    20‚Üí  name: string;
    21‚Üí  type: 'Folder';
    22‚Üí  parent: string | null;
    23‚Üí  description?: string;
    24‚Üí  color?: string;
    25‚Üí  sort: number;
    26‚Üí  flags?: any;
    27‚Üí}
    28‚Üí
    29‚Üíinterface FolderValidationResult {
    30‚Üí  valid: boolean;
    31‚Üí  errors: string[];
    32‚Üí  warnings: string[];
    33‚Üí  folders: FolderDocument[];
    34‚Üí  folderCount: number;
    35‚Üí}
    36‚Üí
    37‚Üíinterface FolderValidationOptions {
    38‚Üí  verbose: boolean;
    39‚Üí  packsDirectory?: string;
    40‚Üí}
    41‚Üí
    42‚Üíexport class FolderValidator {
    43‚Üí  private packsDirectory: string;
    44‚Üí  private validationResults: Map<string, FolderValidationResult> = new Map();
    45‚Üí  private globalFolderIds: Set<string> = new Set();
    46‚Üí
    47‚Üí  constructor(packsDirectory?: string) {
    48‚Üí    this.packsDirectory = packsDirectory || path.join(__dirname, '../../packs');
    49‚Üí  }
    50‚Üí
    51‚Üí  /**
    52‚Üí   * Validate all _folders.json files
    53‚Üí   */
    54‚Üí  async validateAll(options: FolderValidationOptions = { verbose: false }): Promise<boolean> {
    55‚Üí    console.log('üîç Starting Folder Validation (Phase C)...');
    56‚Üí    console.log(`üìÅ Packs directory: ${this.packsDirectory}`);
    57‚Üí    
    58‚Üí    if (!fs.existsSync(this.packsDirectory)) {
    59‚Üí      console.error(`‚ùå Packs directory not found: ${this.packsDirectory}`);
    60‚Üí      return false;
    61‚Üí    }
    62‚Üí
    63‚Üí    // Reset state
    64‚Üí    this.validationResults.clear();
    65‚Üí    this.globalFolderIds.clear();
    66‚Üí
    67‚Üí    // Get all pack directories
    68‚Üí    const packDirs = fs.readdirSync(this.packsDirectory, { withFileTypes: true })
    69‚Üí      .filter(dirent => dirent.isDirectory())
    70‚Üí      .map(dirent => dirent.name);
    71‚Üí
    72‚Üí    console.log(`üì¶ Found pack types: ${packDirs.join(', ')}`);
    73‚Üí
    74‚Üí    let allValid = true;
    75‚Üí
    76‚Üí    // First pass: validate individual folder files
    77‚Üí    for (const packDir of packDirs) {
    78‚Üí      const packPath = path.join(this.packsDirectory, packDir);
    79‚Üí      const valid = await this.validatePackFolders(packDir, packPath, options);
    80‚Üí      
    81‚Üí      if (!valid) {
    82‚Üí        allValid = false;
    83‚Üí      }
    84‚Üí    }
    85‚Üí
    86‚Üí    // Second pass: validate cross-references
    87‚Üí    this.validateGlobalReferences();
    88‚Üí
    89‚Üí    // Print summary
    90‚Üí    this.printValidationSummary(options);
    91‚Üí
    92‚Üí    return allValid;
    93‚Üí  }
    94‚Üí
    95‚Üí  /**
    96‚Üí   * Validate folders for a single pack
    97‚Üí   */
    98‚Üí  private async validatePackFolders(packName: string, packPath: string, options: FolderValidationOptions): Promise<boolean> {
    99‚Üí    console.log(`\nüìã Validating folders for pack: ${packName}`);
   100‚Üí    
   101‚Üí    const foldersPath = path.join(packPath, '_folders.json');
   102‚Üí    const result: FolderValidationResult = {
   103‚Üí      valid: true,
   104‚Üí      errors: [],
   105‚Üí      warnings: [],
   106‚Üí      folders: [],
   107‚Üí      folderCount: 0
   108‚Üí    };
   109‚Üí
   110‚Üí    // Check if _folders.json exists
   111‚Üí    if (!fs.existsSync(foldersPath)) {
   112‚Üí      result.warnings.push('No _folders.json file found (pack will use flat structure)');
   113‚Üí      console.log(`  ‚ÑπÔ∏è  No _folders.json file found for ${packName}`);
   114‚Üí      this.validationResults.set(packName, result);
   115‚Üí      return true;
   116‚Üí    }
   117‚Üí
   118‚Üí    try {
   119‚Üí      // Read and parse _folders.json
   120‚Üí      const fileContent = fs.readFileSync(foldersPath, 'utf8');
   121‚Üí      const folders: FolderDocument[] = JSON.parse(fileContent);
   122‚Üí
   123‚Üí      if (!Array.isArray(folders)) {
   124‚Üí        result.valid = false;
   125‚Üí        result.errors.push('_folders.json must contain an array of folder objects');
   126‚Üí        console.error(`  ‚ùå ${packName}: _folders.json must be an array`);
   127‚Üí        this.validationResults.set(packName, result);
   128‚Üí        return false;
   129‚Üí      }
   130‚Üí
   131‚Üí      result.folders = folders;
   132‚Üí      result.folderCount = folders.length;
   133‚Üí
   134‚Üí      console.log(`  üìÑ Found ${folders.length} folder(s) in ${packName}`);
   135‚Üí
   136‚Üí      // Validate each folder
   137‚Üí      const folderIds = new Set<string>();
   138‚Üí      for (const folder of folders) {
   139‚Üí        this.validateSingleFolder(folder, packName, folderIds, result, options);
   140‚Üí      }
   141‚Üí
   142‚Üí      // Validate parent references within pack
   143‚Üí      this.validateParentReferences(folders, packName, result);
   144‚Üí
   145‚Üí      this.validationResults.set(packName, result);
   146‚Üí
   147‚Üí      if (result.valid) {
   148‚Üí        console.log(`  ‚úÖ ${packName}: ${folders.length} folders validated successfully`);
   149‚Üí      } else {
   150‚Üí        console.log(`  ‚ùå ${packName}: ${result.errors.length} errors, ${result.warnings.length} warnings`);
   151‚Üí      }
   152‚Üí
   153‚Üí      return result.valid;
   154‚Üí
   155‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   156‚Üí      result.valid = false;
   157‚Üí      if (error instanceof SyntaxError) {
   158‚Üí        result.errors.push(`Invalid JSON syntax in _folders.json: ${error.message}`);
   159‚Üí      } else {
   160‚Üí        result.errors.push(`Error reading _folders.json: ${error.message}`);
   161‚Üí      }
   162‚Üí      console.error(`  ‚ùå ${packName}: ${result.errors[result.errors.length - 1]}`);
   163‚Üí      this.validationResults.set(packName, result);
   164‚Üí      return false;
   165‚Üí    }
   166‚Üí  }
   167‚Üí
   168‚Üí  /**
   169‚Üí   * Validate a single folder document
   170‚Üí   */
   171‚Üí  private validateSingleFolder(
   172‚Üí    folder: FolderDocument, 
   173‚Üí    packName: string, 
   174‚Üí    folderIds: Set<string>, 
   175‚Üí    result: FolderValidationResult, 
   176‚Üí    options: FolderValidationOptions
   177‚Üí  ): void {
   178‚Üí    const folderLabel = `${packName}/${folder.name}`;
   179‚Üí
   180‚Üí    // Check required fields
   181‚Üí    if (!folder._id) {
   182‚Üí      result.valid = false;
   183‚Üí      result.errors.push(`${folderLabel}: Missing required _id field`);
   184‚Üí      return;
   185‚Üí    }
   186‚Üí
   187‚Üí    if (folder._id.length !== 16) {
   188‚Üí      result.valid = false;
   189‚Üí      result.errors.push(`${folderLabel}: _id must be 16 characters, got ${folder._id.length}`);
   190‚Üí    }
   191‚Üí
   192‚Üí    if (!folder.name) {
   193‚Üí      result.valid = false;
   194‚Üí      result.errors.push(`${folderLabel}: Missing required name field`);
   195‚Üí    }
   196‚Üí
   197‚Üí    if (folder.type !== 'Folder') {
   198‚Üí      result.valid = false;
   199‚Üí      result.errors.push(`${folderLabel}: Type must be 'Folder', got '${folder.type}'`);
   200‚Üí    }
   201‚Üí
   202‚Üí    if (typeof folder.sort !== 'number') {
   203‚Üí      result.valid = false;
   204‚Üí      result.errors.push(`${folderLabel}: Sort must be a number, got ${typeof folder.sort}`);
   205‚Üí    }
   206‚Üí
   207‚Üí    // Check for duplicate IDs within pack
   208‚Üí    if (folderIds.has(folder._id)) {
   209‚Üí      result.valid = false;
   210‚Üí      result.errors.push(`${folderLabel}: Duplicate _id '${folder._id}' within pack`);
   211‚Üí    } else {
   212‚Üí      folderIds.add(folder._id);
   213‚Üí    }
   214‚Üí
   215‚Üí    // Check for duplicate IDs globally
   216‚Üí    if (this.globalFolderIds.has(folder._id)) {
   217‚Üí      result.valid = false;
   218‚Üí      result.errors.push(`${folderLabel}: Duplicate _id '${folder._id}' across packs`);
   219‚Üí    } else {
   220‚Üí      this.globalFolderIds.add(folder._id);
   221‚Üí    }
   222‚Üí
   223‚Üí    // Validate optional fields
   224‚Üí    if (folder.color && !/^#[0-9A-Fa-f]{6}$/.test(folder.color)) {
   225‚Üí      result.warnings.push(`${folderLabel}: Invalid color format '${folder.color}' (should be #RRGGBB)`);
   226‚Üí    }
   227‚Üí
   228‚Üí    if (folder.description && folder.description.length < 10) {
   229‚Üí      result.warnings.push(`${folderLabel}: Very short description`);
   230‚Üí    }
   231‚Üí
   232‚Üí    if (options.verbose) {
   233‚Üí      console.log(`    ‚úÖ ${folder.name} (${folder._id})`);
   234‚Üí    }
   235‚Üí  }
   236‚Üí
   237‚Üí  /**
   238‚Üí   * Validate parent references within a pack
   239‚Üí   */
   240‚Üí  private validateParentReferences(folders: FolderDocument[], packName: string, result: FolderValidationResult): void {
   241‚Üí    const folderIds = new Set(folders.map(f => f._id));
   242‚Üí    
   243‚Üí    for (const folder of folders) {
   244‚Üí      if (folder.parent) {
   245‚Üí        if (!folderIds.has(folder.parent)) {
   246‚Üí          result.valid = false;
   247‚Üí          result.errors.push(`${packName}/${folder.name}: Parent '${folder.parent}' not found in pack`);
   248‚Üí        }
   249‚Üí      }
   250‚Üí    }
   251‚Üí  }
   252‚Üí
   253‚Üí  /**
   254‚Üí   * Validate global folder references (for future cross-pack support)
   255‚Üí   */
   256‚Üí  private validateGlobalReferences(): void {
   257‚Üí    console.log('\nüîó Validating global folder references...');
   258‚Üí    
   259‚Üí    // Currently no cross-pack references, but this is where they would be validated
   260‚Üí    console.log('‚úÖ Global folder references validated');
   261‚Üí  }
   262‚Üí
   263‚Üí  /**
   264‚Üí   * Print comprehensive validation summary
   265‚Üí   */
   266‚Üí  private printValidationSummary(options: FolderValidationOptions): void {
   267‚Üí    console.log('\nüìä Folder Validation Summary');
   268‚Üí    console.log('‚ïê'.repeat(50));
   269‚Üí
   270‚Üí    const totalFolders = Array.from(this.validationResults.values())
   271‚Üí      .reduce((sum, result) => sum + result.folderCount, 0);
   272‚Üí    
   273‚Üí    const totalErrors = Array.from(this.validationResults.values())
   274‚Üí      .reduce((sum, result) => sum + result.errors.length, 0);
   275‚Üí    
   276‚Üí    const totalWarnings = Array.from(this.validationResults.values())
   277‚Üí      .reduce((sum, result) => sum + result.warnings.length, 0);
   278‚Üí
   279‚Üí    const validPacks = Array.from(this.validationResults.values())
   280‚Üí      .filter(result => result.valid).length;
   281‚Üí
   282‚Üí    console.log(`üìÅ Total folders: ${totalFolders}`);
   283‚Üí    console.log(`‚úÖ Valid packs: ${validPacks}/${this.validationResults.size}`);
   284‚Üí    console.log(`‚ùå Total errors: ${totalErrors}`);
   285‚Üí    console.log(`‚ö†Ô∏è  Total warnings: ${totalWarnings}`);
   286‚Üí
   287‚Üí    // Print pack-by-pack results
   288‚Üí    for (const [packName, result] of this.validationResults.entries()) {
   289‚Üí      const status = result.valid ? '‚úÖ' : '‚ùå';
   290‚Üí      console.log(`  ${status} ${packName}: ${result.folderCount} folders, ${result.errors.length} errors, ${result.warnings.length} warnings`);
   291‚Üí    }
   292‚Üí
   293‚Üí    // Print error details
   294‚Üí    if (totalErrors > 0) {
   295‚Üí      console.log('\n‚ùå Error Details:');
   296‚Üí      for (const [packName, result] of this.validationResults.entries()) {
   297‚Üí        if (result.errors.length > 0) {
   298‚Üí          console.log(`  üì¶ ${packName}:`);
   299‚Üí          result.errors.forEach((error, index) => {
   300‚Üí            console.log(`    ${index + 1}. ${error}`);
   301‚Üí          });
   302‚Üí        }
   303‚Üí      }
   304‚Üí    }
   305‚Üí
   306‚Üí    // Print warning details
   307‚Üí    if (totalWarnings > 0) {
   308‚Üí      console.log('\n‚ö†Ô∏è Warning Details:');
   309‚Üí      for (const [packName, result] of this.validationResults.entries()) {
   310‚Üí        if (result.warnings.length > 0) {
   311‚Üí          console.log(`  üì¶ ${packName}:`);
   312‚Üí          result.warnings.forEach((warning, index) => {
   313‚Üí            console.log(`    ${index + 1}. ${warning}`);
   314‚Üí          });
   315‚Üí        }
   316‚Üí      }
   317‚Üí    }
   318‚Üí
   319‚Üí    // Overall status
   320‚Üí    const allValid = totalErrors === 0;
   321‚Üí    console.log(`\nüéØ Overall Status: ${allValid ? '‚úÖ PASS' : '‚ùå FAIL'}`);
   322‚Üí  }
   323‚Üí
   324‚Üí  /**
   325‚Üí   * Get validation results for programmatic use
   326‚Üí   */
   327‚Üí  getResults(): {
   328‚Üí    valid: boolean;
   329‚Üí    totalFolders: number;
   330‚Üí    totalErrors: number;
   331‚Üí    totalWarnings: number;
   332‚Üí    packResults: Record<string, FolderValidationResult>;
   333‚Üí  } {
   334‚Üí    const totalFolders = Array.from(this.validationResults.values())
   335‚Üí      .reduce((sum, result) => sum + result.folderCount, 0);
   336‚Üí    
   337‚Üí    const totalErrors = Array.from(this.validationResults.values())
   338‚Üí      .reduce((sum, result) => sum + result.errors.length, 0);
   339‚Üí    
   340‚Üí    const totalWarnings = Array.from(this.validationResults.values())
   341‚Üí      .reduce((sum, result) => sum + result.warnings.length, 0);
   342‚Üí
   343‚Üí    return {
   344‚Üí      valid: totalErrors === 0,
   345‚Üí      totalFolders,
   346‚Üí      totalErrors,
   347‚Üí      totalWarnings,
   348‚Üí      packResults: Object.fromEntries(this.validationResults)
   349‚Üí    };
   350‚Üí  }
   351‚Üí}
   352‚Üí
   353‚Üí// CLI interface
   354‚Üíif (import.meta.url === `file://${process.argv[1]}`) {
   355‚Üí  const args = process.argv.slice(2);
   356‚Üí  const options: FolderValidationOptions = {
   357‚Üí    verbose: args.includes('--verbose') || args.includes('-v'),
   358‚Üí    packsDirectory: args.find(arg => arg.startsWith('--packs='))?.split('=')[1]
   359‚Üí  };
   360‚Üí
   361‚Üí  const validator = new FolderValidator(options.packsDirectory);
   362‚Üí  
   363‚Üí  validator.validateAll(options).then(success => {
   364‚Üí    process.exit(success ? 0 : 1);
   365‚Üí  }).catch(error => {
   366‚Üí    console.error('‚ùå Folder validation failed:', error);
   367‚Üí    process.exit(1);
   368‚Üí  });
   369‚Üí}
   370‚Üí
   371‚Üíexport default FolderValidator;
```

   150‚Üí  // Filter for custom/world traits only (exclude system traits)
   151‚Üí  const customTraits = allTraitsResult.data.filter(trait => trait.source === 'world');
   152‚Üí  console.log(\`üìä Found \${customTraits.length} custom traits (filtered from \${allTraitsResult.data.length} total)\`);
   153‚Üí  
   154‚Üí  if (customTraits.length === 0) {
   155‚Üí    ui.notifications.warn("No custom traits found to export. Only custom/world traits are exported (system traits excluded).");
   156‚Üí    console.log("üí° Tip: Create custom traits using the 'Create Custom Trait' macro or by adding items to the 'Custom Traits' compendium.");
   157‚Üí    return;
   158‚Üí  }
   159‚Üí  
   160‚Üí  // Build export data structure
   161‚Üí  const exportData = {
   162‚Üí    metadata: {
   163‚Üí      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
   164‚Üí      systemVersion: game.system.version,
   165‚Üí      traitCount: customTraits.length,
   166‚Üí      formatVersion: "1.0.0",
   167‚Üí      exportSource: "custom-only",
   168‚Üí      description: "Custom traits export (excludes system built-in traits)"
   169‚Üí    },
   170‚Üí    traits: customTraits.map(trait => ({
   171‚Üí      id: trait.id,
   172‚Üí      name: trait.name,
   173‚Üí      color: trait.color,
   174‚Üí      icon: trait.icon,
   175‚Üí      localKey: trait.localKey,
   176‚Üí      description: trait.description,
   177‚Üí      source: trait.source,
   178‚Üí      tags: trait.item.system?.tags || [],
   179‚Üí      rarity: trait.item.system?.rarity || "common",
   180‚Üí      effects: trait.item.system?.effects || "",
   181‚Üí      textColor: trait.item.system?.textColor || "#000000",
   182‚Üí      systemData: trait.item.system,
   183‚Üí      exportedAt: new Date().toISOString()
   184‚Üí    }))
   185‚Üí  };
   186‚Üí  
   187‚Üí  // Create JSON content and blob
   188‚Üí  const jsonContent = JSON.stringify(exportData, null, 2);
   189‚Üí  const blob = new Blob([jsonContent], { type: 'application/json' });
   190‚Üí  const filename = \`custom-traits-export-\${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.json\`;
   191‚Üí  
   192‚Üí  // Use robust download function
   193‚Üí  const downloadSuccess = await saveFile(blob, filename);
   194‚Üí  
   195‚Üí  if (downloadSuccess !== false) { // Success or fallback, but not user cancel
   196‚Üí    console.log(\`‚úÖ Export complete: \${customTraits.length} custom traits\`);
   197‚Üí    console.log("üìÅ Custom traits exported:", customTraits.map(t => t.name));
   198‚Üí    ui.notifications.info(\`Successfully exported \${customTraits.length} custom traits!\`);
   199‚Üí  } else {
   200‚Üí    console.log("‚ÑπÔ∏è Export canceled by user");
   201‚Üí  }
   202‚Üí  
   203‚Üí} catch (error) {
   204‚Üí  console.error("‚ùå Export failed:", error);
   205‚Üí  ui.notifications.error(\`Export failed: \${error.message}\`);
   206‚Üí}
   207‚Üí    `,
   208‚Üí    img: "icons/svg/download.svg",
   209‚Üí    folder: null,
   210‚Üí    sort: 100,
   211‚Üí    flags: {}
   212‚Üí  },
   213‚Üí
   214‚Üí  {
   215‚Üí    name: "Create Custom Trait",
   216‚Üí    type: "script",
   217‚Üí    scope: "global",
   218‚Üí    command: `
   219‚Üí/**
   220‚Üí * Create Custom Trait Macro
   221‚Üí * Opens trait creation sheet and ensures custom trait compendium exists
   222‚Üí */
   223‚Üí
   224‚Üíconsole.log("üé® Starting custom trait creation...");
   225‚Üí
   226‚Üí// Ensure custom traits compendium exists
   227‚Üílet customTraitsPack = game.packs.get('world.custom-traits');
   228‚Üí
   229‚Üíif (!customTraitsPack) {
   230‚Üí    console.log("üì¶ Creating custom traits compendium...");
   231‚Üí    
   232‚Üí    try {
   233‚Üí        // Create the custom traits compendium
   234‚Üí        const packData = {
   235‚Üí            name: 'world.custom-traits',
   236‚Üí            label: 'Custom Traits',
   237‚Üí            type: 'Item',
   238‚Üí            system: game.system.id,
   239‚Üí            private: false
   240‚Üí        };
   241‚Üí        
   242‚Üí        customTraitsPack = await foundry.documents.collections.CompendiumCollection.createCompendium(packData);
   243‚Üí        
   244‚Üí        console.log("‚úÖ Custom traits compendium created successfully!");
   245‚Üí        ui.notifications.info("üì¶ Created 'Custom Traits' compendium!");
   246‚Üí        
   247‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   248‚Üí        console.error("‚ùå Failed to create custom traits compendium:", error);
   249‚Üí        ui.notifications.error("Failed to create custom traits compendium. Using world items instead.");
   250‚Üí        
   251‚Üí        // Fallback: create trait as world item instead
   252‚Üí        console.log("üîÑ Falling back to world item creation...");
   253‚Üí        
   254‚Üí        const traitData = {
   255‚Üí            name: "New Custom Trait",
   256‚Üí            type: "trait",
   257‚Üí            img: "icons/svg/item-bag.svg",
   258‚Üí            system: {
   259‚Üí                description: "",
   260‚Üí                color: "#00E0DC",
   261‚Üí                icon: "fas fa-tag",
   262‚Üí                localKey: "",
   263‚Üí                tags: [],
   264‚Üí                rarity: "common",
   265‚Üí                effects: "",
   266‚Üí                textColor: "#000000"
   267‚Üí            }
   268‚Üí        };
   269‚Üí        
   270‚Üí        try {
   271‚Üí            const newTrait = await Item.create(traitData);
   272‚Üí            console.log("‚úÖ Created world trait item:", newTrait.name);
   273‚Üí            ui.notifications.info(\`Created trait '\${newTrait.name}' in world items!\`);
   274‚Üí            
   275‚Üí            // Open the trait sheet for editing
   276‚Üí            newTrait.sheet.render(true);
   277‚Üí            
   278‚Üí        } catch (itemError) {
   279‚Üí            console.error("‚ùå Failed to create world trait:", itemError);
   280‚Üí            ui.notifications.error("Failed to create trait item.");
   281‚Üí        }
   282‚Üí        
   283‚Üí        return;
   284‚Üí    }
   285‚Üí}
   286‚Üí
   287‚Üíconsole.log("‚úÖ Custom traits compendium available:", customTraitsPack.metadata.label);
   288‚Üí
   289‚Üí// Check if compendium is locked
   290‚Üíif (customTraitsPack.locked) {
   291‚Üí    console.log("üîì Custom traits compendium is locked, unlocking for editing...");
   292‚Üí    
   293‚Üí    try {
   294‚Üí        // Unlock the compendium for editing
   295‚Üí        await customTraitsPack.configure({ locked: false });
   296‚Üí        console.log("‚úÖ Compendium unlocked successfully!");
   297‚Üí        ui.notifications.info("üîì Unlocked custom traits compendium for editing!");
   298‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   299‚Üí        console.error("‚ùå Failed to unlock compendium:", error);
   300‚Üí        ui.notifications.warn("‚ö†Ô∏è Could not unlock compendium. You may need to right-click it and select 'Toggle Edit Lock'.");
   301‚Üí    }
   302‚Üí}
   303‚Üí
   304‚Üí// Create new trait in the custom compendium
   305‚Üíconsole.log("üé® Creating new trait in custom compendium...");
   306‚Üí
   307‚Üíconst traitData = {
   308‚Üí    name: "New Custom Trait",
   309‚Üí    type: "trait",
   310‚Üí    img: "icons/svg/item-bag.svg",
   311‚Üí    system: {
   312‚Üí        description: "",
   313‚Üí        color: "#00E0DC",
   314‚Üí        icon: "fas fa-tag",
   315‚Üí        localKey: "",
   316‚Üí        tags: [],
   317‚Üí        rarity: "common",
   318‚Üí        effects: "",
   319‚Üí        textColor: "#000000"
   320‚Üí    }
   321‚Üí};
   322‚Üí
   323‚Üítry {
   324‚Üí    // Create the trait in the compendium
   325‚Üí    const newTrait = await Item.create(traitData, { pack: customTraitsPack.collection });
   326‚Üí    console.log("‚úÖ Created custom trait:", newTrait.name);
   327‚Üí    ui.notifications.info(\`Created trait '\${newTrait.name}' in Custom Traits compendium!\`);
   328‚Üí    
   329‚Üí    // Open the trait sheet for immediate editing
   330‚Üí    newTrait.sheet.render(true);
   331‚Üí    
   332‚Üí    console.log("üé® Trait creation complete! Edit the trait and save your changes.");
   333‚Üí    
   334‚Üí    // Clear trait provider cache so new trait appears in autocomplete
   335‚Üí    if (game?.avant?.initializationManager) {
   336‚Üí        const traitProvider = game.avant.initializationManager.getService('traitProvider');
   337‚Üí        if (traitProvider && typeof traitProvider.clearCache === 'function') {
   338‚Üí            traitProvider.clearCache();
   339‚Üí            console.log("üîÑ Cleared trait provider cache - new trait will appear in autocomplete");
   340‚Üí        }
   341‚Üí    }
   342‚Üí    
   343‚Üí} catch (error) {
   344‚Üí    console.error("‚ùå Failed to create trait:", error);
   345‚Üí    ui.notifications.error(\`Failed to create trait: \${error.message}\`);
   346‚Üí}
   347‚Üí    `,
   348‚Üí    img: "icons/svg/item-bag.svg",
   349‚Üí    folder: null,
   350‚Üí    sort: 50,
   351‚Üí    flags: {
   352‚Üí      "avant": {
   353‚Üí        "description": "Create a new custom trait in the Custom Traits compendium with trait sheet interface",
   354‚Üí        "version": "1.0.0",
   355‚Üí        "category": "trait-management"
   356‚Üí      }
   357‚Üí    }
   358‚Üí  },
   359‚Üí
   360‚Üí  {
   361‚Üí    name: "Import to Avant Traits",
   362‚Üí    type: "script",
   363‚Üí    scope: "global",
   364‚Üí    command: `
   365‚Üí/**
   366‚Üí * Import to Avant Traits Macro
   367‚Üí * Imports traits from JSON files into the Avant Traits system compendium
   368‚Üí */
   369‚Üí
   370‚Üíconsole.log("üîÑ Starting trait import process...");
   371‚Üí
   372‚Üí// Check if Avant Traits compendium exists and is unlocked
   373‚Üíconst avantTraitsPack = game.packs.get('avant.avant-traits');
   374‚Üíif (!avantTraitsPack) {
   375‚Üí  ui.notifications.error("Avant Traits compendium pack not found!");
   376‚Üí  return;
   377‚Üí}
   378‚Üí
   379‚Üíif (avantTraitsPack.locked) {
   380‚Üí  ui.notifications.warn("Avant Traits compendium is locked! Please unlock it first by right-clicking the compendium and selecting 'Toggle Edit Lock'.");
   381‚Üí  return;
   382‚Üí}
   383‚Üí
   384‚Üí// Also check for world custom traits pack as fallback
   385‚Üíconst customTraitsPack = game.packs.get('world.custom-traits');
   386‚Üí
   387‚Üí// Create dialog to let user choose target and select file
   388‚Üíconst dialogContent = \`
   389‚Üí  <div style="padding: 10px;">
   390‚Üí    <h3>Import Avant Traits</h3>
   391‚Üí    <p>Select a JSON file containing trait data to import.</p>
   392‚Üí    
   393‚Üí    <div style="margin: 10px 0;">
   394‚Üí      <label><strong>Import to:</strong></label>
   395‚Üí      <select id="target-pack" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 5px;">
   396‚Üí        <option value="avant.avant-traits">Avant Traits (System Pack)</option>
   397‚Üí        \${customTraitsPack ? '<option value="world.custom-traits">Custom Traits (World Pack)</option>' : ''}
   398‚Üí      </select>
   399‚Üí    </div>
   400‚Üí    
   401‚Üí    <div style="margin: 10px 0;">
   402‚Üí      <label for="trait-file"><strong>Select JSON File:</strong></label>
   403‚Üí      <input type="file" id="trait-file" accept=".json" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 5px;">
   404‚Üí    </div>
   405‚Üí    
   406‚Üí    <div style="margin: 10px 0;">
   407‚Üí      <label>
   408‚Üí        <input type="checkbox" id="overwrite-existing" checked>
   409‚Üí        Overwrite existing traits with same name
   410‚Üí      </label>
   411‚Üí    </div>
   412‚Üí  </div>
   413‚Üí\`;
   414‚Üí
   415‚Üí// Show dialog
   416‚Üínew Dialog({
   417‚Üí  title: "Import Avant Traits",
   418‚Üí  content: dialogContent,
   419‚Üí  buttons: {
   420‚Üí    import: {
   421‚Üí      label: "Import Traits",
   422‚Üí      callback: async (html) => {
   423‚Üí        const targetPackId = html.find('#target-pack').val();
   424‚Üí        const fileInput = html.find('#trait-file')[0];
   425‚Üí        const overwriteExisting = html.find('#overwrite-existing').prop('checked');
   426‚Üí        
   427‚Üí        if (!fileInput.files.length) {
   428‚Üí          ui.notifications.error("Please select a JSON file to import.");
   429‚Üí          return;
   430‚Üí        }
   431‚Üí        
   432‚Üí        const file = fileInput.files[0];
   433‚Üí        console.log(\`üìÅ Selected file: \${file.name}\`);
   434‚Üí        
   435‚Üí        try {
   436‚Üí          // Read file content
   437‚Üí          const text = await file.text();
   438‚Üí          const data = JSON.parse(text);
   439‚Üí          
   440‚Üí          console.log("üìä Parsed JSON data:", data);
   441‚Üí          
   442‚Üí          if (!data.traits || !Array.isArray(data.traits)) {
   443‚Üí            ui.notifications.error("Invalid file format. Expected JSON with 'traits' array.");
   444‚Üí            return;
   445‚Üí          }
   446‚Üí          
   447‚Üí          const targetPack = game.packs.get(targetPackId);
   448‚Üí          if (!targetPack) {
   449‚Üí            ui.notifications.error(\`Target pack '\${targetPackId}' not found!\`);
   450‚Üí            return;
   451‚Üí          }
   452‚Üí          
   453‚Üí          if (targetPack.locked) {
   454‚Üí            ui.notifications.error(\`Target pack '\${targetPack.metadata.label}' is locked! Please unlock it first.\`);
   455‚Üí            return;
   456‚Üí          }
   457‚Üí          
   458‚Üí          console.log(\`üéØ Importing \${data.traits.length} traits to \${targetPack.metadata.label}...\`);
   459‚Üí          
   460‚Üí          let importedCount = 0;
   461‚Üí          let skippedCount = 0;
   462‚Üí          let updatedCount = 0;
   463‚Üí          
   464‚Üí          for (const traitData of data.traits) {
   465‚Üí            try {
   466‚Üí              // Validate trait data
   467‚Üí              if (!traitData.name || !traitData.color || !traitData.icon) {
   468‚Üí                console.warn("‚ö†Ô∏è Skipping invalid trait:", traitData);
   469‚Üí                skippedCount++;
   470‚Üí                continue;
   471‚Üí              }
   472‚Üí              
   473‚Üí              // Check if trait already exists in the pack
   474‚Üí              const existingItems = await targetPack.getDocuments();
   475‚Üí              const existingTrait = existingItems.find(item => 
   476‚Üí                item.name === traitData.name && item.type === 'trait'
   477‚Üí              );
   478‚Üí              
   479‚Üí              // Prepare item data for creation/update
   480‚Üí              const itemData = {
   481‚Üí                name: traitData.name,
   482‚Üí                type: "trait",
   483‚Üí                img: "icons/svg/item-bag.svg", // Use default image since FontAwesome icons go in system.icon
   484‚Üí                system: {
   485‚Üí                  description: traitData.description || "",
   486‚Üí                  color: traitData.color,
   487‚Üí                  icon: traitData.icon || "fas fa-tag",
   488‚Üí                  localKey: traitData.localKey || "",
   489‚Üí                  tags: Array.isArray(traitData.tags) ? traitData.tags.filter(tag => tag != null) : [],
   490‚Üí                  rarity: traitData.rarity || "common",
   491‚Üí                  effects: traitData.effects || "",
   492‚Üí                  textColor: traitData.textColor || "#000000"
   493‚Üí                }
   494‚Üí              };
   495‚Üí              
   496‚Üí              if (existingTrait) {
   497‚Üí                if (overwriteExisting) {
   498‚Üí                  // Update existing trait - include _id for FoundryVTT v13 compatibility
   499‚Üí                  const updateData = {
   500‚Üí                    _id: existingTrait._id,
   501‚Üí                    ...itemData
   502‚Üí                  };
   503‚Üí                  await existingTrait.update(updateData);
   504‚Üí                  console.log(\`‚úÖ Updated trait: \${traitData.name}\`);
   505‚Üí                  updatedCount++;
   506‚Üí                } else {
   507‚Üí                  console.log(\`‚è≠Ô∏è Skipped existing trait: \${traitData.name}\`);
   508‚Üí                  skippedCount++;
   509‚Üí                }
   510‚Üí              } else {
   511‚Üí                // Create new trait
   512‚Üí                await Item.create(itemData, { pack: targetPackId });
   513‚Üí                console.log(\`‚úÖ Imported trait: \${traitData.name}\`);
   514‚Üí                importedCount++;
   515‚Üí              }
   516‚Üí              
   517‚Üí            } catch (error) {
   518‚Üí              console.error(\`‚ùå Error importing trait '\${traitData.name}':\`, error);
   519‚Üí              skippedCount++;
   520‚Üí            }
   521‚Üí          }
   522‚Üí          
   523‚Üí          // Show summary
   524‚Üí          const summary = [
   525‚Üí            \`üìä Import Summary for \${targetPack.metadata.label}:\`,
   526‚Üí            \`‚Ä¢ \${importedCount} traits imported\`,
   527‚Üí            \`‚Ä¢ \${updatedCount} traits updated\`,
   528‚Üí            \`‚Ä¢ \${skippedCount} traits skipped\`
   529‚Üí          ].join('\\n');
   530‚Üí          
   531‚Üí          console.log(summary);
   532‚Üí          ui.notifications.info(\`Successfully processed \${data.traits.length} traits! Check console for details.\`);
   533‚Üí          
   534‚Üí          // Clear trait provider cache to refresh autocomplete
   535‚Üí          if (game?.avant?.initializationManager) {
   536‚Üí            const traitProvider = game.avant.initializationManager.getService('traitProvider');
   537‚Üí            if (traitProvider && typeof traitProvider.clearCache === 'function') {
   538‚Üí              traitProvider.clearCache();
   539‚Üí              console.log("üîÑ Cleared trait provider cache");
   540‚Üí            }
   541‚Üí          }
   542‚Üí          
   543‚Üí        } catch (error) {
   544‚Üí          console.error("‚ùå Import failed:", error);
   545‚Üí          ui.notifications.error(\`Import failed: \${error.message}\`);
   546‚Üí        }
   547‚Üí      }
   548‚Üí    },
   549‚Üí    cancel: {
   550‚Üí      label: "Cancel"
   551‚Üí    }
   552‚Üí  },
   553‚Üí  default: "import",
   554‚Üí  render: (html) => {
   555‚Üí    console.log("üè∑Ô∏è Import dialog rendered");
   556‚Üí  }
   557‚Üí}).render(true);
   558‚Üí    `,
   559‚Üí    img: "icons/svg/upload.svg",
   560‚Üí    folder: null,
   561‚Üí    sort: 200,
   562‚Üí    flags: {
   563‚Üí      "avant": {
   564‚Üí        "description": "Imports traits from JSON file into the world compendium with file dialog interface",
   565‚Üí        "version": "1.0.0",
   566‚Üí        "category": "trait-management"
   567‚Üí      }
   568‚Üí    }
   569‚Üí  }
   570‚Üí];
   571‚Üí
   572‚Üíconst TRAIT_SEEDS = [
   573‚Üí  {
   574‚Üí    name: "Fire",
   575‚Üí    type: "trait",
   576‚Üí    system: {
   577‚Üí      color: "#FF6B6B",
   578‚Üí      icon: "fas fa-fire",
   579‚Üí      localKey: "AVANT.Trait.Fire",
   580‚Üí      description: "Represents fire-based abilities, damage types, or elemental affinities",
   581‚Üí      category: "general",
   582‚Üí      isActive: false,
   583‚Üí      powerPointCost: 0,
   584‚Üí      uses: { value: 0, max: 0 }
   585‚Üí    },
   586‚Üí    img: "icons/svg/item-bag.svg",
   587‚Üí    sort: 100
   588‚Üí  },
   589‚Üí  {
   590‚Üí    name: "Ice",
   591‚Üí    type: "trait",
   592‚Üí    system: {
   593‚Üí      color: "#4ECDC4",
   594‚Üí      icon: "fas fa-snowflake",
   595‚Üí      localKey: "AVANT.Trait.Ice",
   596‚Üí      description: "Represents ice and cold-based abilities, damage types, or elemental affinities",
   597‚Üí      category: "general",
   598‚Üí      isActive: false,
   599‚Üí      powerPointCost: 0,
   600‚Üí      uses: { value: 0, max: 0 }
   601‚Üí    },
   602‚Üí    img: "icons/svg/item-bag.svg",

   789‚Üí
   790‚Üí/**
   791‚Üí * Create FoundryVTT NeDB compendium pack file (.db format)
   792‚Üí * FoundryVTT will automatically migrate this to LevelDB on first load
   793‚Üí * 
   794‚Üí * @param {string} packPath - Path to the pack file (should end with .db)
   795‚Üí * @param {Array} items - Array of item data to populate
   796‚Üí * @param {Array} folders - Array of folder data to include (Phase C)
   797‚Üí */
   798‚Üíasync function createNeDBPack(packPath, items, folders = []) {
   799‚Üí  console.log(`üî® Creating NeDB pack at: ${packPath}`);
   800‚Üí
   801‚Üí  // Ensure parent directory exists
   802‚Üí  const parentDir = path.dirname(packPath);
   803‚Üí  if (!fs.existsSync(parentDir)) {
   804‚Üí    fs.mkdirSync(parentDir, { recursive: true });
   805‚Üí  }
   806‚Üí
   807‚Üí  // Phase C: Combine folders and items, with folders first for proper loading order
   808‚Üí  const allDocuments = [...folders, ...items];
   809‚Üí
   810‚Üí  // Create NeDB data - each document on its own line as JSON
   811‚Üí  const nedbData = allDocuments.map(item => JSON.stringify(item)).join('\n') + '\n';
   812‚Üí
   813‚Üí  // Write the .db file
   814‚Üí  fs.writeFileSync(packPath, nedbData, 'utf8');
   815‚Üí
   816‚Üí  console.log(`‚úÖ Created NeDB pack with ${items.length} items and ${folders.length} folders`);
   817‚Üí  console.log(`üì¶ File size: ${Buffer.byteLength(nedbData, 'utf8')} bytes`);
   818‚Üí  console.log(`üîÑ FoundryVTT will auto-migrate this to LevelDB on first load`);
   819‚Üí}
   820‚Üí
   821‚Üí/**
   822‚Üí * Generate FoundryVTT-native document IDs for compendium items
   823‚Üí * 
   824‚Üí * UNIFIED ID STRATEGY: Uses FoundryVTT's native randomID() function for ALL items.
   825‚Üí * This ensures:
   826‚Üí * 1. Complete consistency between system and custom traits
   827‚Üí * 2. Multiple traits with same names can coexist
   828‚Üí * 3. Future-proof scalability
   829‚Üí * 4. True database-style unique identifiers
   830‚Üí * 
   831‚Üí * EXAMPLES:
   832‚Üí * - System Fire Trait: "a1b2c3d4e5f6g7h8" 
   833‚Üí * - Custom Fire Trait: "x9y8z7w6v5u4t3s2"
   834‚Üí * - Another Fire Trait: "m1n2o3p4q5r6s7t8"
   835‚Üí * 
   836‚Üí * All different IDs, all can coexist, all work identically.
   837‚Üí * 
   838‚Üí * @returns {string} A native FoundryVTT 16-character alphanumeric ID
   839‚Üí */
   840‚Üífunction generateFoundryId() {
   841‚Üí  // Use FoundryVTT's native random ID generation
   842‚Üí  // This is the same function FoundryVTT uses internally for all documents
   843‚Üí  // Format: 16-character alphanumeric string (e.g., "a1b2c3d4e5f6g7h8")
   844‚Üí
   845‚Üí  // For Node.js build environment, we need to replicate the randomID function
   846‚Üí  // since we don't have access to the full FoundryVTT runtime
   847‚Üí  const chars = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789';
   848‚Üí  let result = '';
   849‚Üí
   850‚Üí  // Generate 16 random characters using crypto-quality randomness
   851‚Üí  for (let i = 0; i < 16; i++) {
   852‚Üí    result += chars.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * chars.length));
   853‚Üí  }
   854‚Üí
   855‚Üí  return result;
   856‚Üí}
   857‚Üí
   858‚Üí/**
   859‚Üí * Generate FoundryVTT item data with proper IDs and validation
   860‚Üí * 
   861‚Üí * @param {Array} seeds - Item seed data
   862‚Üí * @param {string} itemType - The type of items being generated (trait, talent, augment)
   863‚Üí * @returns {Array} FoundryVTT item documents
   864‚Üí */
   865‚Üífunction generateItemDocuments(seeds, itemType = 'trait') {
   866‚Üí  console.log(`üèóÔ∏è Generating ${itemType} documents with validation...`);
   867‚Üí
   868‚Üí  // Generate a consistent user ID for build script (deterministic)
   869‚Üí  const buildUserId = 'AvantBuildScript';
   870‚Üí
   871‚Üí  return seeds.map((seed, index) => {
   872‚Üí    // Validate item data based on type
   873‚Üí    let validatedSystemData;
   874‚Üí    if (itemType === 'talent') {
   875‚Üí      validatedSystemData = validateTalent(seed.system);
   876‚Üí      console.log(`‚úÖ Validated talent: ${seed.name}`, validatedSystemData);
   877‚Üí    } else if (itemType === 'augment') {
   878‚Üí      validatedSystemData = validateAugment(seed.system);
   879‚Üí      console.log(`‚úÖ Validated augment: ${seed.name}`, validatedSystemData);
   880‚Üí    } else {
   881‚Üí      // For traits and other types, use the system data as-is for now
   882‚Üí      validatedSystemData = seed.system;
   883‚Üí    }
   884‚Üí
   885‚Üí    // Use permanent ID from JSON file (Pipeline Phase A compliance)
   886‚Üí    const id = seed._id || generateFoundryId();
   887‚Üí    if (seed._id) {
   888‚Üí      console.log(`üìù Using permanent ID for ${seed.name}: ${id}`);
   889‚Üí    } else {
   890‚Üí      console.log(`üìù Generated ID for ${seed.name}: ${id}`);
   891‚Üí    }
   892‚Üí
   893‚Üí    return {
   894‚Üí      _id: id,
   895‚Üí      name: seed.name,
   896‚Üí      type: seed.type,
   897‚Üí      img: seed.img || 'icons/svg/item-bag.svg',
   898‚Üí      system: validatedSystemData,
   899‚Üí      effects: [],
   900‚Üí      folder: null,
   901‚Üí      sort: seed.sort || ((index + 1) * 100),
   902‚Üí      ownership: {
   903‚Üí        default: 0
   904‚Üí      },
   905‚Üí      flags: {},
   906‚Üí      _stats: {
   907‚Üí        systemId: 'avant',
   908‚Üí        systemVersion: '0.4.0',
   909‚Üí        coreVersion: '13.344',
   910‚Üí        createdTime: 1700000000000, // Fixed timestamp for deterministic builds
   911‚Üí        modifiedTime: 1700000000000,
   912‚Üí        lastModifiedBy: buildUserId
   913‚Üí      }
   914‚Üí    };
   915‚Üí  });
   916‚Üí}
   917‚Üí
   918‚Üí/**
   919‚Üí * Generate FoundryVTT macro data with proper IDs
   920‚Üí * 
   921‚Üí * @param {Array} seeds - Macro seed data
   922‚Üí * @returns {Array} FoundryVTT macro documents
   923‚Üí */
   924‚Üífunction generateMacroDocuments(seeds) {
   925‚Üí  // Generate a consistent user ID for build script (deterministic)
   926‚Üí  const buildUserId = 'AvantBuildScript';
   927‚Üí
   928‚Üí  return seeds.map((seed, index) => {
   929‚Üí    // Use permanent ID from JSON file (Pipeline Phase A compliance)
   930‚Üí    const id = seed._id || generateFoundryId();
   931‚Üí    if (seed._id) {
   932‚Üí      console.log(`üìù Using permanent ID for ${seed.name}: ${id}`);
   933‚Üí    } else {
   934‚Üí      console.log(`üìù Generated ID for ${seed.name}: ${id}`);
   935‚Üí    }
   936‚Üí
   937‚Üí    return {
   938‚Üí      _id: id,
   939‚Üí      name: seed.name,
   940‚Üí      type: seed.type,
   941‚Üí      img: seed.img || 'icons/svg/dice-target.svg',
   942‚Üí      command: seed.command,
   943‚Üí      scope: seed.scope || 'global',
   944‚Üí      folder: seed.folder || null,
   945‚Üí      sort: seed.sort || ((index + 1) * 100),
   946‚Üí      ownership: {
   947‚Üí        default: 3 // OWNER level so players can use the macros
   948‚Üí      },
   949‚Üí      flags: seed.flags || {},
   950‚Üí      _stats: {
   951‚Üí        systemId: 'avant',
   952‚Üí        systemVersion: '0.4.0',
   953‚Üí        coreVersion: '13.344',
   954‚Üí        createdTime: 1700000000000, // Fixed timestamp for deterministic builds
   955‚Üí        modifiedTime: 1700000000000,
   956‚Üí        lastModifiedBy: buildUserId
   957‚Üí      }
   958‚Üí    };
   959‚Üí  });
   960‚Üí}
   961‚Üí
   962‚Üí/**
   963‚Üí * Update system.json to use LevelDB format (folder paths for FoundryVTT v13)
   964‚Üí * 
   965‚Üí * @param {string} systemJsonPath - Path to system.json
   966‚Üí */
   967‚Üífunction updateSystemJsonForLevelDB(systemJsonPath) {
   968‚Üí  console.log('üî® Updating system.json for LevelDB format (FoundryVTT v13)...');
   969‚Üí
   970‚Üí  if (!fs.existsSync(systemJsonPath)) {
   971‚Üí    console.error('‚ùå system.json not found!');
   972‚Üí    return;
   973‚Üí  }
   974‚Üí
   975‚Üí  const systemJson = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(systemJsonPath, 'utf8'));
   976‚Üí
   977‚Üí  // Update pack definitions to use folder paths instead of .db files for v13
   978‚Üí  if (systemJson.packs) {
   979‚Üí    systemJson.packs.forEach(pack => {
   980‚Üí      if (pack.path === './packs/avant-traits.db') {
   981‚Üí        pack.path = './packs/avant-traits';
   982‚Üí        console.log(`‚úÖ Updated pack path for v13: ${pack.path}`);
   983‚Üí      }
   984‚Üí      if (pack.path === './packs/avant-macros.db') {
   985‚Üí        pack.path = './packs/avant-macros';
   986‚Üí        console.log(`‚úÖ Updated pack path for v13: ${pack.path}`);
   987‚Üí      }
   988‚Üí      if (pack.path === './packs/avant-talents.db') {
   989‚Üí        pack.path = './packs/avant-talents';
   990‚Üí        console.log(`‚úÖ Updated pack path for v13: ${pack.path}`);
   991‚Üí      }
   992‚Üí      if (pack.path === './packs/avant-augments.db') {
   993‚Üí        pack.path = './packs/avant-augments';
   994‚Üí        console.log(`‚úÖ Updated pack path for v13: ${pack.path}`);
   995‚Üí      }
   996‚Üí    });
   997‚Üí  }
   998‚Üí
   999‚Üí  // Write updated system.json
  1000‚Üí  fs.writeFileSync(systemJsonPath, JSON.stringify(systemJson, null, 2));
  1001‚Üí  console.log('‚úÖ system.json updated for LevelDB format (v13)');
  1002‚Üí}
  1003‚Üí
  1004‚Üí/**
  1005‚Üí * Main build function
  1006‚Üí */
  1007‚Üíasync function buildPacks() {
  1008‚Üí  try {
  1009‚Üí    console.log('üöÄ Building Avant VTT compendium packs...');
  1010‚Üí
  1011‚Üí    // Define paths
  1012‚Üí    const projectRoot = path.resolve(__dirname, '..');
  1013‚Üí    const distPath = path.join(projectRoot, 'dist');
  1014‚Üí    const packsPath = path.join(distPath, 'packs');
  1015‚Üí    const traitPackPath = path.join(packsPath, 'avant-traits.db');
  1016‚Üí    const macroPackPath = path.join(packsPath, 'avant-macros.db');
  1017‚Üí    const talentPackPath = path.join(packsPath, 'avant-talents.db');
  1018‚Üí    const augmentPackPath = path.join(packsPath, 'avant-augments.db');
  1019‚Üí    const systemJsonPath = path.join(distPath, 'system.json');
  1020‚Üí
  1021‚Üí    console.log(`üìÅ Project root: ${projectRoot}`);
  1022‚Üí    console.log(`üìÅ Dist path: ${distPath}`);
  1023‚Üí    console.log(`üìÅ Pack paths:`);
  1024‚Üí    console.log(`   - Traits: ${traitPackPath}`);
  1025‚Üí    console.log(`   - Macros: ${macroPackPath}`);
  1026‚Üí    console.log(`   - Talents: ${talentPackPath}`);
  1027‚Üí    console.log(`   - Augments: ${augmentPackPath}`);
  1028‚Üí
  1029‚Üí    // Ensure dist directory exists
  1030‚Üí    if (!fs.existsSync(distPath)) {
  1031‚Üí      fs.mkdirSync(distPath, { recursive: true });
  1032‚Üí    }
  1033‚Üí
  1034‚Üí    // Load compendium data from JSON files (with fallback to hardcoded seeds)
  1035‚Üí    console.log('üîÑ Phase 2: Loading compendium data from JSON sources...');
  1036‚Üí    const { traits: TRAIT_SEEDS, talents: TALENT_SEEDS, augments: AUGMENT_SEEDS, macros: MACRO_SEEDS } = 
  1037‚Üí      await loadCompendiumDataWithFallback();
  1038‚Üí
  1039‚Üí    // Phase C: Load folder metadata using enhanced CompendiumLoader
  1040‚Üí    console.log('üîÑ Phase C: Loading folder metadata...');
  1041‚Üí    const loader = new CompendiumLoader();
  1042‚Üí    const loaderResult = await loader.loadAll();
  1043‚Üí    
  1044‚Üí    if (!loaderResult.success) {
  1045‚Üí      console.error('‚ùå Failed to load folder metadata:', loaderResult.errors);
  1046‚Üí      throw new Error('Folder metadata loading failed');
  1047‚Üí    }
  1048‚Üí

  1051‚Üí    const talentFolders = loader.getFoldersByType('talents');

  1053‚Üí    const macroFolders = loader.getFoldersByType('macros');

     2‚Üí
     3‚Üí/**
     4‚Üí * @fileoverview Link Rewriter - Phase D: Link Rewriting
     5‚Üí * @version 1.0.0 - Pipeline Implementation
     6‚Üí * @description Converts @Compendium references to @UUID format for proper cross-referencing
     7‚Üí * @author Avant VTT Team
     8‚Üí */
     9‚Üí
    10‚Üíimport fs from 'fs';
    11‚Üíimport path from 'path';
    12‚Üíimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url';
    13‚Üí
    14‚Üí// ES module compatibility
    15‚Üíconst __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
    16‚Üíconst __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);
    17‚Üí
    18‚Üíinterface CompendiumDocument {
    19‚Üí  _id: string;
    20‚Üí  name: string;
    21‚Üí  type: string;
    22‚Üí  system?: any;
    23‚Üí  [key: string]: any;
    24‚Üí}
    25‚Üí
    26‚Üíinterface LinkRewriteRule {
    27‚Üí  pattern: RegExp;
    28‚Üí  replacement: (match: string, ...args: any[]) => string;
    29‚Üí  description: string;
    30‚Üí}
    31‚Üí
    32‚Üíinterface LinkRewriteResult {
    33‚Üí  success: boolean;
    34‚Üí  originalText: string;
    35‚Üí  rewrittenText: string;
    36‚Üí  changes: LinkChange[];
    37‚Üí  errors: string[];
    38‚Üí}
    39‚Üí
    40‚Üíinterface LinkChange {
    41‚Üí  type: 'compendium-link' | 'trait-reference' | 'item-reference';
    42‚Üí  original: string;
    43‚Üí  rewritten: string;
    44‚Üí  location: string;
    45‚Üí}
