```
    52‚Üí
    53‚Üíexport class LinkRewriter {
    54‚Üí  private packsDirectory: string;
    55‚Üí  private compendiumMap: Map<string, Map<string, CompendiumDocument>> = new Map();
    56‚Üí  private nameToIdMap: Map<string, string> = new Map();
    57‚Üí  private rewriteRules: LinkRewriteRule[] = [];
    58‚Üí  private totalChanges: number = 0;
    59‚Üí  private processedFiles: number = 0;
    60‚Üí
    61‚Üí  constructor(packsDirectory?: string) {
    62‚Üí    this.packsDirectory = packsDirectory || path.join(__dirname, '../../packs');
    63‚Üí    this.initializeRewriteRules();
    64‚Üí  }
    65‚Üí
    66‚Üí  /**
    67‚Üí   * Initialize rewrite rules for different link patterns
    68‚Üí   */
    69‚Üí  private initializeRewriteRules(): void {
    70‚Üí    // Rule 1: @Compendium[pack.name]{label} ‚Üí @UUID[Compendium.pack.name.{id}]{label}
    71‚Üí    this.rewriteRules.push({
    72‚Üí      pattern: /@Compendium\[([^.]+)\.([^.]+)\]\{([^}]+)\}/g,
    73‚Üí      replacement: (match, system, pack, label) => {
    74‚Üí        const id = this.findItemIdByName(pack, label);
    75‚Üí        if (id) {
    76‚Üí          return `@UUID[Compendium.${system}.${pack}.${id}]{${label}}`;
    77‚Üí        }
    78‚Üí        return match; // Return original if no match found
    79‚Üí      },
    80‚Üí      description: 'Convert @Compendium references to @UUID format'
    81‚Üí    });
    82‚Üí
    83‚Üí    // Rule 2: @Compendium[pack.name] ‚Üí @UUID[Compendium.pack.name.{id}]
    84‚Üí    this.rewriteRules.push({
    85‚Üí      pattern: /@Compendium\[([^.]+)\.([^.]+)\]/g,
    86‚Üí      replacement: (match, system, pack) => {
    87‚Üí        // For bare compendium references, we need more context
    88‚Üí        return match; // Keep original for now
    89‚Üí      },
    90‚Üí      description: 'Convert bare @Compendium references (needs context)'
    91‚Üí    });
    92‚Üí
    93‚Üí    // Rule 3: Plain trait names in trait arrays ‚Üí UUID references
    94‚Üí    // This will be handled separately in processTraitReferences
    95‚Üí  }
    96‚Üí
    97‚Üí  /**
    98‚Üí   * Load all compendium data and build name-to-ID mapping
    99‚Üí   */
   100‚Üí  async loadCompendiumData(): Promise<void> {
   101‚Üí    console.log('üîÑ Loading compendium data for link rewriting...');
   102‚Üí    
   103‚Üí    if (!fs.existsSync(this.packsDirectory)) {
   104‚Üí      throw new Error(`Packs directory not found: ${this.packsDirectory}`);
   105‚Üí    }
   106‚Üí
   107‚Üí    // Get all pack directories
   108‚Üí    const packDirs = fs.readdirSync(this.packsDirectory, { withFileTypes: true })
   109‚Üí      .filter(dirent => dirent.isDirectory())
   110‚Üí      .map(dirent => dirent.name);
   111‚Üí
   112‚Üí    console.log(`üì¶ Found pack types: ${packDirs.join(', ')}`);
   113‚Üí
   114‚Üí    // Load each pack
   115‚Üí    for (const packDir of packDirs) {
   116‚Üí      await this.loadPackData(packDir);
   117‚Üí    }
   118‚Üí
   119‚Üí    console.log(`üìä Loaded ${this.nameToIdMap.size} items across ${this.compendiumMap.size} packs`);
   120‚Üí  }
   121‚Üí
   122‚Üí  /**
   123‚Üí   * Load data from a specific pack directory
   124‚Üí   */
   125‚Üí  private async loadPackData(packName: string): Promise<void> {
   126‚Üí    const packPath = path.join(this.packsDirectory, packName);
   127‚Üí    const packMap = new Map<string, CompendiumDocument>();
   128‚Üí
   129‚Üí    try {
   130‚Üí      // Get all JSON files (excluding metadata files)
   131‚Üí      const files = fs.readdirSync(packPath)
   132‚Üí        .filter(file => file.endsWith('.json') && !file.startsWith('_'))
   133‚Üí        .sort();
   134‚Üí
   135‚Üí      console.log(`üìÑ Loading ${packName}: ${files.length} files`);
   136‚Üí
   137‚Üí      for (const file of files) {
   138‚Üí        const filePath = path.join(packPath, file);
   139‚Üí        const fileContent = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
   140‚Üí        const item: CompendiumDocument = JSON.parse(fileContent);
   141‚Üí
   142‚Üí        if (item._id && item.name) {
   143‚Üí          packMap.set(item._id, item);
   144‚Üí          
   145‚Üí          // Build name-to-ID mapping for easy lookup
   146‚Üí          const nameKey = `${packName}.${item.name}`;
   147‚Üí          this.nameToIdMap.set(nameKey, item._id);
   148‚Üí          
   149‚Üí          // Also add just the name for trait references
   150‚Üí          if (item.type === 'trait') {
   151‚Üí            this.nameToIdMap.set(item.name, item._id);
   152‚Üí          }
   153‚Üí        }
   154‚Üí      }
   155‚Üí
   156‚Üí      this.compendiumMap.set(packName, packMap);
   157‚Üí      console.log(`‚úÖ ${packName}: ${packMap.size} items loaded`);
   158‚Üí
   159‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   160‚Üí      console.error(`‚ùå Error loading pack ${packName}: ${error.message}`);
   161‚Üí      throw error;
   162‚Üí    }
   163‚Üí  }
   164‚Üí
   165‚Üí  /**
   166‚Üí   * Find item ID by name in a specific pack
   167‚Üí   */
   168‚Üí  private findItemIdByName(packName: string, itemName: string): string | null {
   169‚Üí    const nameKey = `${packName}.${itemName}`;
   170‚Üí    return this.nameToIdMap.get(nameKey) || this.nameToIdMap.get(itemName) || null;
   171‚Üí  }
   172‚Üí
   173‚Üí  /**
   174‚Üí   * Process all files in the compendium for link rewriting

   176‚Üí  async processAllFiles(options: LinkRewriteOptions = { verbose: false, dryRun: false }): Promise<boolean> {
   177‚Üí    console.log('üîÑ Starting link rewriting process...');
   178‚Üí    
   179‚Üí    if (options.dryRun) {
   180‚Üí      console.log('üß™ DRY RUN MODE: No files will be modified');
   181‚Üí    }
   182‚Üí
   183‚Üí    let allSuccessful = true;
   184‚Üí    this.totalChanges = 0;
   185‚Üí    this.processedFiles = 0;
   186‚Üí
   187‚Üí    // Process each pack
   188‚Üí    for (const packName of this.compendiumMap.keys()) {
   189‚Üí      const packSuccess = await this.processPackFiles(packName, options);
   190‚Üí      if (!packSuccess) {
   191‚Üí        allSuccessful = false;
   192‚Üí      }
   193‚Üí    }
   194‚Üí
   195‚Üí    // Summary
   196‚Üí    console.log('\nüìä Link Rewriting Summary:');
   197‚Üí    console.log(`   üìÅ Files processed: ${this.processedFiles}`);
   198‚Üí    console.log(`   üîÑ Total changes: ${this.totalChanges}`);
   199‚Üí    console.log(`   üéØ Status: ${allSuccessful ? '‚úÖ SUCCESS' : '‚ùå ERRORS'}`);
   200‚Üí
   201‚Üí    return allSuccessful;
   202‚Üí  }
   203‚Üí
   204‚Üí  /**
   205‚Üí   * Process files in a specific pack
   206‚Üí   */
   207‚Üí  private async processPackFiles(packName: string, options: LinkRewriteOptions): Promise<boolean> {
   208‚Üí    const packPath = path.join(this.packsDirectory, packName);
   209‚Üí    let packSuccess = true;
   210‚Üí
   211‚Üí    try {
   212‚Üí      // Get all JSON files (excluding metadata files)
   213‚Üí      const files = fs.readdirSync(packPath)
   214‚Üí        .filter(file => file.endsWith('.json') && !file.startsWith('_'))
   215‚Üí        .sort();
   216‚Üí
   217‚Üí      console.log(`\nüì¶ Processing ${packName}: ${files.length} files`);
   218‚Üí
   219‚Üí      for (const file of files) {
   220‚Üí        const filePath = path.join(packPath, file);
   221‚Üí        const fileSuccess = await this.processFile(filePath, packName, options);
   222‚Üí        
   223‚Üí        if (!fileSuccess) {
   224‚Üí          packSuccess = false;
   225‚Üí        }
   226‚Üí        
   227‚Üí        this.processedFiles++;
   228‚Üí      }
   229‚Üí
   230‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   231‚Üí      console.error(`‚ùå Error processing pack ${packName}: ${error.message}`);
   232‚Üí      packSuccess = false;
   233‚Üí    }
   234‚Üí
   235‚Üí    return packSuccess;
   236‚Üí  }
   237‚Üí
   238‚Üí  /**
   239‚Üí   * Process a single file for link rewriting
   240‚Üí   */
   241‚Üí  private async processFile(filePath: string, packName: string, options: LinkRewriteOptions): Promise<boolean> {
   242‚Üí    const fileName = path.basename(filePath);
   243‚Üí    
   244‚Üí    try {
   245‚Üí      // Read the file
   246‚Üí      const originalContent = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
   247‚Üí      const item: CompendiumDocument = JSON.parse(originalContent);
   248‚Üí
   249‚Üí      // Apply link rewriting
   250‚Üí      const result = this.rewriteItemLinks(item, fileName);
   251‚Üí
   252‚Üí      if (result.changes.length > 0) {
   253‚Üí        this.totalChanges += result.changes.length;
   254‚Üí        
   255‚Üí        if (options.verbose) {
   256‚Üí          console.log(`  üîÑ ${fileName}: ${result.changes.length} changes`);
   257‚Üí          for (const change of result.changes) {
   258‚Üí            console.log(`    ${change.type}: ${change.original} ‚Üí ${change.rewritten}`);
   259‚Üí          }
   260‚Üí        } else {
   261‚Üí          console.log(`  üîÑ ${fileName}: ${result.changes.length} changes`);
   262‚Üí        }
   263‚Üí
   264‚Üí        // Write the modified content (unless dry run)
   265‚Üí        if (!options.dryRun) {
   266‚Üí          const modifiedContent = JSON.stringify(item, null, 2);
   267‚Üí          fs.writeFileSync(filePath, modifiedContent, 'utf8');
   268‚Üí        }
   269‚Üí      } else if (options.verbose) {
   270‚Üí        console.log(`  ‚úÖ ${fileName}: No changes needed`);
   271‚Üí      }
   272‚Üí
   273‚Üí      if (result.errors.length > 0) {
   274‚Üí        console.error(`  ‚ùå ${fileName}: ${result.errors.length} errors`);
   275‚Üí        result.errors.forEach(error => console.error(`    ${error}`));
   276‚Üí        return false;
   277‚Üí      }
   278‚Üí
   279‚Üí      return true;
   280‚Üí
   281‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   282‚Üí      console.error(`‚ùå Error processing file ${fileName}: ${error.message}`);
   283‚Üí      return false;
   284‚Üí    }
   285‚Üí  }
   286‚Üí
   287‚Üí  /**
   288‚Üí   * Rewrite links in a single item
   289‚Üí   */
   290‚Üí  private rewriteItemLinks(item: CompendiumDocument, fileName: string): LinkRewriteResult {
   291‚Üí    const result: LinkRewriteResult = {
   292‚Üí      success: true,
   293‚Üí      originalText: JSON.stringify(item),
   294‚Üí      rewrittenText: '',
   295‚Üí      changes: [],
   296‚Üí      errors: []
   297‚Üí    };
   298‚Üí
   299‚Üí    try {
   300‚Üí      // Process different types of links
   301‚Üí      this.processDescriptionLinks(item, result, fileName);
   302‚Üí      this.processTraitReferences(item, result, fileName);
   303‚Üí      this.processRequirementLinks(item, result, fileName);
   304‚Üí      this.processCommandLinks(item, result, fileName);
   305‚Üí
   306‚Üí      result.rewrittenText = JSON.stringify(item);
   307‚Üí      result.success = result.errors.length === 0;
   308‚Üí
   309‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   310‚Üí      result.success = false;
   311‚Üí      result.errors.push(`Rewriting failed: ${error.message}`);
   312‚Üí    }
   313‚Üí
   314‚Üí    return result;
   315‚Üí  }
   316‚Üí
   317‚Üí  /**
   318‚Üí   * Process links in description fields
   319‚Üí   */
   320‚Üí  private processDescriptionLinks(item: CompendiumDocument, result: LinkRewriteResult, fileName: string): void {
   321‚Üí    if (item.system?.description) {
   322‚Üí      const original = item.system.description;
   323‚Üí      const rewritten = this.applyRewriteRules(original);
   324‚Üí      
   325‚Üí      if (rewritten !== original) {
   326‚Üí        item.system.description = rewritten;
   327‚Üí        result.changes.push({
   328‚Üí          type: 'compendium-link',
   329‚Üí          original: original,
   330‚Üí          rewritten: rewritten,
   331‚Üí          location: `${fileName}.system.description`
   332‚Üí        });
   333‚Üí      }
   334‚Üí    }
   335‚Üí  }
   336‚Üí
   337‚Üí  /**
   338‚Üí   * Process trait references in trait arrays
   339‚Üí   */
   340‚Üí  private processTraitReferences(item: CompendiumDocument, result: LinkRewriteResult, fileName: string): void {
   341‚Üí    if (item.system?.traits && Array.isArray(item.system.traits)) {
   342‚Üí      for (let i = 0; i < item.system.traits.length; i++) {
   343‚Üí        const traitName = item.system.traits[i];
   344‚Üí        
   345‚Üí        if (typeof traitName === 'string' && !traitName.startsWith('@UUID')) {
   346‚Üí          const traitId = this.findItemIdByName('traits', traitName);
   347‚Üí          
   348‚Üí          if (traitId) {
   349‚Üí            const uuidReference = `@UUID[Compendium.avant.avant-traits.${traitId}]{${traitName}}`;
   350‚Üí            item.system.traits[i] = uuidReference;
   351‚Üí            
   352‚Üí            result.changes.push({
   353‚Üí              type: 'trait-reference',
   354‚Üí              original: traitName,
   355‚Üí              rewritten: uuidReference,
   356‚Üí              location: `${fileName}.system.traits[${i}]`
   357‚Üí            });
   358‚Üí          } else {
   359‚Üí            result.errors.push(`Trait not found: ${traitName} in ${fileName}`);
   360‚Üí          }
   361‚Üí        }
   362‚Üí      }
   363‚Üí    }
   364‚Üí  }
   365‚Üí
   366‚Üí  /**
   367‚Üí   * Process links in requirement fields
   368‚Üí   */
   369‚Üí  private processRequirementLinks(item: CompendiumDocument, result: LinkRewriteResult, fileName: string): void {
   370‚Üí    if (item.system?.requirements) {
   371‚Üí      const original = item.system.requirements;
   372‚Üí      const rewritten = this.applyRewriteRules(original);
   373‚Üí      
   374‚Üí      if (rewritten !== original) {
   375‚Üí        item.system.requirements = rewritten;
   376‚Üí        result.changes.push({
   377‚Üí          type: 'compendium-link',
   378‚Üí          original: original,
   379‚Üí          rewritten: rewritten,
   380‚Üí          location: `${fileName}.system.requirements`
   381‚Üí        });
   382‚Üí      }
   383‚Üí    }
   384‚Üí  }
   385‚Üí
   386‚Üí  /**
   387‚Üí   * Process links in macro command fields
   388‚Üí   */
   389‚Üí  private processCommandLinks(item: CompendiumDocument, result: LinkRewriteResult, fileName: string): void {
   390‚Üí    if (item.command) {
   391‚Üí      const original = item.command;
   392‚Üí      const rewritten = this.applyRewriteRules(original);
   393‚Üí      
   394‚Üí      if (rewritten !== original) {
   395‚Üí        item.command = rewritten;
   396‚Üí        result.changes.push({
   397‚Üí          type: 'compendium-link',
   398‚Üí          original: original,
   399‚Üí          rewritten: rewritten,
   400‚Üí          location: `${fileName}.command`
   401‚Üí        });
   402‚Üí      }
   403‚Üí    }
   404‚Üí  }
   405‚Üí
   406‚Üí  /**
   407‚Üí   * Apply all rewrite rules to a text string
   408‚Üí   */
   409‚Üí  private applyRewriteRules(text: string): string {
   410‚Üí    let result = text;
   411‚Üí    
   412‚Üí    for (const rule of this.rewriteRules) {
   413‚Üí      result = result.replace(rule.pattern, rule.replacement);
   414‚Üí    }
   415‚Üí    
   416‚Üí    return result;
   417‚Üí  }
   418‚Üí
   419‚Üí  /**
   420‚Üí   * Validate that all links are properly formatted and point to existing items
   421‚Üí   */
   422‚Üí  async validateLinks(options: LinkRewriteOptions = { verbose: false, dryRun: false }): Promise<boolean> {
   423‚Üí    console.log('üîç Validating link integrity...');
   424‚Üí    
   425‚Üí    let allValid = true;
   426‚Üí    let totalLinks = 0;
   427‚Üí    let brokenLinks = 0;
   428‚Üí
   429‚Üí    // Process each pack
   430‚Üí    for (const packName of this.compendiumMap.keys()) {
   431‚Üí      const packValid = await this.validatePackLinks(packName, options);
   432‚Üí      if (!packValid) {
   433‚Üí        allValid = false;
   434‚Üí      }
   435‚Üí    }
   436‚Üí
   437‚Üí    console.log('\nüìä Link Validation Summary:');
   438‚Üí    console.log(`   üîó Total links: ${totalLinks}`);
   439‚Üí    console.log(`   ‚ùå Broken links: ${brokenLinks}`);
   440‚Üí    console.log(`   üéØ Status: ${allValid ? '‚úÖ ALL VALID' : '‚ùå BROKEN LINKS FOUND'}`);
   441‚Üí
   442‚Üí    return allValid;
   443‚Üí  }
   444‚Üí
   445‚Üí  /**
   446‚Üí   * Validate links in a specific pack
   447‚Üí   */
   448‚Üí  private async validatePackLinks(packName: string, options: LinkRewriteOptions): Promise<boolean> {
   449‚Üí    const packPath = path.join(this.packsDirectory, packName);
   450‚Üí    let packValid = true;
   451‚Üí
   452‚Üí    try {
   453‚Üí      const files = fs.readdirSync(packPath)
   454‚Üí        .filter(file => file.endsWith('.json') && !file.startsWith('_'))
   455‚Üí        .sort();
   456‚Üí
   457‚Üí      console.log(`\nüîç Validating ${packName}: ${files.length} files`);
   458‚Üí
   459‚Üí      for (const file of files) {
   460‚Üí        const filePath = path.join(packPath, file);
   461‚Üí        const fileValid = await this.validateFileLinks(filePath, packName, options);
   462‚Üí        
   463‚Üí        if (!fileValid) {
   464‚Üí          packValid = false;
   465‚Üí        }
   466‚Üí      }
   467‚Üí
   468‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   469‚Üí      console.error(`‚ùå Error validating pack ${packName}: ${error.message}`);
   470‚Üí      packValid = false;
   471‚Üí    }
   472‚Üí
   473‚Üí    return packValid;
   474‚Üí  }
   475‚Üí
   476‚Üí  /**
   477‚Üí   * Validate links in a single file
   478‚Üí   */
   479‚Üí  private async validateFileLinks(filePath: string, packName: string, options: LinkRewriteOptions): Promise<boolean> {
   480‚Üí    const fileName = path.basename(filePath);
   481‚Üí    
   482‚Üí    try {
   483‚Üí      const fileContent = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
   484‚Üí      const item: CompendiumDocument = JSON.parse(fileContent);
   485‚Üí
   486‚Üí      // Find all @UUID references
   487‚Üí      const uuidPattern = /@UUID\[([^\]]+)\]/g;
   488‚Üí      const content = JSON.stringify(item);
   489‚Üí      const matches = Array.from(content.matchAll(uuidPattern));
   490‚Üí
   491‚Üí      let fileValid = true;
   492‚Üí      
   493‚Üí      for (const match of matches) {
   494‚Üí        const uuidPath = match[1];
   495‚Üí        const isValid = this.validateUuidPath(uuidPath);
   496‚Üí        
   497‚Üí        if (!isValid) {
   498‚Üí          console.error(`  ‚ùå ${fileName}: Invalid UUID path: ${uuidPath}`);
   499‚Üí          fileValid = false;
   500‚Üí        } else if (options.verbose) {
   501‚Üí          console.log(`  ‚úÖ ${fileName}: Valid UUID: ${uuidPath}`);
   502‚Üí        }
   503‚Üí      }
   504‚Üí
   505‚Üí      return fileValid;
   506‚Üí
   507‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   508‚Üí      console.error(`‚ùå Error validating file ${fileName}: ${error.message}`);
   509‚Üí      return false;
   510‚Üí    }
   511‚Üí  }
   512‚Üí
   513‚Üí  /**
   514‚Üí   * Validate a UUID path format
   515‚Üí   */
   516‚Üí  private validateUuidPath(uuidPath: string): boolean {
   517‚Üí    // Check if it's a compendium reference
   518‚Üí    if (uuidPath.startsWith('Compendium.')) {
   519‚Üí      const parts = uuidPath.split('.');
   520‚Üí      if (parts.length >= 4) {
   521‚Üí        const [, system, fullPackName, id] = parts;
   522‚Üí        
   523‚Üí        // Map full pack names to directory names
   524‚Üí        const packNameMap: Record<string, string> = {
   525‚Üí          'avant-traits': 'traits',
   526‚Üí          'avant-talents': 'talents',
   527‚Üí          'avant-augments': 'augments',
   528‚Üí          'avant-macros': 'macros'
   529‚Üí        };
   530‚Üí        
   531‚Üí        const packName = packNameMap[fullPackName];
   532‚Üí        if (packName) {
   533‚Üí          // Check if the item exists in our loaded data
   534‚Üí          const packMap = this.compendiumMap.get(packName);
   535‚Üí          if (packMap && packMap.has(id)) {
   536‚Üí            return true;
   537‚Üí          }
   538‚Üí        }
   539‚Üí      }
   540‚Üí    }
   541‚Üí    
   542‚Üí    return false;
   543‚Üí  }
   544‚Üí
   545‚Üí  /**
   546‚Üí   * Get rewriting statistics
   547‚Üí   */
   548‚Üí  getStats(): {
   549‚Üí    totalPacks: number;
   550‚Üí    totalItems: number;
   551‚Üí    totalChanges: number;
   552‚Üí    processedFiles: number;
   553‚Üí    rewriteRules: number;
   554‚Üí  } {
   555‚Üí    return {
   556‚Üí      totalPacks: this.compendiumMap.size,
   557‚Üí      totalItems: this.nameToIdMap.size,
   558‚Üí      totalChanges: this.totalChanges,
   559‚Üí      processedFiles: this.processedFiles,
   560‚Üí      rewriteRules: this.rewriteRules.length
   561‚Üí    };
   562‚Üí  }
   563‚Üí}
   564‚Üí
   565‚Üí// CLI interface
   566‚Üíif (import.meta.url === `file://${process.argv[1]}`) {
   567‚Üí  const args = process.argv.slice(2);
   568‚Üí  const options: LinkRewriteOptions = {
   569‚Üí    verbose: args.includes('--verbose') || args.includes('-v'),
   570‚Üí    dryRun: args.includes('--dry-run') || args.includes('-n'),
   571‚Üí    packsDirectory: args.find(arg => arg.startsWith('--packs='))?.split('=')[1]
   572‚Üí  };
   573‚Üí
   574‚Üí  const rewriter = new LinkRewriter(options.packsDirectory);
   575‚Üí  
   576‚Üí  const command = args[0] || 'rewrite';
   577‚Üí  
   578‚Üí  async function runCommand() {
   579‚Üí    try {
   580‚Üí      await rewriter.loadCompendiumData();
   581‚Üí      
   582‚Üí      switch (command) {
   583‚Üí        case 'rewrite':
   584‚Üí          const success = await rewriter.processAllFiles(options);
   585‚Üí          process.exit(success ? 0 : 1);
   586‚Üí          break;
   587‚Üí          
   588‚Üí        case 'validate':
   589‚Üí          const valid = await rewriter.validateLinks(options);
   590‚Üí          process.exit(valid ? 0 : 1);
   591‚Üí          break;
   592‚Üí          
   593‚Üí        default:
   594‚Üí          console.error(`‚ùå Unknown command: ${command}`);
   595‚Üí          console.log('Available commands: rewrite, validate');
   596‚Üí          process.exit(1);
   597‚Üí      }
   598‚Üí      
   599‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   600‚Üí      console.error('‚ùå Link rewriting failed:', error);
   601‚Üí      process.exit(1);
   602‚Üí    }
   603‚Üí  }
   604‚Üí  
   605‚Üí  runCommand();
   606‚Üí}
   607‚Üí
   608‚Üíexport default LinkRewriter;
```

```
1‚Üí#!/usr/bin/env node
     2‚Üí
     3‚Üí/**
     4‚Üí * @fileoverview Link Rewriter - JavaScript wrapper for build integration
     5‚Üí * @description Wraps the TypeScript LinkRewriter for use in build system
     6‚Üí */
     7‚Üí
     8‚Üíimport { spawn } from 'child_process';
     9‚Üíimport path from 'path';
    10‚Üíimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url';
    11‚Üí
    12‚Üíconst __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
    13‚Üíconst __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);
    14‚Üí
    15‚Üí/**
    16‚Üí * Simple JavaScript wrapper for the TypeScript LinkRewriter
    17‚Üí */
    18‚Üíexport class LinkRewriter {
    19‚Üí  constructor(packsDirectory) {
    20‚Üí    this.packsDirectory = packsDirectory;
    21‚Üí  }
    22‚Üí
    23‚Üí  /**
    24‚Üí   * Validate links using the TypeScript implementation
    25‚Üí   */
    26‚Üí  async validateLinks(options = {}) {
    27‚Üí    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    28‚Üí      const tsxPath = path.join(__dirname, 'link-rewriter.ts');
    29‚Üí      const args = ['validate'];
    30‚Üí      
    31‚Üí      if (options.verbose) args.push('--verbose');
    32‚Üí      if (options.dryRun) args.push('--dry-run');
    33‚Üí      if (this.packsDirectory) args.push(`--packs=${this.packsDirectory}`);
    34‚Üí
    35‚Üí      const process = spawn('tsx', [tsxPath, ...args], {
    36‚Üí        stdio: 'inherit',
    37‚Üí        cwd: path.join(__dirname, '../..')
    38‚Üí      });
    39‚Üí
    40‚Üí      process.on('close', (code) => {
    41‚Üí        resolve(code === 0);
    42‚Üí      });
    43‚Üí
    44‚Üí      process.on('error', (error) => {
    45‚Üí        reject(error);
    46‚Üí      });
    47‚Üí    });
    48‚Üí  }
    49‚Üí
    50‚Üí  /**
    51‚Üí   * Load compendium data - no-op for wrapper
    52‚Üí   */
    53‚Üí  async loadCompendiumData() {
    54‚Üí    // No-op for wrapper - handled by TypeScript implementation
    55‚Üí  }
    56‚Üí}
    57‚Üí
    58‚Üíexport default LinkRewriter;
```

Result:

```
1‚Üí#!/usr/bin/env node
     2‚Üí
     3‚Üí/**
     4‚Üí * @fileoverview Round-trip Extractor - Phase E: Round-trip Validation
     5‚Üí * @version 1.0.0 - Pipeline Implementation
     6‚Üí * @description Extracts data from built compendium packs and validates round-trip consistency
     7‚Üí * @author Avant VTT Team
     8‚Üí */
     9‚Üí
    10‚Üíimport fs from 'fs';
    11‚Üíimport path from 'path';
    12‚Üíimport crypto from 'crypto';
    13‚Üíimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url';
    14‚Üí
    15‚Üí// ES module compatibility
    16‚Üíconst __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
    17‚Üíconst __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);
    18‚Üí
    19‚Üíinterface ExtractedDocument {
    20‚Üí  _id: string;
    21‚Üí  name: string;
    22‚Üí  type: string;
    23‚Üí  category?: string;
    24‚Üí  [key: string]: any;
    25‚Üí}
    26‚Üí
    27‚Üíinterface ExtractionResult {
    28‚Üí  success: boolean;
    29‚Üí  packName: string;
    30‚Üí  documents: ExtractedDocument[];
    31‚Üí  folders: ExtractedDocument[];
    32‚Üí  items: ExtractedDocument[];
    33‚Üí  errors: string[];
    34‚Üí  warnings: string[];
    35‚Üí  metrics: {
    36‚Üí    totalDocuments: number;
    37‚Üí    folderCount: number;
    38‚Üí    itemCount: number;
    39‚Üí    packSizeBytes: number;
    40‚Üí    extractionTimeMs: number;
    41‚Üí  };
    42‚Üí}
    43‚Üí
    44‚Üíinterface RoundTripResult {
    45‚Üí  success: boolean;
    46‚Üí  packName: string;
    47‚Üí  sourcePath: string;
    48‚Üí  builtPath: string;
    49‚Üí  consistency: {
    50‚Üí    itemCount: boolean;
    51‚Üí    folderCount: boolean;
    52‚Üí    idsMatch: boolean;
    53‚Üí    namesMatch: boolean;
    54‚Üí    structureMatch: boolean;
    55‚Üí  };
    56‚Üí  differences: {
    57‚Üí    missingItems: string[];
    58‚Üí    extraItems: string[];
    59‚Üí    modifiedItems: string[];
    60‚Üí    structuralChanges: string[];
    61‚Üí  };
    62‚Üí  hashes: {
    63‚Üí    sourceHash: string;
    64‚Üí    builtHash: string;
    65‚Üí    match: boolean;
    66‚Üí  };
    67‚Üí  errors: string[];
    68‚Üí  warnings: string[];
    69‚Üí}
    70‚Üí
    71‚Üíinterface ExtractionOptions {
    72‚Üí  verbose: boolean;
    73‚Üí  includeFolders: boolean;
    74‚Üí  validateStructure: boolean;
    75‚Üí  computeHashes: boolean;
    76‚Üí  outputDirectory?: string;
    77‚Üí}
    78‚Üí
    79‚Üíexport class RoundTripExtractor {
    80‚Üí  private packsDirectory: string;
    81‚Üí  private distDirectory: string;
    82‚Üí  private extractedData: Map<string, ExtractionResult> = new Map();
    83‚Üí
    84‚Üí  constructor(packsDirectory?: string, distDirectory?: string) {
    85‚Üí    this.packsDirectory = packsDirectory || path.join(__dirname, '../../packs');
    86‚Üí    this.distDirectory = distDirectory || path.join(__dirname, '../../dist/packs');
    87‚Üí  }
    88‚Üí
    89‚Üí  /**
    90‚Üí   * Extract all documents from a specific compendium pack
    91‚Üí   */
    92‚Üí  async extractPack(packName: string, options: ExtractionOptions = { verbose: false, includeFolders: true, validateStructure: true, computeHashes: true }): Promise<ExtractionResult> {
    93‚Üí    const startTime = Date.now();
    94‚Üí    const packPath = path.join(this.distDirectory, `${packName}.db`);
    95‚Üí    
    96‚Üí    console.log(`üîÑ Extracting pack: ${packName}`);
    97‚Üí    console.log(`üìÅ Pack path: ${packPath}`);
    98‚Üí
    99‚Üí    const result: ExtractionResult = {
   100‚Üí      success: false,
   101‚Üí      packName,
   102‚Üí      documents: [],
   103‚Üí      folders: [],
   104‚Üí      items: [],
   105‚Üí      errors: [],
   106‚Üí      warnings: [],
   107‚Üí      metrics: {
   108‚Üí        totalDocuments: 0,
   109‚Üí        folderCount: 0,
   110‚Üí        itemCount: 0,
   111‚Üí        packSizeBytes: 0,
   112‚Üí        extractionTimeMs: 0
   113‚Üí      }
   114‚Üí    };
   115‚Üí
   116‚Üí    try {
   117‚Üí      // Check if pack exists
   118‚Üí      if (!fs.existsSync(packPath)) {
   119‚Üí        throw new Error(`Pack file not found: ${packPath}`);
   120‚Üí      }
   121‚Üí
   122‚Üí      // Get file size
   123‚Üí      const stats = fs.statSync(packPath);
   124‚Üí      result.metrics.packSizeBytes = stats.size;
   125‚Üí
   126‚Üí      // Read the pack file
   127‚Üí      const fileContent = fs.readFileSync(packPath, 'utf8');
   128‚Üí      
   129‚Üí      // Parse each line as a JSON document
   130‚Üí      const lines = fileContent.trim().split('\n');
   131‚Üí      console.log(`üìÑ Found ${lines.length} documents in pack`);
   132‚Üí
   133‚Üí      for (const line of lines) {
   134‚Üí        if (line.trim()) {
   135‚Üí          try {
   136‚Üí            const document: ExtractedDocument = JSON.parse(line);
   137‚Üí            
   138‚Üí            // Validate required fields
   139‚Üí            if (!document._id || !document.name || !document.type) {
   140‚Üí              result.warnings.push(`Document missing required fields: ${JSON.stringify(document)}`);
   141‚Üí              continue;
   142‚Üí            }
   143‚Üí
   144‚Üí            result.documents.push(document);
   145‚Üí
   146‚Üí            // Categorize by type
   147‚Üí            if (document.type === 'Folder') {
   148‚Üí              result.folders.push(document);
   149‚Üí            } else {
   150‚Üí              result.items.push(document);
   151‚Üí            }
   152‚Üí
   153‚Üí            if (options.verbose) {
   154‚Üí              console.log(`  üìù ${document.type}: ${document.name} (${document._id})`);
   155‚Üí            }
   156‚Üí
   157‚Üí          } catch (parseError) {
   158‚Üí            result.errors.push(`Failed to parse document: ${line.substring(0, 100)}...`);
   159‚Üí          }
   160‚Üí        }
   161‚Üí      }
   162‚Üí
   163‚Üí      // Update metrics
   164‚Üí      result.metrics.totalDocuments = result.documents.length;
   165‚Üí      result.metrics.folderCount = result.folders.length;
   166‚Üí      result.metrics.itemCount = result.items.length;
   167‚Üí      result.metrics.extractionTimeMs = Date.now() - startTime;
   168‚Üí
   169‚Üí      // Validate structure if requested
   170‚Üí      if (options.validateStructure) {
   171‚Üí        this.validatePackStructure(result);
   172‚Üí      }
   173‚Üí
   174‚Üí      console.log(`‚úÖ Extracted ${result.metrics.totalDocuments} documents (${result.metrics.folderCount} folders, ${result.metrics.itemCount} items)`);
   175‚Üí      
   176‚Üí      result.success = result.errors.length === 0;
   177‚Üí      return result;
   178‚Üí
   179‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   180‚Üí      result.errors.push(`Extraction failed: ${error.message}`);
   181‚Üí      result.metrics.extractionTimeMs = Date.now() - startTime;
   182‚Üí      console.error(`‚ùå Failed to extract pack ${packName}: ${error.message}`);
   183‚Üí      return result;
   184‚Üí    }
   185‚Üí  }
   186‚Üí
   187‚Üí  /**
   188‚Üí   * Extract all compendium packs
   189‚Üí   */
   190‚Üí  async extractAllPacks(options: ExtractionOptions = { verbose: false, includeFolders: true, validateStructure: true, computeHashes: true }): Promise<boolean> {
   191‚Üí    console.log('üîÑ Starting pack extraction for all compendium packs...');
   192‚Üí    
   193‚Üí    const packNames = ['avant-traits', 'avant-talents', 'avant-augments', 'avant-macros'];
   194‚Üí    let allSuccessful = true;
   195‚Üí
   196‚Üí    this.extractedData.clear();
   197‚Üí
   198‚Üí    for (const packName of packNames) {
   199‚Üí      const result = await this.extractPack(packName, options);
   200‚Üí      this.extractedData.set(packName, result);
   201‚Üí      
   202‚Üí      if (!result.success) {
   203‚Üí        allSuccessful = false;
   204‚Üí      }
   205‚Üí    }
   206‚Üí
   207‚Üí    // Print summary
   208‚Üí    this.printExtractionSummary(options);
   209‚Üí
   210‚Üí    return allSuccessful;
   211‚Üí  }
   212‚Üí
   213‚Üí  /**
   214‚Üí   * Perform round-trip validation by comparing source JSON with extracted data
   215‚Üí   */
   216‚Üí  async validateRoundTrip(options: ExtractionOptions = { verbose: false, includeFolders: true, validateStructure: true, computeHashes: true }): Promise<boolean> {
   217‚Üí    console.log('üîÑ Starting round-trip validation...');
   218‚Üí    
   219‚Üí    const packTypeMap = {
   220‚Üí      'avant-traits': 'traits',
   221‚Üí      'avant-talents': 'talents', 
   222‚Üí      'avant-augments': 'augments',
   223‚Üí      'avant-macros': 'macros'
   224‚Üí    };
   225‚Üí
   226‚Üí    let allValid = true;
   227‚Üí    const results: RoundTripResult[] = [];
   228‚Üí
   229‚Üí    for (const [packName, sourceDir] of Object.entries(packTypeMap)) {
   230‚Üí      const result = await this.validatePackRoundTrip(packName, sourceDir, options);
   231‚Üí      results.push(result);
   232‚Üí      
   233‚Üí      if (!result.success) {
   234‚Üí        allValid = false;
   235‚Üí      }
   236‚Üí    }
   237‚Üí
   238‚Üí    // Print comprehensive summary
   239‚Üí    this.printRoundTripSummary(results, options);
   240‚Üí
   241‚Üí    return allValid;
   242‚Üí  }
   243‚Üí
   244‚Üí  /**
   245‚Üí   * Validate round-trip consistency for a specific pack
   246‚Üí   */
   247‚Üí  private async validatePackRoundTrip(packName: string, sourceDir: string, options: ExtractionOptions): Promise<RoundTripResult> {
   248‚Üí    console.log(`\nüîç Validating round-trip: ${packName} ‚Üî ${sourceDir}`);
   249‚Üí
   250‚Üí    const result: RoundTripResult = {
   251‚Üí      success: false,
   252‚Üí      packName,
   253‚Üí      sourcePath: path.join(this.packsDirectory, sourceDir),
   254‚Üí      builtPath: path.join(this.distDirectory, `${packName}.db`),
   255‚Üí      consistency: {
   256‚Üí        itemCount: false,
   257‚Üí        folderCount: false,
   258‚Üí        idsMatch: false,
   259‚Üí        namesMatch: false,
   260‚Üí        structureMatch: false
   261‚Üí      },
   262‚Üí      differences: {
   263‚Üí        missingItems: [],
   264‚Üí        extraItems: [],
   265‚Üí        modifiedItems: [],
   266‚Üí        structuralChanges: []
   267‚Üí      },
   268‚Üí      hashes: {
   269‚Üí        sourceHash: '',
   270‚Üí        builtHash: '',
   271‚Üí        match: false
   272‚Üí      },
   273‚Üí      errors: [],
   274‚Üí      warnings: []
   275‚Üí    };
   276‚Üí
   277‚Üí    try {
   278‚Üí      // Load source data
   279‚Üí      const sourceData = await this.loadSourceData(sourceDir);
   280‚Üí      
   281‚Üí      // Extract built data
   282‚Üí      const extractedResult = await this.extractPack(packName, options);
   283‚Üí      if (!extractedResult.success) {
   284‚Üí        result.errors.push(...extractedResult.errors);
   285‚Üí        return result;
   286‚Üí      }
   287‚Üí
   288‚Üí      // Compare counts
   289‚Üí      result.consistency.itemCount = sourceData.items.length === extractedResult.items.length;
   290‚Üí      result.consistency.folderCount = sourceData.folders.length === extractedResult.folders.length;
   291‚Üí
   292‚Üí      console.log(`  üìä Source: ${sourceData.items.length} items, ${sourceData.folders.length} folders`);
   293‚Üí      console.log(`  üìä Built: ${extractedResult.items.length} items, ${extractedResult.folders.length} folders`);
   294‚Üí
   295‚Üí      // Compare IDs and names
   296‚Üí      const sourceIds = new Set(sourceData.items.map(item => item._id));
   297‚Üí      const builtIds = new Set(extractedResult.items.map(item => item._id));
   298‚Üí      
   299‚Üí      result.consistency.idsMatch = this.compareSets(sourceIds, builtIds);
   300‚Üí      
   301‚Üí      // Find differences
   302‚Üí      for (const id of sourceIds) {
   303‚Üí        if (!builtIds.has(id)) {
   304‚Üí          const item = sourceData.items.find(item => item._id === id);
   305‚Üí          result.differences.missingItems.push(`${item?.name} (${id})`);
   306‚Üí        }
   307‚Üí      }
   308‚Üí
   309‚Üí      for (const id of builtIds) {
   310‚Üí        if (!sourceIds.has(id)) {
   311‚Üí          const item = extractedResult.items.find(item => item._id === id);
   312‚Üí          result.differences.extraItems.push(`${item?.name} (${id})`);
   313‚Üí        }
   314‚Üí      }
   315‚Üí
   316‚Üí      // Compare item structures
   317‚Üí      for (const sourceItem of sourceData.items) {
   318‚Üí        const builtItem = extractedResult.items.find(item => item._id === sourceItem._id);
   319‚Üí        if (builtItem) {
   320‚Üí          if (!this.compareItemStructure(sourceItem, builtItem)) {
   321‚Üí            result.differences.modifiedItems.push(`${sourceItem.name} (${sourceItem._id})`);
   322‚Üí          }
   323‚Üí        }
   324‚Üí      }
   325‚Üí
   326‚Üí      // Compute hashes if requested
   327‚Üí      if (options.computeHashes) {
   328‚Üí        result.hashes.sourceHash = this.computeDataHash(sourceData);
   329‚Üí        result.hashes.builtHash = this.computeDataHash({
   330‚Üí          items: extractedResult.items,
   331‚Üí          folders: extractedResult.folders
   332‚Üí        });
   333‚Üí        result.hashes.match = result.hashes.sourceHash === result.hashes.builtHash;
   334‚Üí      }
   335‚Üí
   336‚Üí      // Overall consistency
   337‚Üí      result.consistency.structureMatch = result.differences.missingItems.length === 0 && 
   338‚Üí                                        result.differences.extraItems.length === 0 &&
   339‚Üí                                        result.differences.modifiedItems.length === 0;
   340‚Üí
   341‚Üí      result.success = result.consistency.itemCount && 
   342‚Üí                      result.consistency.folderCount && 
   343‚Üí                      result.consistency.idsMatch && 
   344‚Üí                      result.consistency.structureMatch;
   345‚Üí
   346‚Üí      if (result.success) {
   347‚Üí        console.log(`  ‚úÖ Round-trip validation passed`);
   348‚Üí      } else {
   349‚Üí        console.log(`  ‚ùå Round-trip validation failed`);
   350‚Üí      }
   351‚Üí
   352‚Üí      return result;
   353‚Üí
   354‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   355‚Üí      result.errors.push(`Round-trip validation failed: ${error.message}`);
   356‚Üí      console.error(`  ‚ùå Error: ${error.message}`);
   357‚Üí      return result;
   358‚Üí    }
   359‚Üí  }
   360‚Üí
   361‚Üí  /**
   362‚Üí   * Load source data from JSON files
   363‚Üí   */
   364‚Üí  private async loadSourceData(sourceDir: string): Promise<{ items: ExtractedDocument[], folders: ExtractedDocument[] }> {
   365‚Üí    const sourcePath = path.join(this.packsDirectory, sourceDir);
   366‚Üí    const items: ExtractedDocument[] = [];
   367‚Üí    const folders: ExtractedDocument[] = [];
   368‚Üí
   369‚Üí    // Load items
   370‚Üí    const files = fs.readdirSync(sourcePath)
   371‚Üí      .filter(file => file.endsWith('.json') && !file.startsWith('_'))
   372‚Üí      .sort();
   373‚Üí
   374‚Üí    for (const file of files) {
   375‚Üí      const filePath = path.join(sourcePath, file);
   376‚Üí      const content = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
   377‚Üí      const item = JSON.parse(content);
   378‚Üí      items.push(item);
   379‚Üí    }
   380‚Üí
   381‚Üí    // Load folders
   382‚Üí    const foldersPath = path.join(sourcePath, '_folders.json');
   383‚Üí    if (fs.existsSync(foldersPath)) {
   384‚Üí      const foldersContent = fs.readFileSync(foldersPath, 'utf8');
   385‚Üí      const folderData = JSON.parse(foldersContent);
   386‚Üí      folders.push(...folderData);
   387‚Üí    }
   388‚Üí
   389‚Üí    return { items, folders };
   390‚Üí  }
   391‚Üí
   392‚Üí  /**
   393‚Üí   * Compare two sets for equality
   394‚Üí   */
   395‚Üí  private compareSets<T>(set1: Set<T>, set2: Set<T>): boolean {
   396‚Üí    if (set1.size !== set2.size) return false;
   397‚Üí    for (const item of set1) {
   398‚Üí      if (!set2.has(item)) return false;
   399‚Üí    }
   400‚Üí    return true;
   401‚Üí  }
   402‚Üí
   403‚Üí  /**
   404‚Üí   * Compare item structures for consistency
   405‚Üí   */
   406‚Üí  private compareItemStructure(sourceItem: ExtractedDocument, builtItem: ExtractedDocument): boolean {
   407‚Üí    // Compare essential fields
   408‚Üí    const essentialFields = ['_id', 'name', 'type'];
   409‚Üí    for (const field of essentialFields) {
   410‚Üí      if (sourceItem[field] !== builtItem[field]) {
   411‚Üí        return false;
   412‚Üí      }
   413‚Üí    }
   414‚Üí
   415‚Üí    // Compare system data if present
   416‚Üí    if (sourceItem.system && builtItem.system) {
   417‚Üí      // For detailed comparison, we'd need to normalize the structures
   418‚Üí      // For now, just check if both have system data
   419‚Üí      return true;
   420‚Üí    }
   421‚Üí
   422‚Üí    return true;
   423‚Üí  }
   424‚Üí
   425‚Üí  /**
   426‚Üí   * Compute hash for data consistency verification
   427‚Üí   */
   428‚Üí  private computeDataHash(data: { items: ExtractedDocument[], folders: ExtractedDocument[] }): string {
   429‚Üí    // Sort items by ID for consistent hashing
   430‚Üí    const sortedItems = [...data.items].sort((a, b) => a._id.localeCompare(b._id));
   431‚Üí    const sortedFolders = [...data.folders].sort((a, b) => a._id.localeCompare(b._id));
   432‚Üí    
   433‚Üí    // Create normalized data structure
   434‚Üí    const normalized = {
   435‚Üí      items: sortedItems.map(item => ({
   436‚Üí        _id: item._id,
   437‚Üí        name: item.name,
   438‚Üí        type: item.type,
   439‚Üí        category: item.category
   440‚Üí      })),
   441‚Üí      folders: sortedFolders.map(folder => ({
   442‚Üí        _id: folder._id,
   443‚Üí        name: folder.name,
   444‚Üí        type: folder.type,
   445‚Üí        parent: folder.parent
   446‚Üí      }))
   447‚Üí    };
   448‚Üí
   449‚Üí    return crypto.createHash('sha256').update(JSON.stringify(normalized)).digest('hex');
   450‚Üí  }
   451‚Üí
   452‚Üí  /**
   453‚Üí   * Validate pack structure
   454‚Üí   */
   455‚Üí  private validatePackStructure(result: ExtractionResult): void {
   456‚Üí    // Check for required folder structure
   457‚Üí    if (result.folders.length === 0) {
   458‚Üí      result.warnings.push('No folders found in pack');
   459‚Üí    }
   460‚Üí
   461‚Üí    // Check for orphaned items (items without valid folder references)
   462‚Üí    const folderIds = new Set(result.folders.map(f => f._id));
   463‚Üí    
   464‚Üí    for (const item of result.items) {
   465‚Üí      if (item.folder && !folderIds.has(item.folder)) {
   466‚Üí        result.warnings.push(`Item ${item.name} references non-existent folder: ${item.folder}`);
   467‚Üí      }
   468‚Üí    }
   469‚Üí
   470‚Üí    // Check for duplicate IDs
   471‚Üí    const allIds = result.documents.map(doc => doc._id);
   472‚Üí    const uniqueIds = new Set(allIds);
   473‚Üí    
   474‚Üí    if (allIds.length !== uniqueIds.size) {
   475‚Üí      result.errors.push('Duplicate IDs found in pack');
   476‚Üí    }
   477‚Üí  }
   478‚Üí
   479‚Üí  /**
   480‚Üí   * Print extraction summary
   481‚Üí   */
   482‚Üí  private printExtractionSummary(options: ExtractionOptions): void {
   483‚Üí    console.log('\nüìä Extraction Summary:');
   484‚Üí    console.log('‚ïê'.repeat(50));
   485‚Üí
   486‚Üí    let totalDocs = 0;
   487‚Üí    let totalFolders = 0;
   488‚Üí    let totalItems = 0;
   489‚Üí    let totalErrors = 0;
   490‚Üí    let totalWarnings = 0;
   491‚Üí
   492‚Üí    for (const [packName, result] of this.extractedData.entries()) {
   493‚Üí      totalDocs += result.metrics.totalDocuments;
   494‚Üí      totalFolders += result.metrics.folderCount;
   495‚Üí      totalItems += result.metrics.itemCount;
   496‚Üí      totalErrors += result.errors.length;
   497‚Üí      totalWarnings += result.warnings.length;
   498‚Üí
   499‚Üí      const status = result.success ? '‚úÖ' : '‚ùå';
   500‚Üí      console.log(`${status} ${packName}: ${result.metrics.totalDocuments} docs (${result.metrics.folderCount} folders, ${result.metrics.itemCount} items)`);
   501‚Üí      
   502‚Üí      if (result.errors.length > 0) {
   503‚Üí        console.log(`    ‚ùå Errors: ${result.errors.length}`);
   504‚Üí      }
   505‚Üí      
   506‚Üí      if (result.warnings.length > 0) {
   507‚Üí        console.log(`    ‚ö†Ô∏è  Warnings: ${result.warnings.length}`);
   508‚Üí      }
   509‚Üí    }
   510‚Üí
   511‚Üí    console.log(`\nüìà Totals: ${totalDocs} documents, ${totalFolders} folders, ${totalItems} items`);
   512‚Üí    console.log(`üìä Status: ${totalErrors} errors, ${totalWarnings} warnings`);
   513‚Üí  }
   514‚Üí
   515‚Üí  /**
   516‚Üí   * Print round-trip validation summary
   517‚Üí   */
   518‚Üí  private printRoundTripSummary(results: RoundTripResult[], options: ExtractionOptions): void {
   519‚Üí    console.log('\nüîÑ Round-trip Validation Summary:');
   520‚Üí    console.log('‚ïê'.repeat(50));
   521‚Üí
   522‚Üí    let totalValidated = 0;
   523‚Üí    let totalPassed = 0;
   524‚Üí    let totalFailed = 0;
   525‚Üí
   526‚Üí    for (const result of results) {
   527‚Üí      totalValidated++;
   528‚Üí      
   529‚Üí      if (result.success) {
   530‚Üí        totalPassed++;
   531‚Üí        console.log(`‚úÖ ${result.packName}: PASS`);
   532‚Üí      } else {
   533‚Üí        totalFailed++;
   534‚Üí        console.log(`‚ùå ${result.packName}: FAIL`);
   535‚Üí        
   536‚Üí        if (result.differences.missingItems.length > 0) {
   537‚Üí          console.log(`    Missing: ${result.differences.missingItems.join(', ')}`);
   538‚Üí        }
   539‚Üí        
   540‚Üí        if (result.differences.extraItems.length > 0) {
   541‚Üí          console.log(`    Extra: ${result.differences.extraItems.join(', ')}`);
   542‚Üí        }
   543‚Üí        
   544‚Üí        if (result.differences.modifiedItems.length > 0) {
   545‚Üí          console.log(`    Modified: ${result.differences.modifiedItems.join(', ')}`);
   546‚Üí        }
   547‚Üí      }
   548‚Üí
   549‚Üí      if (options.computeHashes) {
   550‚Üí        const hashStatus = result.hashes.match ? '‚úÖ' : '‚ùå';
   551‚Üí        console.log(`    ${hashStatus} Hash: ${result.hashes.sourceHash.substring(0, 16)}...`);
   552‚Üí      }
   553‚Üí    }
   554‚Üí
   555‚Üí    console.log(`\nüìä Summary: ${totalPassed}/${totalValidated} packs passed validation`);
   556‚Üí    console.log(`üéØ Overall Status: ${totalFailed === 0 ? '‚úÖ PASS' : '‚ùå FAIL'}`);
   557‚Üí  }
   558‚Üí
   559‚Üí  /**
   560‚Üí   * Export extracted data to JSON files
   561‚Üí   */
   562‚Üí  async exportExtractedData(outputDir: string, options: ExtractionOptions = { verbose: false, includeFolders: true, validateStructure: true, computeHashes: true }): Promise<void> {
   563‚Üí    console.log(`üì§ Exporting extracted data to: ${outputDir}`);
   564‚Üí    
   565‚Üí    // Ensure output directory exists
   566‚Üí    if (!fs.existsSync(outputDir)) {
   567‚Üí      fs.mkdirSync(outputDir, { recursive: true });
   568‚Üí    }
   569‚Üí
   570‚Üí    for (const [packName, result] of this.extractedData.entries()) {
   571‚Üí      const outputPath = path.join(outputDir, `${packName}-extracted.json`);
   572‚Üí      
   573‚Üí      const exportData = {
   574‚Üí        metadata: {
   575‚Üí          packName: result.packName,
   576‚Üí          extractedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
   577‚Üí          success: result.success,
   578‚Üí          metrics: result.metrics
   579‚Üí        },
   580‚Üí        folders: result.folders,
   581‚Üí        items: result.items,
   582‚Üí        errors: result.errors,
   583‚Üí        warnings: result.warnings
   584‚Üí      };
   585‚Üí
   586‚Üí      fs.writeFileSync(outputPath, JSON.stringify(exportData, null, 2));
   587‚Üí      console.log(`  ‚úÖ Exported ${packName} to ${outputPath}`);
   588‚Üí    }
   589‚Üí  }
   590‚Üí
   591‚Üí  /**
   592‚Üí   * Get extraction statistics
   593‚Üí   */
   594‚Üí  getStats(): {
   595‚Üí    totalPacks: number;
   596‚Üí    totalDocuments: number;
   597‚Üí    totalFolders: number;
   598‚Üí    totalItems: number;
   599‚Üí    totalErrors: number;
   600‚Üí    totalWarnings: number;
   601‚Üí    averageExtractionTime: number;
   602‚Üí  } {
   603‚Üí    const results = Array.from(this.extractedData.values());
   604‚Üí    
   605‚Üí    return {
   606‚Üí      totalPacks: results.length,
   607‚Üí      totalDocuments: results.reduce((sum, r) => sum + r.metrics.totalDocuments, 0),
   608‚Üí      totalFolders: results.reduce((sum, r) => sum + r.metrics.folderCount, 0),
   609‚Üí      totalItems: results.reduce((sum, r) => sum + r.metrics.itemCount, 0),
   610‚Üí      totalErrors: results.reduce((sum, r) => sum + r.errors.length, 0),
   611‚Üí      totalWarnings: results.reduce((sum, r) => sum + r.warnings.length, 0),
   612‚Üí      averageExtractionTime: results.reduce((sum, r) => sum + r.metrics.extractionTimeMs, 0) / results.length
   613‚Üí    };
   614‚Üí  }
   615‚Üí}
   616‚Üí
   617‚Üí// CLI interface
   618‚Üíif (import.meta.url === `file://${process.argv[1]}`) {
   619‚Üí  const args = process.argv.slice(2);
   620‚Üí  const options: ExtractionOptions = {
   621‚Üí    verbose: args.includes('--verbose') || args.includes('-v'),
   622‚Üí    includeFolders: !args.includes('--no-folders'),
   623‚Üí    validateStructure: !args.includes('--no-validation'),
   624‚Üí    computeHashes: !args.includes('--no-hashes'),
   625‚Üí    outputDirectory: args.find(arg => arg.startsWith('--output='))?.split('=')[1]
   626‚Üí  };
   627‚Üí
   628‚Üí  const extractor = new RoundTripExtractor();
   629‚Üí  const command = args[0] || 'validate';
   630‚Üí  
   631‚Üí  async function runCommand() {
   632‚Üí    try {
   633‚Üí      switch (command) {
   634‚Üí        case 'extract':
   635‚Üí          const extractSuccess = await extractor.extractAllPacks(options);
   636‚Üí          
   637‚Üí          if (options.outputDirectory) {
   638‚Üí            await extractor.exportExtractedData(options.outputDirectory, options);
   639‚Üí          }
   640‚Üí          
   641‚Üí          process.exit(extractSuccess ? 0 : 1);
   642‚Üí          break;
   643‚Üí          
   644‚Üí        case 'validate':
   645‚Üí        case 'roundtrip':
   646‚Üí          const validateSuccess = await extractor.validateRoundTrip(options);
   647‚Üí          process.exit(validateSuccess ? 0 : 1);
   648‚Üí          break;
   649‚Üí          
   650‚Üí        default:
   651‚Üí          console.error(`‚ùå Unknown command: ${command}`);
   652‚Üí          console.log('Available commands: extract, validate, roundtrip');
   653‚Üí          process.exit(1);
   654‚Üí      }
   655‚Üí      
   656‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   657‚Üí      console.error('‚ùå Round-trip extraction failed:', error);
   658‚Üí      process.exit(1);
   659‚Üí    }
   660‚Üí  }
   661‚Üí  
   662‚Üí  runCommand();
   663‚Üí}
   664‚Üí
   665‚Üíexport default RoundTripExtractor;
```

```
     7‚Üí

     9‚Üíimport path from 'path';
    10‚Üíimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url';
    11‚Üí
    12‚Üíconst __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
    13‚Üíconst __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);
    14‚Üí
    15‚Üí/**
    16‚Üí * Simple JavaScript wrapper for the TypeScript RoundTripExtractor
    17‚Üí */
    18‚Üíexport class RoundTripExtractor {
    19‚Üí  constructor(packsDirectory, distDirectory) {
    20‚Üí    this.packsDirectory = packsDirectory;
    21‚Üí    this.distDirectory = distDirectory;
    22‚Üí  }
    23‚Üí
    24‚Üí  /**
    25‚Üí   * Validate round-trip using the TypeScript implementation
    26‚Üí   */
    27‚Üí  async validateRoundTrip(options = {}) {
    28‚Üí    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    29‚Üí      const tsxPath = path.join(__dirname, 'round-trip-extractor.ts');
    30‚Üí      const args = ['validate'];
    31‚Üí      
    32‚Üí      if (options.verbose) args.push('--verbose');
    33‚Üí      if (options.outputDirectory) args.push(`--output=${options.outputDirectory}`);
    34‚Üí      if (this.packsDirectory) args.push(`--packs=${this.packsDirectory}`);
    35‚Üí
    36‚Üí      const process = spawn('tsx', [tsxPath, ...args], {
    37‚Üí        stdio: 'inherit',
    38‚Üí        cwd: path.join(__dirname, '../..')
    39‚Üí      });
    40‚Üí
    41‚Üí      process.on('close', (code) => {
    42‚Üí        resolve(code === 0);
    43‚Üí      });
    44‚Üí
    45‚Üí      process.on('error', (error) => {
    46‚Üí        reject(error);
    47‚Üí      });
    48‚Üí    });
    49‚Üí  }
    50‚Üí

    65‚Üí      });
```

```
    10‚Üí
    11‚Üí// Environment-based logging configuration

    13‚Üíconst LOG_LEVEL = process.env.AVANT_LOG_LEVEL || 'info'; // error, warn, info, debug
    14‚Üí
    15‚Üí/**
    16‚Üí * Enhanced logger with multiple levels and debugging support

    18‚Üíclass CompendiumLogger {
    19‚Üí  constructor(component = 'CompendiumIntegration') {
    20‚Üí    this.component = component;
    21‚Üí    this.levels = {
    22‚Üí      error: 0,
    23‚Üí      warn: 1, 
    24‚Üí      info: 2,
    25‚Üí      debug: 3
    26‚Üí    };
    27‚Üí    this.currentLevel = this.levels[LOG_LEVEL] || this.levels.info;
    28‚Üí  }
    29‚Üí
    30‚Üí  _shouldLog(level) {
    31‚Üí    return this.levels[level] <= this.currentLevel;
    32‚Üí  }
    33‚Üí
    34‚Üí  _formatMessage(level, message, data = null) {
    35‚Üí    const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();

    37‚Üí      error: '‚ùå',
    38‚Üí      warn: '‚ö†Ô∏è',

    50‚Üí  }
    51‚Üí
    52‚Üí  error(message, data = null) {

    55‚Üí    }
    56‚Üí  }
    57‚Üí
    58‚Üí  warn(message, data = null) {

    61‚Üí    }
    62‚Üí  }
    63‚Üí
    64‚Üí  info(message, data = null) {
    65‚Üí    if (this._shouldLog('info')) {
    66‚Üí      console.log(this._formatMessage('info', message, data));
    67‚Üí    }
    68‚Üí  }
    69‚Üí
    70‚Üí  debug(message, data = null) {

    73‚Üí    }
    74‚Üí  }

    92‚Üí  }
    93‚Üí}

   271‚Üí      nodeVersion: process.version,

   287‚Üí    const loader = new CompendiumLoader();
   288‚Üí    const result = await loader.loadAll();
   289‚Üí    const loadTime = Date.now() - startTime;
   290‚Üí    
   291‚Üí    diagnostics.configuration.packsDirectory = loader.packsDirectory;
   292‚Üí    diagnostics.configuration.compendiumStatus = result.success ? 'healthy' : 'degraded';
   293‚Üí    diagnostics.performance.loadTimeMs = loadTime;
   294‚Üí    diagnostics.lastLoadResult = {
   295‚Üí      success: result.success,
   296‚Üí      stats: loader.getStats(),
   297‚Üí      errorCount: result.errors?.length || 0,
   298‚Üí      warningCount: result.warnings?.length || 0
   299‚Üí    };
   300‚Üí    
   301‚Üí    logger.info('Diagnostics collected successfully');
   302‚Üí    
   303‚Üí  } catch (error) {
   304‚Üí    diagnostics.configuration.compendiumStatus = 'failed';
   305‚Üí    diagnostics.lastLoadResult = {
   306‚Üí      error: error.message,
   307‚Üí      stack: DEBUG_MODE ? error.stack : undefined
   308‚Üí    };
   309‚Üí    
   310‚Üí    logger.warn('Error during diagnostics collection', error);
   311‚Üí  }
   312‚Üí  
   313‚Üí  return diagnostics;
   314‚Üí}

   316‚Üí/**
```
