   319‚Üíexport async function validateSystemHealth() {
   320‚Üí  logger.info('Running system health validation...');
   321‚Üí  
   322‚Üí  const issues = [];
   323‚Üí  const warnings = [];
   324‚Üí  
   325‚Üí  try {
   326‚Üí    // Test basic loading
   327‚Üí    const loader = new CompendiumLoader();
   328‚Üí    const result = await loader.loadAll();
   329‚Üí    
   330‚Üí    if (!result.success) {
   331‚Üí      issues.push(`Compendium loading failed: ${result.errors?.[0] || 'Unknown error'}`);
   332‚Üí    }
   333‚Üí    
   334‚Üí    const stats = loader.getStats();
   335‚Üí    
   336‚Üí    // Check for minimum content requirements
   337‚Üí    if (stats.itemsByType.traits < 20) {
   338‚Üí      warnings.push(`Low trait count: ${stats.itemsByType.traits} (recommended: ‚â•20)`);
   339‚Üí    }
   340‚Üí    
   341‚Üí    if (stats.itemsByType.talents < 15) {
   342‚Üí      warnings.push(`Low talent count: ${stats.itemsByType.talents} (recommended: ‚â•15)`);
   343‚Üí    }
   344‚Üí    
   345‚Üí    if (stats.itemsByType.augments < 15) {
   346‚Üí      warnings.push(`Low augment count: ${stats.itemsByType.augments} (recommended: ‚â•15)`);
   347‚Üí    }
   348‚Üí    
   349‚Üí    if (stats.itemsByType.macros < 10) {
   350‚Üí      warnings.push(`Low macro count: ${stats.itemsByType.macros} (recommended: ‚â•10)`);
   351‚Üí    }
   352‚Üí    
   353‚Üí    // Check error/warning ratios
   354‚Üí    const errorRate = stats.errorCount / stats.totalItems;
   355‚Üí    if (errorRate > 0.1) { // More than 10% error rate
   356‚Üí      issues.push(`High error rate: ${Math.round(errorRate * 100)}%`);
   357‚Üí    }
   358‚Üí    
   359‚Üí    logger.info(`Health validation complete: ${issues.length} issues, ${warnings.length} warnings`);
   360‚Üí    
   361‚Üí    return {
   362‚Üí      healthy: issues.length === 0,
   363‚Üí      issues,
   364‚Üí      warnings,
   365‚Üí      stats
   366‚Üí    };
   367‚Üí    
   368‚Üí  } catch (error) {
   369‚Üí    logger.error('Health validation failed', error);
   370‚Üí    return {
   371‚Üí      healthy: false,
   372‚Üí      issues: [`System validation failed: ${error.message}`],
   373‚Üí      warnings: [],
   374‚Üí      stats: null
   375‚Üí    };
   376‚Üí  }
   377‚Üí}
   378‚Üí
   379‚Üíexport default {
   380‚Üí  loadCompendiumData,
   381‚Üí  loadCompendiumDataWithFallback,
   382‚Üí  demonstrateIntegration,
   383‚Üí  setDebugMode,
   384‚Üí  getDiagnostics,
   385‚Üí  validateSystemHealth,
   386‚Üí  CompendiumLogger
   387‚Üí};
```

Result:

```
1‚Üí#!/usr/bin/env node
     2‚Üí
     3‚Üí/**
     4‚Üí * @fileoverview Compendium Loader - JSON-First Architecture
     5‚Üí * @version 1.3.0 - Phase C Folder Support
     6‚Üí * @description Generic loader supporting both monolithic and split JSON formats with folder metadata
     7‚Üí * @author Avant VTT Team
     8‚Üí */
     9‚Üí
    10‚Üíimport fs from 'fs';
    11‚Üíimport path from 'path';
    12‚Üíimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url';
    13‚Üí
    14‚Üí// ES module compatibility
    15‚Üíconst __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
    16‚Üíconst __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);
    17‚Üí
    18‚Üí/**
    19‚Üí * CompendiumLoader - Loads and validates JSON compendium sources
    20‚Üí */
    21‚Üíexport class CompendiumLoader {
    22‚Üí  constructor(packsDirectory = null) {
    23‚Üí    // Default to project root packs/ directory
    24‚Üí    this.packsDirectory = packsDirectory || path.join(__dirname, '../../packs');
    25‚Üí    this.loadedData = new Map();
    26‚Üí    this.folders = new Map(); // Phase C: Store folder metadata
    27‚Üí    this.errors = [];
    28‚Üí    this.warnings = [];
    29‚Üí    this.validationSummary = {
    30‚Üí      totalFiles: 0,
    31‚Üí      successfulFiles: 0,
    32‚Üí      errorFiles: 0,
    33‚Üí      warningFiles: 0
    34‚Üí    };
    35‚Üí  }
    36‚Üí
    37‚Üí  /**
    38‚Üí   * Load all compendium data from the packs directory
    39‚Üí   * @returns {Promise<{success: boolean, data: Map, errors: Array}>}
    40‚Üí   */
    41‚Üí  async loadAll() {
    42‚Üí    this.loadedData.clear();
    43‚Üí    this.folders.clear(); // Phase C: Clear folder metadata
    44‚Üí    this.errors = [];
    45‚Üí    this.warnings = [];
    46‚Üí    this.validationSummary = {
    47‚Üí      totalFiles: 0,
    48‚Üí      successfulFiles: 0,
    49‚Üí      errorFiles: 0,
    50‚Üí      warningFiles: 0
    51‚Üí    };
    52‚Üí
    53‚Üí    console.log('üîÑ CompendiumLoader: Starting JSON compendium load...');
    54‚Üí    console.log(`üìÅ Packs directory: ${this.packsDirectory}`);
    55‚Üí
    56‚Üí    try {
    57‚Üí      // Verify packs directory exists
    58‚Üí      if (!fs.existsSync(this.packsDirectory)) {
    59‚Üí        throw new Error(`Packs directory not found: ${this.packsDirectory}`);
    60‚Üí      }
    61‚Üí
    62‚Üí      // Get all subdirectories (traits, talents, augments, macros)
    63‚Üí      const subdirs = fs.readdirSync(this.packsDirectory, { withFileTypes: true })
    64‚Üí        .filter(dirent => dirent.isDirectory())
    65‚Üí        .map(dirent => dirent.name);
    66‚Üí
    67‚Üí      console.log(`üìã Found compendium types: ${subdirs.join(', ')}`);
    68‚Üí
    69‚Üí      // Load each type
    70‚Üí      for (const subdir of subdirs) {
    71‚Üí        await this.loadCompendiumType(subdir);
    72‚Üí      }
    73‚Üí
    74‚Üí      const totalItems = Array.from(this.loadedData.values())
    75‚Üí        .reduce((sum, items) => sum + items.length, 0);
    76‚Üí
    77‚Üí      // Enhanced reporting
    78‚Üí      this.printValidationSummary();
    79‚Üí
    80‚Üí      if (this.errors.length > 0) {
    81‚Üí        console.warn(`‚ö†Ô∏è CompendiumLoader: Loaded ${totalItems} items with ${this.errors.length} errors and ${this.warnings.length} warnings`);
    82‚Üí        return { 
    83‚Üí          success: false, 
    84‚Üí          data: this.loadedData, 
    85‚Üí          folders: this.folders, // Phase C: Include folder metadata
    86‚Üí          errors: this.errors,
    87‚Üí          warnings: this.warnings,
    88‚Üí          summary: this.validationSummary 
    89‚Üí        };
    90‚Üí      }
    91‚Üí
    92‚Üí      console.log(`‚úÖ CompendiumLoader: Successfully loaded ${totalItems} items with ${this.warnings.length} warnings`);
    93‚Üí      return { 
    94‚Üí        success: true, 
    95‚Üí        data: this.loadedData, 
    96‚Üí        folders: this.folders, // Phase C: Include folder metadata
    97‚Üí        errors: [],
    98‚Üí        warnings: this.warnings,
    99‚Üí        summary: this.validationSummary 
   100‚Üí      };
   101‚Üí
   102‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   103‚Üí      const errorMessage = `Failed to load compendium data: ${error.message}`;
   104‚Üí      this.errors.push(errorMessage);
   105‚Üí      console.error(`‚ùå CompendiumLoader: ${errorMessage}`);
   106‚Üí      return { success: false, data: this.loadedData, folders: this.folders, errors: this.errors };
   107‚Üí    }
   108‚Üí  }
   109‚Üí
   110‚Üí  /**
   111‚Üí   * Load all JSON files from a specific compendium type directory
   112‚Üí   * Supports both monolithic arrays and individual file formats (Phase B)
   113‚Üí   * Also loads folder metadata (Phase C)
   114‚Üí   * @param {string} typeName - The compendium type (traits, talents, etc.)
   115‚Üí   */
   116‚Üí  async loadCompendiumType(typeName) {
   117‚Üí    const typeDir = path.join(this.packsDirectory, typeName);
   118‚Üí    
   119‚Üí    try {
   120‚Üí      // Phase C: Load folder metadata first
   121‚Üí      await this.loadFolderMetadata(typeName, typeDir);
   122‚Üí      // Get all JSON files in the directory (excluding metadata files)
   123‚Üí      const files = fs.readdirSync(typeDir)
   124‚Üí        .filter(file => file.endsWith('.json'))
   125‚Üí        .filter(file => !file.startsWith('_')) // Skip _folders.json etc. (Phase C support)
   126‚Üí        .sort(); // Sort for consistent ordering
   127‚Üí
   128‚Üí      console.log(`üìÑ Loading ${typeName}: ${files.length} JSON files`);
   129‚Üí
   130‚Üí      const items = [];
   131‚Üí      
   132‚Üí      for (const file of files) {
   133‚Üí        const filePath = path.join(typeDir, file);
   134‚Üí        this.validationSummary.totalFiles++;
   135‚Üí        
   136‚Üí        try {
   137‚Üí          const loadedItems = await this.loadJsonFile(filePath, typeName);
   138‚Üí          if (loadedItems) {
   139‚Üí            // Handle both single items and arrays (hybrid support)
   140‚Üí            if (Array.isArray(loadedItems)) {
   141‚Üí              // Monolithic format: array of items
   142‚Üí              items.push(...loadedItems);
   143‚Üí              this.validationSummary.successfulFiles++;
   144‚Üí              console.log(`  ‚úÖ Loaded: ${file} (${loadedItems.length} items from monolithic file)`);
   145‚Üí            } else {
   146‚Üí              // Split format: single item per file
   147‚Üí              items.push(loadedItems);
   148‚Üí              this.validationSummary.successfulFiles++;
   149‚Üí              console.log(`  ‚úÖ Loaded: ${file} (${loadedItems.name})`);
   150‚Üí            }
   151‚Üí          }
   152‚Üí        } catch (error) {
   153‚Üí          this.validationSummary.errorFiles++;
   154‚Üí          const errorMessage = `Error loading ${file}: ${error.message}`;
   155‚Üí          this.errors.push(errorMessage);
   156‚Üí          console.error(`  ‚ùå ${errorMessage}`);
   157‚Üí          
   158‚Üí          // Add detailed error context for debugging
   159‚Üí          this.errors.push(`    üìç File: ${filePath}`);
   160‚Üí          this.errors.push(`    üîç Error Type: ${error.name || 'Unknown'}`);
   161‚Üí        }
   162‚Üí      }
   163‚Üí
   164‚Üí      // Store loaded items for this type
   165‚Üí      this.loadedData.set(typeName, items);
   166‚Üí      console.log(`üì¶ ${typeName}: ${items.length} items loaded successfully`);
   167‚Üí
   168‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   169‚Üí      const errorMessage = `Failed to read directory ${typeDir}: ${error.message}`;
   170‚Üí      this.errors.push(errorMessage);
   171‚Üí      console.error(`‚ùå ${errorMessage}`);
   172‚Üí    }
   173‚Üí  }
   174‚Üí
   175‚Üí  /**
   176‚Üí   * Load folder metadata for a compendium type (Phase C)
   177‚Üí   * @param {string} typeName - The compendium type (traits, talents, etc.)
   178‚Üí   * @param {string} typeDir - Directory path for the type
   179‚Üí   */
   180‚Üí  async loadFolderMetadata(typeName, typeDir) {
   181‚Üí    const foldersPath = path.join(typeDir, '_folders.json');
   182‚Üí    
   183‚Üí    try {
   184‚Üí      if (fs.existsSync(foldersPath)) {
   185‚Üí        const folderContent = fs.readFileSync(foldersPath, 'utf8');
   186‚Üí        const folders = JSON.parse(folderContent);
   187‚Üí        
   188‚Üí        if (Array.isArray(folders)) {
   189‚Üí          this.folders.set(typeName, folders);
   190‚Üí          console.log(`üìÅ Loaded ${folders.length} folder(s) for ${typeName}`);
   191‚Üí        } else {
   192‚Üí          this.addWarning(`Invalid _folders.json format for ${typeName}: expected array`);
   193‚Üí        }
   194‚Üí      } else {
   195‚Üí        console.log(`üìÅ No folder metadata found for ${typeName} (using flat structure)`);
   196‚Üí        this.folders.set(typeName, []);
   197‚Üí      }
   198‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   199‚Üí      this.addWarning(`Failed to load folder metadata for ${typeName}: ${error.message}`);
   200‚Üí      this.folders.set(typeName, []);
   201‚Üí    }
   202‚Üí  }
   203‚Üí
   204‚Üí  /**
   205‚Üí   * Load and validate a single JSON file
   206‚Üí   * @param {string} filePath - Path to the JSON file
   207‚Üí   * @param {string} expectedType - Expected compendium type
   208‚Üí   * @returns {Promise<Object|null>} Parsed and validated item data
   209‚Üí   */
   210‚Üí  async loadJsonFile(filePath, expectedType) {
   211‚Üí    const fileName = path.basename(filePath);
   212‚Üí    
   213‚Üí    try {
   214‚Üí      // Check file size (warn if unusually large)
   215‚Üí      const stats = fs.statSync(filePath);
   216‚Üí      if (stats.size > 50000) { // 50KB threshold
   217‚Üí        this.addWarning(`Large file detected: ${fileName} (${Math.round(stats.size / 1024)}KB)`);
   218‚Üí      }
   219‚Üí
   220‚Üí      // Read and parse JSON
   221‚Üí      const fileContent = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
   222‚Üí      
   223‚Üí      // Check for empty files
   224‚Üí      if (!fileContent.trim()) {
   225‚Üí        throw new Error(`Empty file: ${fileName}`);
   226‚Üí      }
   227‚Üí
   228‚Üí      const itemData = JSON.parse(fileContent);
   229‚Üí
   230‚Üí      // Enhanced validation
   231‚Üí      this.validateItemStructure(itemData, filePath, expectedType);
   232‚Üí      this.performSemanticValidation(itemData, fileName, expectedType);
   233‚Üí
   234‚Üí      return itemData;
   235‚Üí
   236‚Üí    } catch (error) {
   237‚Üí      if (error.name === 'SyntaxError') {
   238‚Üí        throw new Error(`Invalid JSON syntax in ${fileName}: ${error.message}`);
   239‚Üí      } else if (error.code === 'ENOENT') {
   240‚Üí        throw new Error(`File not found: ${fileName}`);
   241‚Üí      } else if (error.code === 'EACCES') {
   242‚Üí        throw new Error(`Permission denied reading: ${fileName}`);
   243‚Üí      }
   244‚Üí      throw error;
   245‚Üí    }
   246‚Üí  }
   247‚Üí
   248‚Üí  /**
   249‚Üí   * Validate basic item structure
   250‚Üí   * @param {Object} item - Item data to validate
   251‚Üí   * @param {string} filePath - File path for error reporting
   252‚Üí   * @param {string} expectedType - Expected compendium type
   253‚Üí   */
   254‚Üí  validateItemStructure(item, filePath, expectedType) {
   255‚Üí    const fileName = path.basename(filePath);
   256‚Üí
   257‚Üí    // Required fields for all items (except macros don't have 'system')
   258‚Üí    const baseRequiredFields = ['name', 'type'];
   259‚Üí    for (const field of baseRequiredFields) {
   260‚Üí      if (!item[field]) {
   261‚Üí        throw new Error(`Missing required field '${field}' in ${fileName}`);
   262‚Üí      }
   263‚Üí    }
   264‚Üí    
   265‚Üí    // Non-macro items require 'system' field
   266‚Üí    const expectedItemType = this.getExpectedItemType(expectedType);
   267‚Üí    if (expectedItemType !== 'script' && !item.system) {
   268‚Üí      throw new Error(`Missing required field 'system' in ${fileName}`);
   269‚Üí    }
   270‚Üí
   271‚Üí    // Validate type consistency  
   272‚Üí    if (item.type !== expectedItemType) {
   273‚Üí      throw new Error(`Type mismatch in ${fileName}: expected '${expectedItemType}', got '${item.type}'`);
   274‚Üí    }
   275‚Üí
   276‚Üí    // Type-specific validation
   277‚Üí    this.validateTypeSpecificFields(item, fileName, expectedType);
   278‚Üí  }
   279‚Üí
   280‚Üí  /**
   281‚Üí   * Get expected item type from directory name
   282‚Üí   * @param {string} dirName - Directory name (traits, talents, etc.)
   283‚Üí   * @returns {string} Expected item type
   284‚Üí   */
   285‚Üí  getExpectedItemType(dirName) {
   286‚Üí    const typeMap = {
   287‚Üí      'traits': 'trait',
   288‚Üí      'talents': 'talent',
   289‚Üí      'augments': 'augment',
   290‚Üí      'macros': 'script'
   291‚Üí    };
   292‚Üí    return typeMap[dirName] || dirName.slice(0, -1); // Remove 's' as fallback
   293‚Üí  }
   294‚Üí
   295‚Üí  /**
   296‚Üí   * Validate type-specific required fields
   297‚Üí   * @param {Object} item - Item data
   298‚Üí   * @param {string} fileName - File name for error reporting
   299‚Üí   * @param {string} compendiumType - Compendium type
   300‚Üí   */
   301‚Üí  validateTypeSpecificFields(item, fileName, compendiumType) {
   302‚Üí    switch (compendiumType) {
   303‚Üí      case 'traits':
   304‚Üí        this.validateTraitFields(item, fileName);
   305‚Üí        break;
   306‚Üí      case 'talents':
   307‚Üí      case 'augments':
   308‚Üí        this.validateTalentAugmentFields(item, fileName);
   309‚Üí        break;
   310‚Üí      case 'macros':
   311‚Üí        this.validateMacroFields(item, fileName);
   312‚Üí        break;
   313‚Üí    }
   314‚Üí  }
   315‚Üí
   316‚Üí  /**
   317‚Üí   * Validate trait-specific fields
   318‚Üí   */
   319‚Üí  validateTraitFields(item, fileName) {
   320‚Üí    const required = ['color', 'icon', 'description'];
   321‚Üí    for (const field of required) {
   322‚Üí      if (!item.system[field]) {
   323‚Üí        throw new Error(`Missing required trait field 'system.${field}' in ${fileName}`);
   324‚Üí      }
   325‚Üí    }
   326‚Üí
   327‚Üí    // Validate color format (hex color)
   328‚Üí    if (!/^#[0-9A-Fa-f]{6}$/.test(item.system.color)) {
   329‚Üí      throw new Error(`Invalid color format in ${fileName}: expected hex color like #FF6B6B`);
   330‚Üí    }
   331‚Üí  }
   332‚Üí
   333‚Üí  /**
   334‚Üí   * Validate talent/augment-specific fields
   335‚Üí   */
   336‚Üí  validateTalentAugmentFields(item, fileName) {
   337‚Üí    const required = ['description'];
   338‚Üí    for (const field of required) {
   339‚Üí      if (!item.system[field]) {
   340‚Üí        throw new Error(`Missing required field 'system.${field}' in ${fileName}`);
   341‚Üí      }
   342‚Üí    }
   343‚Üí
   344‚Üí    // Validate traits array if present
   345‚Üí    if (item.system.traits && !Array.isArray(item.system.traits)) {
   346‚Üí      throw new Error(`Field 'system.traits' must be an array in ${fileName}`);
   347‚Üí    }
   348‚Üí  }
   349‚Üí
   350‚Üí  /**
   351‚Üí   * Validate macro-specific fields
   352‚Üí   */
   353‚Üí  validateMacroFields(item, fileName) {
   354‚Üí    if (!item.command) {
   355‚Üí      throw new Error(`Missing required field 'command' in ${fileName}`);
   356‚Üí    }
   357‚Üí  }
   358‚Üí
   359‚Üí  /**
   360‚Üí   * Get all items of a specific type
   361‚Üí   * @param {string} typeName - Type name (traits, talents, etc.)
   362‚Üí   * @returns {Array} Array of items
   363‚Üí   */
   364‚Üí  getItemsByType(typeName) {
   365‚Üí    return this.loadedData.get(typeName) || [];
   366‚Üí  }
   367‚Üí
   368‚Üí  /**
   369‚Üí   * Get folder metadata for a specific type (Phase C)
   370‚Üí   * @param {string} typeName - Type name (traits, talents, etc.)
   371‚Üí   * @returns {Array} Array of folder metadata
   372‚Üí   */
   373‚Üí  getFoldersByType(typeName) {
   374‚Üí    return this.folders.get(typeName) || [];
   375‚Üí  }
   376‚Üí
   377‚Üí  /**
   378‚Üí   * Get all loaded items as a flat array
   379‚Üí   * @returns {Array} All items
   380‚Üí   */
   381‚Üí  getAllItems() {
   382‚Üí    const allItems = [];
   383‚Üí    for (const items of this.loadedData.values()) {
   384‚Üí      allItems.push(...items);
   385‚Üí    }
   386‚Üí    return allItems;
   387‚Üí  }
   388‚Üí
   389‚Üí  /**
   390‚Üí   * Get loading statistics
   391‚Üí   * @returns {Object} Loading statistics
   392‚Üí   */
   393‚Üí  getStats() {
   394‚Üí    const stats = {
   395‚Üí      totalTypes: this.loadedData.size,
   396‚Üí      totalItems: 0,
   397‚Üí      totalFolders: 0, // Phase C: Include folder count
   398‚Üí      itemsByType: {},
   399‚Üí      foldersByType: {}, // Phase C: Include folder breakdown
   400‚Üí      errorCount: this.errors.length,
   401‚Üí      warningCount: this.warnings.length,
   402‚Üí      validationSummary: this.validationSummary
   403‚Üí    };
   404‚Üí
   405‚Üí    for (const [type, items] of this.loadedData.entries()) {
   406‚Üí      stats.itemsByType[type] = items.length;
   407‚Üí      stats.totalItems += items.length;
   408‚Üí    }
   409‚Üí
   410‚Üí    // Phase C: Add folder statistics
   411‚Üí    for (const [type, folders] of this.folders.entries()) {
   412‚Üí      stats.foldersByType[type] = folders.length;
   413‚Üí      stats.totalFolders += folders.length;
   414‚Üí    }
   415‚Üí
   416‚Üí    return stats;
   417‚Üí  }
   418‚Üí
   419‚Üí  /**
   420‚Üí   * Add a warning message
   421‚Üí   * @param {string} message - Warning message
   422‚Üí   */
   423‚Üí  addWarning(message) {
   424‚Üí    this.warnings.push(message);
   425‚Üí    this.validationSummary.warningFiles++;
   426‚Üí    console.warn(`‚ö†Ô∏è Warning: ${message}`);
   427‚Üí  }
   428‚Üí
   429‚Üí  /**
   430‚Üí   * Perform semantic validation on item data
   431‚Üí   * @param {Object} item - Item data
   432‚Üí   * @param {string} fileName - File name for error reporting
   433‚Üí   * @param {string} expectedType - Expected compendium type
   434‚Üí   */
   435‚Üí  performSemanticValidation(item, fileName, expectedType) {
   436‚Üí    // Check for reasonable field lengths
   437‚Üí    if (item.name && item.name.length > 100) {
   438‚Üí      this.addWarning(`Long name in ${fileName}: "${item.name.substring(0, 50)}..."`);
   439‚Üí    }
   440‚Üí
   441‚Üí    // Check for missing descriptions
   442‚Üí    if (expectedType !== 'macros' && item.system && !item.system.description) {
   443‚Üí      this.addWarning(`Missing description in ${fileName}`);
   444‚Üí    }
   445‚Üí
   446‚Üí    // Type-specific semantic validation
   447‚Üí    switch (expectedType) {
   448‚Üí      case 'traits':
   449‚Üí        this.validateTraitSemantics(item, fileName);
   450‚Üí        break;
   451‚Üí      case 'talents':
   452‚Üí      case 'augments':
   453‚Üí        this.validateTalentAugmentSemantics(item, fileName);
   454‚Üí        break;
   455‚Üí      case 'macros':
   456‚Üí        this.validateMacroSemantics(item, fileName);
   457‚Üí        break;
   458‚Üí    }
   459‚Üí  }
   460‚Üí
   461‚Üí  /**
   462‚Üí   * Validate trait semantic correctness
   463‚Üí   */
   464‚Üí  validateTraitSemantics(item, fileName) {
   465‚Üí    if (item.system.description && item.system.description.length < 10) {
   466‚Üí      this.addWarning(`Very short description in trait ${fileName}`);
   467‚Üí    }
   468‚Üí
   469‚Üí    // Check for common icon paths
   470‚Üí    if (item.system.icon && !item.system.icon.includes('/')) {
   471‚Üí      this.addWarning(`Icon path may be incomplete in ${fileName}: ${item.system.icon}`);
   472‚Üí    }
   473‚Üí  }
   474‚Üí
   475‚Üí  /**
   476‚Üí   * Validate talent/augment semantic correctness
   477‚Üí   */
   478‚Üí  validateTalentAugmentSemantics(item, fileName) {
   479‚Üí    if (item.system.description && item.system.description.length < 20) {
   480‚Üí      this.addWarning(`Very short description in ${fileName}`);
   481‚Üí    }
   482‚Üí
   483‚Üí    // Check traits array
   484‚Üí    if (item.system.traits && item.system.traits.length === 0) {
   485‚Üí      this.addWarning(`Empty traits array in ${fileName}`);
   486‚Üí    }
   487‚Üí
   488‚Üí    // Check for power point costs
   489‚Üí    if (item.system.powerPointCost && (item.system.powerPointCost < 0 || item.system.powerPointCost > 20)) {
   490‚Üí      this.addWarning(`Unusual power point cost in ${fileName}: ${item.system.powerPointCost}`);
   491‚Üí    }
   492‚Üí  }
   493‚Üí
   494‚Üí  /**
   495‚Üí   * Validate macro semantic correctness
   496‚Üí   */
   497‚Üí  validateMacroSemantics(item, fileName) {
   498‚Üí    if (item.command && item.command.length < 50) {
   499‚Üí      this.addWarning(`Very short macro command in ${fileName}`);
   500‚Üí    }
   501‚Üí
   502‚Üí    // Check for potential security issues (basic check)
   503‚Üí    if (item.command && item.command.includes('eval(')) {
   504‚Üí      this.addWarning(`Potential security concern: eval() found in ${fileName}`);
   505‚Üí    }
   506‚Üí
   507‚Üí    // Check scope
   508‚Üí    if (item.scope && !['global', 'actor', 'chat'].includes(item.scope)) {
   509‚Üí      this.addWarning(`Unusual scope in ${fileName}: ${item.scope}`);
   510‚Üí    }
   511‚Üí  }
   512‚Üí
   513‚Üí  /**
   514‚Üí   * Print a comprehensive validation summary
   515‚Üí   */
   516‚Üí  printValidationSummary() {
   517‚Üí    console.log('\nüìä Validation Summary:');
   518‚Üí    console.log(`   üìÅ Total Files: ${this.validationSummary.totalFiles}`);
   519‚Üí    console.log(`   ‚úÖ Successful: ${this.validationSummary.successfulFiles}`);
   520‚Üí    console.log(`   ‚ùå Errors: ${this.validationSummary.errorFiles}`);
   521‚Üí    console.log(`   ‚ö†Ô∏è  Warnings: ${this.validationSummary.warningFiles}`);
   522‚Üí    
   523‚Üí    const successRate = this.validationSummary.totalFiles > 0 
   524‚Üí      ? Math.round((this.validationSummary.successfulFiles / this.validationSummary.totalFiles) * 100)
   525‚Üí      : 0;
   526‚Üí    console.log(`   üìà Success Rate: ${successRate}%`);
   527‚Üí
   528‚Üí    // Print error details if any
   529‚Üí    if (this.errors.length > 0) {
   530‚Üí      console.log('\n‚ùå Error Details:');
   531‚Üí      this.errors.forEach((error, index) => {
   532‚Üí        console.log(`   ${index + 1}. ${error}`);
   533‚Üí      });
   534‚Üí    }
   535‚Üí
   536‚Üí    // Print warning details if any
   537‚Üí    if (this.warnings.length > 0) {
   538‚Üí      console.log('\n‚ö†Ô∏è Warning Details:');
   539‚Üí      this.warnings.forEach((warning, index) => {
   540‚Üí        console.log(`   ${index + 1}. ${warning}`);
   541‚Üí      });
   542‚Üí    }
   543‚Üí
   544‚Üí    console.log(''); // Empty line for spacing
   545‚Üí  }
   546‚Üí}
   547‚Üí
   548‚Üíexport default CompendiumLoader;
```

Result:

```
1‚Üí/**
     2‚Üí * @fileoverview Local Compendium Service - FoundryVTT Local Operations
     3‚Üí * @description Service for local compendium management, loading, diffing, and copying
     4‚Üí * @version 2.0.0
     5‚Üí * @author Avant Development Team
     6‚Üí */
     7‚Üí
     8‚Üíimport { diffPacks, DiffResult } from '../logic/compendium/diffPacks';
     9‚Üí
    10‚Üí/**
    11‚Üí * Document interface for compendium operations
    12‚Üí */
    13‚Üíexport interface CompendiumDocument {
    14‚Üí    /** Document name (used for matching) */
    15‚Üí    name: string;
    16‚Üí    /** Document ID (may be preserved during copy operations) */
    17‚Üí    _id?: string;
    18‚Üí    /** Any other document properties */
    19‚Üí    [key: string]: any;
    20‚Üí}
    21‚Üí
    22‚Üí/**
    23‚Üí * Options for document copying operations
    24‚Üí */
    25‚Üíexport interface CopyDocsOptions {
    26‚Üí    /** Filter function to select which documents to copy */
    27‚Üí    filter?: (doc: CompendiumDocument) => boolean;
    28‚Üí    /** Whether to preserve original document IDs when possible */
    29‚Üí    preserveIds?: boolean;
    30‚Üí}
    31‚Üí
    32‚Üí/**
    33‚Üí * Hook data emitted when documents are copied between packs
    34‚Üí */
    35‚Üíexport interface CompendiumCopiedHookData {
    36‚Üí    /** Source pack ID */
    37‚Üí    srcId: string;
    38‚Üí    /** Destination pack ID */
    39‚Üí    destId: string;
    40‚Üí    /** Number of documents successfully copied */
    41‚Üí    docsCopied: number;
    42‚Üí    /** Array of copied document names */
    43‚Üí    copiedNames: string[];
    44‚Üí}
    45‚Üí
    46‚Üí/**
    47‚Üí * Hook data emitted when packs are compared
    48‚Üí */
    49‚Üíexport interface CompendiumDiffedHookData {
    50‚Üí    /** Source pack ID */
    51‚Üí    srcId: string;
    52‚Üí    /** Destination pack ID */
    53‚Üí    destId: string;
    54‚Üí    /** Comparison results */
    55‚Üí    diff: DiffResult;
    56‚Üí    /** Total number of differences found */
    57‚Üí    totalDifferences: number;
    58‚Üí}
    59‚Üí
    60‚Üí/**
    61‚Üí * Service for local compendium pack operations
    62‚Üí * 
    63‚Üí * This service provides utilities for working with FoundryVTT compendium packs
    64‚Üí * stored locally. It handles loading documents, comparing pack contents, and
    65‚Üí * copying documents between packs using only local Foundry APIs.
    66‚Üí * 
    67‚Üí * @example
    68‚Üí * // Basic usage
    69‚Üí * const service = new CompendiumLocalService();
    70‚Üí * 
    71‚Üí * // Load all documents from a pack
    72‚Üí * const docs = await service.loadPack('world.my-weapons');
    73‚Üí * 
    74‚Üí * // Compare two packs
    75‚Üí * const diff = await service.diffLocalPacks('world.pack1', 'world.pack2');
    76‚Üí * 
    77‚Üí * // Copy all documents
    78‚Üí * await service.copyDocs('world.source', 'world.dest');
    79‚Üí * 
    80‚Üí * // Copy with filter
    81‚Üí * await service.copyDocs('world.weapons', 'world.magic-weapons', {
    82‚Üí *   filter: (doc) => doc.system?.magical === true
    83‚Üí * });
    84‚Üí */
    85‚Üíexport class CompendiumLocalService {
    86‚Üí    private initialized: boolean = false;
    87‚Üí
    88‚Üí    /**
    89‚Üí     * Initialize the service (called automatically on first use)
    90‚Üí     * 
    91‚Üí     * Ensures the FoundryVTT game is ready and compendium packs are available.
    92‚Üí     * This is called automatically by other methods, so manual initialization
    93‚Üí     * is not required.
    94‚Üí     * 
    95‚Üí     * @throws {Error} If FoundryVTT game or packs are not available
    96‚Üí     */
    97‚Üí    private ensureInitialized(): void {
    98‚Üí        if (this.initialized) return;
    99‚Üí
   100‚Üí        if (!(globalThis as any).game) {
   101‚Üí            throw new Error('FoundryVTT game not available - service requires active game session');
   102‚Üí        }
   103‚Üí
   104‚Üí        if (!(globalThis as any).game.packs) {
   105‚Üí            throw new Error('FoundryVTT compendium packs not available');
   106‚Üí        }
   107‚Üí
   108‚Üí        this.initialized = true;
   109‚Üí    }
   110‚Üí
   111‚Üí    /**
   112‚Üí     * Load all documents from a compendium pack
   113‚Üí     * 
   114‚Üí     * Retrieves all documents from the specified compendium pack. The pack
   115‚Üí     * must be available in the current game session. Returns an array of
   116‚Üí     * document objects that can be used for comparison or copying operations.
   117‚Üí     * 
   118‚Üí     * @param {string} packId - Full pack identifier (e.g., 'world.my-pack' or 'system.equipment')
   119‚Üí     * @returns {Promise<CompendiumDocument[]>} Array of documents from the pack
   120‚Üí     * 
   121‚Üí     * @throws {Error} If pack is not found or cannot be accessed
   122‚Üí     * 
   123‚Üí     * @example
   124‚Üí     * // Load world-level pack
   125‚Üí     * const worldDocs = await service.loadPack('world.custom-weapons');
   126‚Üí     * 
   127‚Üí     * // Load system pack
   128‚Üí     * const systemDocs = await service.loadPack('dnd5e.spells');
   129‚Üí     * 
   130‚Üí     * // Load module pack
   131‚Üí     * const moduleDocs = await service.loadPack('my-module.monsters');
   132‚Üí     */
   133‚Üí    async loadPack(packId: string): Promise<CompendiumDocument[]> {
   134‚Üí        const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();
   135‚Üí        
   136‚Üí        // PHASE 1 INSTRUMENTATION: Track pack access operations
   137‚Üí        console.debug(`üéØ COMPENDIUM | ${timestamp} | loadPack | ENTRY`, {
   138‚Üí            packId,
   139‚Üí            gameReady: !!(globalThis as any).game?.ready,
   140‚Üí            packsAvailable: !!(globalThis as any).game?.packs,
   141‚Üí            totalPackCount: (globalThis as any).game?.packs?.size || 0
   142‚Üí        });
   143‚Üí        
   144‚Üí        this.ensureInitialized();
   145‚Üí
   146‚Üí        if (!packId || typeof packId !== 'string') {
   147‚Üí            console.error(`üéØ COMPENDIUM | ${timestamp} | loadPack | Invalid pack ID: ${packId}`);
   148‚Üí            throw new Error(`Invalid pack ID: ${packId}. Must be a non-empty string.`);
   149‚Üí        }
   150‚Üí
   151‚Üí        // Get the pack from FoundryVTT
   152‚Üí        const pack = (globalThis as any).game.packs.get(packId);
   153‚Üí        if (!pack) {
   154‚Üí            const availablePacks = Array.from((globalThis as any).game.packs.keys());
   155‚Üí            console.error(`üéØ COMPENDIUM | ${timestamp} | loadPack | Pack not found`, {
   156‚Üí                requestedPack: packId,
   157‚Üí                availablePacks: availablePacks,
   158‚Üí                packCount: availablePacks.length
   159‚Üí            });
   160‚Üí            throw new Error(`Compendium pack '${packId}' not found. Available packs: ${availablePacks.join(', ')}`);
   161‚Üí        }
   162‚Üí
   163‚Üí        console.debug(`üéØ COMPENDIUM | ${timestamp} | loadPack | Pack found`, {
   164‚Üí            packId,
   165‚Üí            packName: pack.metadata?.name,
   166‚Üí            packLabel: pack.metadata?.label,
   167‚Üí            packType: pack.metadata?.type,
   168‚Üí            packSystem: pack.metadata?.system,
   169‚Üí            isLocked: pack.locked
   170‚Üí        });
   171‚Üí
   172‚Üí        try {
   173‚Üí            // Load all documents from the pack
   174‚Üí            const documents = await pack.getDocuments();
   175‚Üí            
   176‚Üí            console.debug(`üéØ COMPENDIUM | ${timestamp} | loadPack | Documents loaded`, {
   177‚Üí                packId,
   178‚Üí                documentCount: documents.length,
   179‚Üí                sampleDocuments: documents.slice(0, 3).map((doc: any) => ({
   180‚Üí                    id: doc.id,
   181‚Üí                    name: doc.name,
   182‚Üí                    type: doc.type
   183‚Üí                }))
   184‚Üí            });
   185‚Üí            
   186‚Üí            // Convert to plain objects for easier manipulation
   187‚Üí            const plainDocs: CompendiumDocument[] = documents.map((doc: any) => {
   188‚Üí                const data = doc.toObject();
   189‚Üí                return {
   190‚Üí                    name: data.name || `Unnamed-${data._id}`,
   191‚Üí                    ...data
   192‚Üí                } as CompendiumDocument;
   193‚Üí            });
   194‚Üí
   195‚Üí            console.debug(`üéØ COMPENDIUM | ${timestamp} | loadPack | COMPLETED`, {
   196‚Üí                packId,
   197‚Üí                finalDocumentCount: plainDocs.length,
   198‚Üí                processingTime: `${Date.now() - new Date(timestamp).getTime()}ms`
   199‚Üí            });
   200‚Üí
   201‚Üí            return plainDocs;
   202‚Üí        } catch (error) {
   203‚Üí            console.error(`üéØ COMPENDIUM | ${timestamp} | loadPack | Error loading documents`, {
   204‚Üí                packId,
   205‚Üí                error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
   206‚Üí                errorStack: error instanceof Error ? error.stack : undefined
   207‚Üí            });
   208‚Üí            throw new Error(`Failed to load documents from pack '${packId}': ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)}`);
   209‚Üí        }
   210‚Üí    }
   211‚Üí
   212‚Üí    /**
   213‚Üí     * Compare two local compendium packs and identify differences
   214‚Üí     * 
   215‚Üí     * Loads documents from both packs and performs a comprehensive comparison
   216‚Üí     * to identify which documents have been added, removed, or changed. The
   217‚Üí     * comparison uses normalized document content to ignore volatile fields.
   218‚Üí     * 
   219‚Üí     * @param {string} srcId - Source pack identifier to compare from
   220‚Üí     * @param {string} destId - Destination pack identifier to compare to
   221‚Üí     * @returns {Promise<DiffResult>} Comparison results with added, removed, and changed documents
   222‚Üí     * 
   223‚Üí     * @throws {Error} If either pack cannot be loaded
   224‚Üí     * 
   225‚Üí     * @example
   226‚Üí     * // Compare world pack with backup
   227‚Üí     * const diff = await service.diffLocalPacks('world.weapons', 'world.weapons-backup');
   228‚Üí     * 
   229‚Üí     * console.log(`Added: ${diff.added.length}`);
   230‚Üí     * console.log(`Removed: ${diff.removed.length}`);
   231‚Üí     * console.log(`Changed: ${diff.changed.length}`);
   232‚Üí     * 
   233‚Üí     * // Access specific changes
   234‚Üí     * diff.changed.forEach(change => {
   235‚Üí     *   console.log(`${change.local.name} differs from ${change.remote.name}`);
   236‚Üí     * });
   237‚Üí     */
   238‚Üí    async diffLocalPacks(srcId: string, destId: string): Promise<DiffResult> {
   239‚Üí        this.ensureInitialized();
   240‚Üí
   241‚Üí        if (!srcId || !destId) {
   242‚Üí            throw new Error('Both source and destination pack IDs are required');
   243‚Üí        }
   244‚Üí
   245‚Üí        if (srcId === destId) {
   246‚Üí            throw new Error('Source and destination pack IDs cannot be the same');
   247‚Üí        }
   248‚Üí
   249‚Üí        try {
   250‚Üí            // Load documents from both packs
   251‚Üí            const [srcDocs, destDocs] = await Promise.all([
   252‚Üí                this.loadPack(srcId),
   253‚Üí                this.loadPack(destId)
   254‚Üí            ]);
   255‚Üí
   256‚Üí            // Perform diff using pure function
   257‚Üí            const diff = diffPacks(srcDocs, destDocs);
   258‚Üí
   259‚Üí            // Emit hook for listeners
   260‚Üí            const totalDifferences = diff.added.length + diff.removed.length + diff.changed.length;
   261‚Üí            const hookData: CompendiumDiffedHookData = {
   262‚Üí                srcId,
   263‚Üí                destId,
   264‚Üí                diff,
   265‚Üí                totalDifferences
   266‚Üí            };
   267‚Üí
   268‚Üí            if ((globalThis as any).Hooks) {
   269‚Üí                (globalThis as any).Hooks.callAll('avantCompendiumDiffed', hookData);
   270‚Üí            }
   271‚Üí
   272‚Üí            return diff;
   273‚Üí        } catch (error) {
   274‚Üí            throw new Error(`Failed to compare packs '${srcId}' and '${destId}': ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)}`);
   275‚Üí        }
   276‚Üí    }
   277‚Üí
   278‚Üí    /**
   279‚Üí     * Copy documents from source pack to destination pack
   280‚Üí     * 
   281‚Üí     * Loads documents from the source pack and creates them in the destination
   282‚Üí     * pack. Supports filtering to copy only specific documents. Handles
   283‚Üí     * document creation, update conflicts, and ID preservation based on options.
   284‚Üí     * 
   285‚Üí     * @param {string} srcId - Source pack identifier to copy from
   286‚Üí     * @param {string} destId - Destination pack identifier to copy to
   287‚Üí     * @param {CopyDocsOptions} [options] - Optional filtering and copy behavior
   288‚Üí     * @returns {Promise<void>} Resolves when copy operation completes
   289‚Üí     * 
   290‚Üí     * @throws {Error} If source/destination packs cannot be accessed or documents cannot be copied
   291‚Üí     * 
   292‚Üí     * @example
   293‚Üí     * // Copy all documents
   294‚Üí     * await service.copyDocs('world.all-weapons', 'world.backup-weapons');
   295‚Üí     * 
   296‚Üí     * // Copy only magical items
   297‚Üí     * await service.copyDocs('world.equipment', 'world.magic-items', {
   298‚Üí     *   filter: (doc) => doc.system?.magical === true
   299‚Üí     * });
   300‚Üí     * 
   301‚Üí     * // Copy with ID preservation
   302‚Üí     * await service.copyDocs('world.source', 'world.dest', {
   303‚Üí     *   preserveIds: true,
   304‚Üí     *   filter: (doc) => doc.system?.rarity === 'legendary'
   305‚Üí     * });
   306‚Üí     */
   307‚Üí    async copyDocs(srcId: string, destId: string, options: CopyDocsOptions = {}): Promise<void> {
   308‚Üí        this.ensureInitialized();
   309‚Üí
   310‚Üí        if (!srcId || !destId) {
   311‚Üí            throw new Error('Both source and destination pack IDs are required');
   312‚Üí        }
   313‚Üí
   314‚Üí        if (srcId === destId) {
   315‚Üí            throw new Error('Cannot copy documents to the same pack');
   316‚Üí        }
   317‚Üí
   318‚Üí        const { filter, preserveIds = false } = options;
   319‚Üí
   320‚Üí        try {
   321‚Üí            // Load source documents
   322‚Üí            const srcDocs = await this.loadPack(srcId);
   323‚Üí            
   324‚Üí            // Apply filter if provided
   325‚Üí            const docsTooCopy = filter ? srcDocs.filter(filter) : srcDocs;
   326‚Üí            
   327‚Üí            if (docsTooCopy.length === 0) {
   328‚Üí                // No documents to copy - emit hook with zero count
   329‚Üí                const hookData: CompendiumCopiedHookData = {
   330‚Üí                    srcId,
   331‚Üí                    destId,
   332‚Üí                    docsCopied: 0,
   333‚Üí                    copiedNames: []
   334‚Üí                };
   335‚Üí
   336‚Üí                if ((globalThis as any).Hooks) {
   337‚Üí                    (globalThis as any).Hooks.callAll('avantCompendiumCopied', hookData);
   338‚Üí                }
   339‚Üí                return;
   340‚Üí            }
   341‚Üí
   342‚Üí            // Get destination pack
   343‚Üí            const destPack = (globalThis as any).game.packs.get(destId);
   344‚Üí            if (!destPack) {
   345‚Üí                throw new Error(`Destination pack '${destId}' not found`);
   346‚Üí            }
   347‚Üí
   348‚Üí            // Prepare documents for creation
   349‚Üí            const copiedNames: string[] = [];
   350‚Üí            const createData = docsTooCopy.map(doc => {
   351‚Üí                const data = { ...doc };
   352‚Üí                
   353‚Üí                // Handle ID preservation
   354‚Üí                if (!preserveIds) {
   355‚Üí                    delete data._id;
   356‚Üí                }
   357‚Üí                
   358‚Üí                // FoundryVTT v13 compatibility: ensure clean data structure
   359‚Üí                // Remove any fields that might cause issues with bulk operations
   360‚Üí                delete data._stats;
   361‚Üí                delete data.folder;
   362‚Üí                delete data.sort;
   363‚Üí                delete data.ownership;
   364‚Üí                
   365‚Üí                copiedNames.push(data.name);
   366‚Üí                return data;
   367‚Üí            });
   368‚Üí
   369‚Üí            // Batch create documents in destination pack with v13 compatibility
   370‚Üí            await destPack.documentClass.createDocuments(createData, { 
   371‚Üí                pack: destPack.collection,
   372‚Üí                keepId: preserveIds  // Explicit v13 option for ID handling
   373‚Üí            });
   374‚Üí
   375‚Üí            // Emit success hook
   376‚Üí            const hookData: CompendiumCopiedHookData = {
   377‚Üí                srcId,
   378‚Üí                destId,
   379‚Üí                docsCopied: createData.length,
   380‚Üí                copiedNames
   381‚Üí            };
   382‚Üí
   383‚Üí            if ((globalThis as any).Hooks) {
   384‚Üí                (globalThis as any).Hooks.callAll('avantCompendiumCopied', hookData);
   385‚Üí            }
   386‚Üí
   387‚Üí        } catch (error) {
   388‚Üí            throw new Error(`Failed to copy documents from '${srcId}' to '${destId}': ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)}`);
   389‚Üí        }
   390‚Üí    }
   391‚Üí
   392‚Üí    /**
   393‚Üí     * Get service initialization status
   394‚Üí     * 
   395‚Üí     * Returns whether the service has been initialized and is ready for use.
   396‚Üí     * Primarily useful for testing and debugging purposes.
   397‚Üí     * 
   398‚Üí     * @returns {boolean} True if service is initialized and ready
   399‚Üí     */
   400‚Üí    isInitialized(): boolean {
   401‚Üí        return this.initialized;
   402‚Üí    }
   403‚Üí
   404‚Üí    /**
   405‚Üí     * Reset service state (primarily for testing)
   406‚Üí     * 
   407‚Üí     * Resets the service to uninitialized state, forcing re-initialization
   408‚Üí     * on next use. This is primarily useful for testing scenarios where
   409‚Üí     * you need to simulate different initialization conditions.
   410‚Üí     */
   411‚Üí    reset(): void {
   412‚Üí        this.initialized = false;
   413‚Üí    }
   414‚Üí}

1‚Üí/**
     2‚Üí * @fileoverview Pack ID Parsing Logic - Pure Functions
     3‚Üí * @description Pure functions for parsing FoundryVTT compendium pack identifiers
     4‚Üí * @version 2.0.0
     5‚Üí * @author Avant Development Team
     6‚Üí */
     7‚Üí
     8‚Üí/**
     9‚Üí * Splits a full pack ID into package and name components
    10‚Üí * 
    11‚Üí * This function takes a compendium pack identifier in the format "package.name"
    12‚Üí * and splits it into its constituent parts. This is used throughout the compendium
    13‚Üí * system to separate the system/module identifier from the pack name.
    14‚Üí * 
    15‚Üí * @param {string} fullId - The full pack ID to split (e.g., "avant.weapons")
    16‚Üí * @returns {{package: string, name: string}} The split pack components
    17‚Üí * @throws {Error} If the pack ID format is invalid
    18‚Üí * 
    19‚Üí * @example
    20‚Üí * // Standard system pack
    21‚Üí * const result = splitPackId("avant.weapons");
    22‚Üí * // Result: { package: "avant", name: "weapons" }
    23‚Üí * 
    24‚Üí * // Module pack
    25‚Üí * const moduleResult = splitPackId("my-module.spells");
    26‚Üí * // Result: { package: "my-module", name: "spells" }
    27‚Üí * 
    28‚Üí * // Invalid format throws error
    29‚Üí * try {
    30‚Üí *   splitPackId("invalid-format");
    31‚Üí * } catch (error) {
    32‚Üí *   // Error: Invalid pack ID format: must be 'package.name'
    33‚Üí * }
    34‚Üí */
    35‚Üíexport function splitPackId(fullId: string): { package: string; name: string } {
    36‚Üí    // Validate input type
    37‚Üí    if (typeof fullId !== 'string') {
    38‚Üí        throw new Error(`Invalid pack ID format: must be 'package.name', got ${typeof fullId}`);
    39‚Üí    }
    40‚Üí    
    41‚Üí    // Validate non-empty string
    42‚Üí    if (fullId.trim() === '') {
    43‚Üí        throw new Error(`Invalid pack ID format: must be 'package.name', got empty string`);
    44‚Üí    }
    45‚Üí    
    46‚Üí    // Split on the dot separator
    47‚Üí    const parts = fullId.split('.');
    48‚Üí    
    49‚Üí    // Must have exactly two parts
    50‚Üí    if (parts.length !== 2) {
    51‚Üí        throw new Error(`Invalid pack ID format: must be 'package.name', got '${fullId}'`);
    52‚Üí    }
    53‚Üí    
    54‚Üí    const [packagePart, namePart] = parts;
    55‚Üí    
    56‚Üí    // Both parts must be non-empty after trimming
    57‚Üí    if (packagePart.trim() === '' || namePart.trim() === '') {
    58‚Üí        throw new Error(`Invalid pack ID format: package and name must be non-empty, got '${fullId}'`);
    59‚Üí    }
    60‚Üí    
    61‚Üí    return {
    62‚Üí        package: packagePart.trim(),
    63‚Üí        name: namePart.trim()
    64‚Üí    };
    65‚Üí}

1‚Üí/**
     2‚Üí * @fileoverview Pack Comparison Logic - Pure Functions
     3‚Üí * @description Pure functions for comparing and diffing document collections
     4‚Üí * @version 2.0.0
     5‚Üí * @author Avant Development Team
     6‚Üí */
     7‚Üí
     8‚Üíimport { sha1Sync } from './sha1';
     9‚Üí
    10‚Üí/**
    11‚Üí * Result of comparing two document collections
    12‚Üí */
    13‚Üíexport interface DiffResult {
    14‚Üí    /** Documents present only in remoteDocs */
    15‚Üí    added: any[];
    16‚Üí    /** Documents present only in localDocs */
    17‚Üí    removed: any[];
    18‚Üí    /** Documents with same name but different content */
    19‚Üí    changed: Array<{ local: any; remote: any }>;
    20‚Üí}
    21‚Üí
    22‚Üí/**
    23‚Üí * Compares two document arrays and identifies differences
    24‚Üí * 
    25‚Üí * This function performs a comprehensive comparison between local and remote
    26‚Üí * document collections, identifying which documents have been added, removed,
    27‚Üí * or changed. Documents are matched by their 'name' field (case-insensitive)
    28‚Üí * and compared using SHA-1 hashes of their normalised content.
    29‚Üí * 
    30‚Üí * @param {any[]} localDocs - The local document collection
    31‚Üí * @param {any[]} remoteDocs - The remote document collection to compare against
    32‚Üí * @returns {DiffResult} Object containing added, removed, and changed documents
    33‚Üí * 
    34‚Üí * @example
    35‚Üí * // Basic pack comparison
    36‚Üí * const localDocs = [
    37‚Üí *   { name: "Sword", damage: "1d8", _id: "local1" },
    38‚Üí *   { name: "Shield", defense: 2, _id: "local2" }
    39‚Üí * ];
    40‚Üí * 
    41‚Üí * const remoteDocs = [
    42‚Üí *   { name: "Sword", damage: "1d10", _id: "remote1" }, // Changed
    43‚Üí *   { name: "Bow", damage: "1d6", _id: "remote2" }     // Added
    44‚Üí * ];
    45‚Üí * 
    46‚Üí * const diff = diffPacks(localDocs, remoteDocs);
    47‚Üí * // Result: {
    48‚Üí * //   added: [{ name: "Bow", damage: "1d6" }],
    49‚Üí * //   removed: [{ name: "Shield", defense: 2 }],
    50‚Üí * //   changed: [{
    51‚Üí * //     local: { name: "Sword", damage: "1d8" },
    52‚Üí * //     remote: { name: "Sword", damage: "1d10" }
    53‚Üí * //   }]
    54‚Üí * // }
    55‚Üí * 
    56‚Üí * // Case-insensitive name matching
    57‚Üí * const local = [{ name: "SWORD", damage: "1d8" }];
    58‚Üí * const remote = [{ name: "sword", damage: "1d8" }];
    59‚Üí * const result = diffPacks(local, remote);
    60‚Üí * // Result: { added: [], removed: [], changed: [] }
    61‚Üí * // (No differences - same content, case-insensitive match)
    62‚Üí */
    63‚Üíexport function diffPacks(localDocs: any[], remoteDocs: any[]): DiffResult {
    64‚Üí    // Validate inputs
    65‚Üí    if (!Array.isArray(localDocs)) {
    66‚Üí        throw new Error('localDocs must be an array');
    67‚Üí    }
    68‚Üí    if (!Array.isArray(remoteDocs)) {
    69‚Üí        throw new Error('remoteDocs must be an array');
    70‚Üí    }
    71‚Üí    
    72‚Üí    // Create maps for efficient lookup by normalised name
    73‚Üí    const localMap = new Map<string, any>();
    74‚Üí    const remoteMap = new Map<string, any>();
    75‚Üí    
    76‚Üí    // Populate local map
    77‚Üí    for (const doc of localDocs) {
    78‚Üí        if (doc && typeof doc === 'object' && doc.name) {
    79‚Üí            const normalisedName = doc.name.toString().toLowerCase().trim();
    80‚Üí            if (normalisedName) {
    81‚Üí                localMap.set(normalisedName, doc);
    82‚Üí            }
    83‚Üí        }
    84‚Üí    }
    85‚Üí    
    86‚Üí    // Populate remote map
    87‚Üí    for (const doc of remoteDocs) {
    88‚Üí        if (doc && typeof doc === 'object' && doc.name) {
    89‚Üí            const normalisedName = doc.name.toString().toLowerCase().trim();
    90‚Üí            if (normalisedName) {
    91‚Üí                remoteMap.set(normalisedName, doc);
    92‚Üí            }
    93‚Üí        }
    94‚Üí    }
    95‚Üí    
    96‚Üí    const added: any[] = [];
    97‚Üí    const removed: any[] = [];
    98‚Üí    const changed: Array<{ local: any; remote: any }> = [];
    99‚Üí    
   100‚Üí    // Find added and changed documents
   101‚Üí    for (const [normalisedName, remoteDoc] of remoteMap) {
   102‚Üí        const localDoc = localMap.get(normalisedName);
   103‚Üí        
   104‚Üí        if (!localDoc) {
   105‚Üí            // Document exists in remote but not local - it's added
   106‚Üí            added.push(remoteDoc);
   107‚Üí        } else {
   108‚Üí            // Document exists in both - check if content differs
   109‚Üí            const localHash = sha1Sync(localDoc);
   110‚Üí            const remoteHash = sha1Sync(remoteDoc);
   111‚Üí            
   112‚Üí            if (localHash !== remoteHash) {
   113‚Üí                // Content differs - it's changed
   114‚Üí                changed.push({
   115‚Üí                    local: localDoc,
   116‚Üí                    remote: remoteDoc
   117‚Üí                });
   118‚Üí            }
   119‚Üí        }
   120‚Üí    }
   121‚Üí    
   122‚Üí    // Find removed documents
   123‚Üí    for (const [normalisedName, localDoc] of localMap) {
   124‚Üí        if (!remoteMap.has(normalisedName)) {
   125‚Üí            // Document exists in local but not remote - it's removed
   126‚Üí            removed.push(localDoc);
   127‚Üí        }
   128‚Üí    }
   129‚Üí    
   130‚Üí    return {
   131‚Üí        added,
   132‚Üí        removed,
   133‚Üí        changed
   134‚Üí    };
   135‚Üí}
```

```
1‚Üí/**
     2‚Üí * @fileoverview SHA-1 Hashing Logic - Pure Functions
     3‚Üí * @description Pure functions for generating stable SHA-1 hashes of objects
     4‚Üí * @version 2.0.0
     5‚Üí * @author Avant Development Team
     6‚Üí */
     7‚Üí
     8‚Üíimport { normaliseDoc } from './normaliseDoc';
     9‚Üí
    10‚Üí/**
    11‚Üí * Generates a SHA-1 hash of an object for change detection
    12‚Üí * 
    13‚Üí * This function creates a stable SHA-1 hash of any object by first normalising
    14‚Üí * it (removing volatile fields and sorting keys) and then converting to JSON
    15‚Üí * for hashing. The hash is returned as a lowercase hexadecimal string.
    16‚Üí * This is used to detect changes between versions of the same document.
    17‚Üí * 
    18‚Üí * @param {any} obj - The object to hash
    19‚Üí * @returns {string} A lowercase hexadecimal SHA-1 hash
    20‚Üí * 
    21‚Üí * @example
    22‚Üí * // Simple object hashing
    23‚Üí * const weapon = {
    24‚Üí *   name: "Sword",
    25‚Üí *   damage: "1d8",
    26‚Üí *   _id: "will-be-removed"
    27‚Üí * };
    28‚Üí * 
    29‚Üí * const hash1 = sha1(weapon);
    30‚Üí * // Result: "a1b2c3d4e5f6789012345678901234567890abcd"
    31‚Üí * 
    32‚Üí * // Same content produces same hash (volatile fields ignored)
    33‚Üí * const weapon2 = {
    34‚Üí *   damage: "1d8",
    35‚Üí *   name: "Sword",
    36‚Üí *   _id: "different-id"
    37‚Üí * };
    38‚Üí * const hash2 = sha1(weapon2);
    39‚Üí * // hash1 === hash2 (true - content is identical)
    40‚Üí * 
    41‚Üí * // Different content produces different hash
    42‚Üí * const weapon3 = { ...weapon, damage: "1d10" };
    43‚Üí * const hash3 = sha1(weapon3);
    44‚Üí * // hash1 !== hash3 (true - content differs)
    45‚Üí */
    46‚Üíexport async function sha1(obj: any): Promise<string> {
    47‚Üí    // Normalise the object first to ensure stable hashing
    48‚Üí    const normalised = normaliseDoc(obj);
    49‚Üí    
    50‚Üí    // Convert to stable JSON string
    51‚Üí    const jsonString = JSON.stringify(normalised);
    52‚Üí    
    53‚Üí    try {
    54‚Üí        // Check if crypto is available
    55‚Üí        const crypto = (globalThis as any).crypto;
    56‚Üí        if (!crypto || !crypto.subtle || !crypto.subtle.digest) {
    57‚Üí            // Fallback to sync version if crypto is not available (e.g., in tests)
    58‚Üí            return sha1Sync(obj);
    59‚Üí        }
    60‚Üí        
    61‚Üí        // Convert string to bytes for hashing
    62‚Üí        const encoder = new TextEncoder();
    63‚Üí        const data = encoder.encode(jsonString);
    64‚Üí        
    65‚Üí        // Generate SHA-1 hash using Web Crypto API
    66‚Üí        const hashBuffer = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-1', data);
    67‚Üí        
    68‚Üí        // Convert hash to lowercase hex string
    69‚Üí        const hashArray = Array.from(new Uint8Array(hashBuffer));
    70‚Üí        const hashHex = hashArray
    71‚Üí            .map(byte => byte.toString(16).padStart(2, '0'))
    72‚Üí            .join('');
    73‚Üí        
    74‚Üí        return hashHex;
    75‚Üí    } catch (error) {
    76‚Üí        // If crypto fails for any reason, fallback to sync version
    77‚Üí        return sha1Sync(obj);
    78‚Üí    }
    79‚Üí}
    80‚Üí
    81‚Üí/**
    82‚Üí * Synchronous version of sha1 for environments where async is not suitable
    83‚Üí * 
    84‚Üí * This is a fallback implementation that uses a simple hash algorithm
    85‚Üí * when the Web Crypto API is not available or when synchronous operation
    86‚Üí * is required. Less secure than true SHA-1 but provides consistent hashing.
    87‚Üí * 
    88‚Üí * @param {any} obj - The object to hash
    89‚Üí * @returns {string} A lowercase hexadecimal hash string
    90‚Üí * 
    91‚Üí * @example
    92‚Üí * // When you need synchronous hashing
    93‚Üí * const weapon = { name: "Sword", damage: "1d8" };
    94‚Üí * const hash = sha1Sync(weapon);
    95‚Üí * // Result: consistent hash string for the same input
    96‚Üí */
    97‚Üíexport function sha1Sync(obj: any): string {
    98‚Üí    // Normalise the object first
    99‚Üí    const normalised = normaliseDoc(obj);
   100‚Üí    
   101‚Üí    // Convert to stable JSON string
   102‚Üí    const jsonString = JSON.stringify(normalised);
   103‚Üí    
   104‚Üí    // Handle null/undefined/empty cases
   105‚Üí    if (!jsonString || jsonString === 'null' || jsonString === 'undefined') {
   106‚Üí        return '00000000';
   107‚Üí    }
   108‚Üí    
   109‚Üí    // Simple hash algorithm (not cryptographically secure, but consistent)
   110‚Üí    let hash = 0;
   111‚Üí    for (let i = 0; i < jsonString.length; i++) {
   112‚Üí        const char = jsonString.charCodeAt(i);
   113‚Üí        hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + char;
   114‚Üí        hash = hash & hash; // Convert to 32-bit integer
   115‚Üí    }
   116‚Üí    
   117‚Üí    // Convert to positive number and then to hex
   118‚Üí    const positiveHash = Math.abs(hash);
   119‚Üí    return positiveHash.toString(16).padStart(8, '0');
   120‚Üí}
```

```
1‚Üí/**
     2‚Üí * @fileoverview Document Normalisation Logic - Pure Functions
     3‚Üí * @description Pure functions for normalising FoundryVTT documents for stable comparison
     4‚Üí * @version 2.0.0
     5‚Üí * @author Avant Development Team
     6‚Üí */
     7‚Üí
     8‚Üí/**
     9‚Üí * Normalises a document by removing volatile fields and sorting keys
    10‚Üí * 
    11‚Üí * This function creates a stable, canonical representation of a document
    12‚Üí * by removing properties that change frequently (like IDs, stats, folder info)
    13‚Üí * and sorting all remaining keys lexicographically. This ensures consistent
    14‚Üí * hashing and comparison between documents with the same content.
    15‚Üí * 
    16‚Üí * @param {any} doc - The document object to normalise
    17‚Üí * @returns {any} A normalised copy with volatile fields removed and keys sorted
    18‚Üí * 
    19‚Üí * @example
    20‚Üí * // FoundryVTT document with volatile fields
    21‚Üí * const rawDoc = {
    22‚Üí *   name: "Sword",
    23‚Üí *   _id: "abc123def456",
    24‚Üí *   _stats: { coreVersion: "12.331" },
    25‚Üí *   folder: "weapons-folder",
    26‚Üí *   sort: 100000,
    27‚Üí *   system: { damage: "1d8", type: "weapon" }
    28‚Üí * };
    29‚Üí * 
    30‚Üí * const normalised = normaliseDoc(rawDoc);
    31‚Üí * // Result: {
    32‚Üí * //   name: "Sword",
    33‚Üí * //   system: { damage: "1d8", type: "weapon" }
    34‚Üí * // }
    35‚Üí * // Keys are guaranteed to be in lexicographic order
    36‚Üí * 
    37‚Üí * // Handles nested objects recursively
    38‚Üí * const complexDoc = {
    39‚Üí *   name: "Spell",
    40‚Üí *   _id: "volatile",
    41‚Üí *   data: { cost: 5, _stats: "remove" }
    42‚Üí * };
    43‚Üí * const result = normaliseDoc(complexDoc);
    44‚Üí * // Result: { data: { cost: 5 }, name: "Spell" }
    45‚Üí */
    46‚Üíexport function normaliseDoc(doc: any, visited: WeakSet<object> = new WeakSet()): any {
    47‚Üí    // Handle null/undefined
    48‚Üí    if (doc === null || doc === undefined) {
    49‚Üí        return doc;
    50‚Üí    }
    51‚Üí    
    52‚Üí    // Handle primitive types (string, number, boolean)
    53‚Üí    if (typeof doc !== 'object') {
    54‚Üí        return doc;
    55‚Üí    }
    56‚Üí    
    57‚Üí    // Handle circular references
    58‚Üí    if (visited.has(doc)) {
    59‚Üí        return {}; // Return empty object for circular references
    60‚Üí    }
    61‚Üí    
    62‚Üí    // Mark this object as visited
    63‚Üí    visited.add(doc);
    64‚Üí    
    65‚Üí    // Handle arrays
    66‚Üí    if (Array.isArray(doc)) {
    67‚Üí        const result = doc.map(item => normaliseDoc(item, visited));
    68‚Üí        visited.delete(doc);
    69‚Üí        return result;
    70‚Üí    }
    71‚Üí    
    72‚Üí    // Handle objects - create deep copy and remove volatile fields
    73‚Üí    const normalised: Record<string, any> = {};
    74‚Üí    const volatileFields = new Set(['_id', '_stats', 'folder', 'sort']);
    75‚Üí    
    76‚Üí    // Process all properties, filtering out volatile ones
    77‚Üí    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(doc)) {
    78‚Üí        if (!volatileFields.has(key)) {
    79‚Üí            normalised[key] = normaliseDoc(value, visited);
    80‚Üí        }
    81‚Üí    }
    82‚Üí    
    83‚Üí    // Sort keys lexicographically for stable ordering
    84‚Üí    const sortedKeys = Object.keys(normalised).sort();
    85‚Üí    const sortedDoc: Record<string, any> = {};
    86‚Üí    
    87‚Üí    for (const key of sortedKeys) {
    88‚Üí        sortedDoc[key] = normalised[key];
    89‚Üí    }
    90‚Üí    
    91‚Üí    // Remove from visited set before returning
    92‚Üí    visited.delete(doc);
    93‚Üí    
    94‚Üí    return sortedDoc;
    95‚Üí}
```

# Comprehensive Analysis of Compendium-Related Code

## Overview
The codebase has an extensive compendium system with multiple layers of functionality ranging from build-time processing to runtime services. I've analyzed 14 core files and identified several areas for improvement.

## Key Findings

### 1. **Duplicate Functionality**

**Issue**: Multiple JavaScript wrappers for TypeScript implementations
- **Files**: `/Users/njisaf/code/avantVtt/scripts/compendium/link-rewriter.js` (lines 1-58)
- **Files**: `/Users/njisaf/code/avantVtt/scripts/compendium/round-trip-extractor.js` (lines 1-78)

**Recommendation**: Remove these wrapper files and use TypeScript files directly in the build process.

### 2. **Unused/Redundant Code**

**Issue**: Hardcoded seed data in build-packs.js that's no longer needed
- **File**: `/Users/njisaf/code/avantVtt/scripts/build-packs.js`
- **Lines**: 572-701 (TRAIT_SEEDS), 703-743 (TALENT_SEEDS), 745-788 (AUGMENT_SEEDS)
- **Lines**: 26-570 (MACRO_SEEDS with embedded full macro implementations)

**Recommendation**: Remove hardcoded seeds since the system now uses JSON files loaded via `loadCompendiumDataWithFallback()`.

### 3. **Over-Engineering in Build System**

**Issue**: Complex multi-phase pipeline that may be overkill
- **Files**: All files in `/Users/njisaf/code/avantVtt/scripts/compendium/` implement a multi-phase pipeline (A-E)
- **Complexity**: 5 separate classes (CompendiumValidator, PackSplitter, FolderValidator, LinkRewriter, RoundTripExtractor)

**Recommendation**: Consolidate into a single CompendiumBuilder class with focused responsibilities.

### 4. **Missing Error Handling**

**Issue**: Inconsistent error handling across components
- **File**: `/Users/njisaf/code/avantVtt/scripts/compendium/link-rewriter.ts`
- **Lines**: 167-171 (basic try-catch without proper error propagation)
- **File**: `/Users/njisaf/code/avantVtt/scripts/compendium/round-trip-extractor.ts`
- **Lines**: 354-358 (generic error handling)

**Recommendation**: Implement consistent error handling with proper error types and recovery strategies.

### 5. **Inefficient Data Processing**

**Issue**: Multiple file reads and processing passes
- **File**: `/Users/njisaf/code/avantVtt/scripts/data/compendium-loader.js`
- **Lines**: 116-173 (loads folder metadata separately from items)
- **File**: `/Users/njisaf/code/avantVtt/scripts/compendium/link-rewriter.ts`
- **Lines**: 114-163 (separate loading phase)

**Recommendation**: Combine data loading operations into a single pass with caching.

### 6. **Poor Code Organization**

**Issue**: Scattered compendium logic across multiple directories
- **Directories**: `/scripts/compendium/`, `/scripts/data/`, `/scripts/services/`, `/scripts/logic/compendium/`
- **Problem**: Related functionality is spread across 4 different directories

**Recommendation**: Consolidate all compendium logic into a single `/scripts/compendium/` directory.

## Specific Improvements

### 1. **Remove Duplicate Files**
```bash
# These files can be deleted:
rm scripts/compendium/link-rewriter.js
rm scripts/compendium/round-trip-extractor.js
```

### 2. **Simplify Build System**
**File**: `/Users/njisaf/code/avantVtt/scripts/build-packs.js`
- **Lines to remove**: 26-788 (all hardcoded seed data)
- **Lines to simplify**: 1036-1144 (overly complex build process)

### 3. **Consolidate Validation Logic**
**Current**: 3 separate validator classes
- CompendiumValidator (430 lines)
- PackSplitter (264 lines)  
- FolderValidator (371 lines)

**Recommendation**: Merge into single ValidationService with focused methods.

### 4. **Optimize Data Loading**
**File**: `/Users/njisaf/code/avantVtt/scripts/data/compendium-loader.js`
- **Lines 116-202**: Separate folder loading is inefficient
- **Lines 210-246**: File reading happens multiple times

**Improved approach**:
```typescript
class CompendiumLoader {
  async loadCompendiumType(typeName: string) {
    // Load everything in one pass
    const [items, folders] = await Promise.all([
      this.loadItems(typeDir),
      this.loadFolders(typeDir)
    ]);
    return { items, folders };
  }
}
```

- **Lines 307-390**: Complex document copying logic can be streamlined

**File**: `/Users/njisaf/code/avantVtt/scripts/logic/compendium/normaliseDoc.ts`
- **Lines 46-95**: Over-engineered normalisation with circular reference handling that's likely unnecessary for compendium documents

## Documentation Issues

- Complex pipeline processes lack architectural documentation

## Performance Improvements

- **Current**: Multiple passes through directory structures
- **Improvement**: Single directory traversal with parallel processing

### 2. **Optimize Hash Generation**
- **File**: `/Users/njisaf/code/avantVtt/scripts/logic/compendium/sha1.ts`
- **Issue**: Falls back to sync version frequently
- **Improvement**: Use faster hash algorithms for build-time operations

### 3. **Cache Loaded Data**
- **File**: `/Users/njisaf/code/avantVtt/scripts/data/compendium-integration.js`
- **Lines 103-152**: Reloads data on every call
- **Improvement**: Add caching layer for build-time operations
